March 19, 2026

ProbeFlow: Training-Free Adaptive Flow Matching for Vision-Language-Action Models

Abstract (English): Recent Vision-Language-Action (VLA) models equipped with Flow Matching (FM) action heads achieve state-of-the-art performance in complex robot manipulation. However, the multi-step iterative ODE solving required by FM introduces inference latency that precludes responsive physical control. While current acceleration efforts optimize the Vision-Language Model (VLM) backbone, the action head bottleneck remains overlooked. To address this, we propose ProbeFlow, a training-free adaptive inference framework tai- lored for continuous robotic control. By evaluating geometric trajectory complexity via the cosine similarity between initial and lookahead velocity vectors, ProbeFlow dynamically sched- ules integration steps to prune redundant network evaluations. On the MetaWorld benchmark, it accelerates action decoding by 14.8x (reducing average steps from N = 50 to 2.6) and cuts end-to-end system latency by 2.8x without compromising the manipulation success rate. On the long-horizon LIBERO benchmark, the probe automatically allocates a denser schedule to navigate semantic bottlenecks, effectively resolving the flow solver delay. Real-world physical deployments confirm that ProbeFlow successfully mitigates action decoding latency while ensuring execution stability, offering a highly practical solution for low-latency continuous generative policies.

摘要（中文）: 配备流匹配(FM)动作头的近期视觉-语言-动作(VLA)模型在复杂机器人操作中取得了最先进的性能。然而，FM所需的多步迭代ODE求解引入了推理延迟，从而阻碍了响应式物理控制。 虽然目前的加速工作优化了视觉-语言模型(VLM)骨干网络，但动作头瓶颈仍然被忽视。为了解决这个问题，我们提出ProbeFlow，一种为连续机器人控制量身定制的免训练自适应推理框架。通过评估初始速度向量和前瞻速度向量之间的余弦相似度来计算几何轨迹复杂度，ProbeFlow动态地调度积分步数，以剪除冗余的网络评估。在MetaWorld基准测试中，它将动作解码加速了14.8倍（将平均步数从N = 50减少到2.6），并将端到端系统延迟降低了2.8倍，而没有影响操作成功率。在长程LIBERO基准测试中，探针自动分配更密集的调度以导航语义瓶颈，从而有效解决了流求解器延迟。真实物理部署证实，ProbeFlow成功缓解了动作解码延迟，同时确保了执行稳定性，为低延迟连续生成策略提供了一种非常实用的解决方案。

TLDR: The paper introduces ProbeFlow, a training-free adaptive inference framework for Vision-Language-Action models which significantly reduces inference latency using dynamic integration step scheduling based on trajectory complexity, without compromising manipulation success.

简要说明: 本文介绍了一种名为ProbeFlow的免训练自适应推理框架，专为视觉-语言-动作模型设计。它通过基于轨迹复杂性的动态积分步长调度，显著降低了推理延迟，同时不影响操纵成功率。

Authors: Zhou Fang, Jiaqi Wang, Yi Zhou, Qiongfeng Shi

AgentVLN: Towards Agentic Vision-and-Language Navigation

Abstract (English): Vision-and-Language Navigation (VLN) requires an embodied agent to ground complex natural-language instructions into long-horizon navigation in unseen environments. While Vision-Language Models (VLMs) offer strong 2D semantic understanding, current VLN systems remain constrained by limited spatial perception, 2D-3D representation mismatch, and monocular scale ambiguity. In this paper, we propose AgentVLN, a novel and efficient embodied navigation framework that can be deployed on edge computing platforms. We formulate VLN as a Partially Observable Semi-Markov Decision Process (POSMDP) and introduce a VLM-as-Brain paradigm that decouples high-level semantic reasoning from perception and planning via a plug-and-play skill library. To resolve multi-level representation inconsistency, we design a cross-space representation mapping that projects perception-layer 3D topological waypoints into the image plane, yielding pixel-aligned visual prompts for the VLM. Building on this bridge, we integrate a context-aware self-correction and active exploration strategy to recover from occlusions and suppress error accumulation over long trajectories. To further address the spatial ambiguity of instructions in unstructured environments, we propose a Query-Driven Perceptual Chain-of-Thought (QD-PCoT) scheme, enabling the agent with the metacognitive ability to actively seek geometric depth information. Finally, we construct AgentVLN-Instruct, a large-scale instruction-tuning dataset with dynamic stage routing conditioned on target visibility. Extensive experiments show that AgentVLN consistently outperforms prior state-of-the-art methods (SOTA) on long-horizon VLN benchmarks, offering a practical paradigm for lightweight deployment of next-generation embodied navigation models. Code: https://github.com/Allenxinn/AgentVLN.

摘要（中文）: 视觉与语言导航（VLN）要求具身智能体将复杂的自然语言指令转化为在未见环境中的长程导航。虽然视觉-语言模型（VLMs）提供了强大的二维语义理解能力，但当前的VLN系统仍然受到有限的空间感知、二维-三维表示不匹配以及单目尺度模糊的限制。在本文中，我们提出了AgentVLN，一种新颖且高效的具身导航框架，可以部署在边缘计算平台上。我们将VLN建模为部分可观测半马尔可夫决策过程（POSMDP），并引入一种“VLM即大脑”的范式，通过一个即插即用的技能库将高层语义推理与感知和规划解耦。为了解决多层表示不一致性问题，我们设计了一种跨空间表示映射，将感知层的三维拓扑路标点投影到图像平面上，从而为VLM生成像素对齐的视觉提示。在此基础上，我们集成了一种上下文感知的自我纠正和主动探索策略，以从遮挡中恢复并抑制长 trajectory 中的误差累积。为了进一步解决非结构化环境中指令的空间模糊性，我们提出了一种查询驱动的感知链式思维（QD-PCoT）方案，使智能体具备主动寻求几何深度信息的元认知能力。最后，我们构建了AgentVLN-Instruct，一个基于目标可见性动态路由的大规模指令调优数据集。大量实验表明，AgentVLN在长程VLN基准测试中始终优于先前最先进的方法（SOTA），为下一代具身导航模型的轻量级部署提供了一种实用的范式。代码：https://github.com/Allenxinn/AgentVLN。

TLDR: The paper introduces AgentVLN, a novel VLN framework leveraging VLM as a "brain" with cross-space representation mapping and active exploration strategies. It significantly outperforms existing methods on long-horizon VLN benchmarks and offers a practical paradigm for lightweight deployment.

简要说明: 本文介绍了AgentVLN，一种新型VLN框架，利用VLM作为“大脑”，采用跨空间表示映射和主动探索策略。它在长程VLN基准测试中明显优于现有方法，并为下一代具身导航模型的轻量级部署提供了一种实用的范例。

Authors: Zihao Xin, Wentong Li, Yixuan Jiang, Ziyuan Huang, Bin Wang, Piji Li, Jianke Zhu, Jie Qin, Shengjun Huang

Action Draft and Verify: A Self-Verifying Framework for Vision-Language-Action Model

Abstract (English): Vision-Language-Action (VLA) models have recently demonstrated strong performance across embodied tasks. Modern VLAs commonly employ diffusion action experts to efficiently generate high-precision continuous action chunks, while auto-regressive generation can be slower and less accurate at low-level control. Yet auto-regressive paradigms still provide complementary priors that can improve robustness and generalization in out-of-distribution environments. To leverage both paradigms, we propose Action-Draft-and-Verify (ADV): diffusion action expert drafts multiple candidate action chunks, and the VLM selects one by scoring all candidates in a single forward pass with a perplexity-style metric. Under matched backbones, training data, and action-chunk length, ADV improves success rate by +4.3 points in simulation and +19.7 points in real-world over diffusion-based baseline, with a single-pass VLM reranking overhead.

摘要（中文）: 视觉-语言-动作（VLA）模型最近在具身任务中表现出强大的性能。现代VLA通常采用扩散动作专家来高效生成高精度连续动作块，而自回归生成在低级控制方面可能较慢且精度较低。然而，自回归范式仍然提供补充的先验知识，可以提高分布式环境外的鲁棒性和泛化能力。为了利用这两种范式，我们提出了动作草稿-验证（ADV）：扩散动作专家起草多个候选动作块，然后VLM通过使用困惑度风格的指标在单个前向传递中对所有候选块进行评分来选择一个。在匹配的骨干网络、训练数据和动作块长度下，ADV在模拟环境中将成功率提高了+4.3个百分点，在真实世界中提高了+19.7个百分点，仅需单次VLM重新排序的开销。

TLDR: The paper introduces Action-Draft-and-Verify (ADV), a novel framework that combines diffusion action experts and vision-language models to improve the performance of VLA models in embodied tasks, achieving significant success rate improvements in both simulation and real-world settings.

简要说明: 该论文介绍了一种名为Action-Draft-and-Verify (ADV) 的新框架，它结合了扩散动作专家和视觉-语言模型，以提高VLA模型在具身任务中的性能，并在仿真和现实世界环境中取得了显著的成功率提升。

Authors: Chen Zhao, Zhuoran Wang, Haoyang Li, Shifeng Bao, Guanlin Li, Youhe Feng, Yang Li, Jie Tang, Jing Zhang

GMT: Goal-Conditioned Multimodal Transformer for 6-DOF Object Trajectory Synthesis in 3D Scenes

Abstract (English): Synthesizing controllable 6-DOF object manipulation trajectories in 3D environments is essential for enabling robots to interact with complex scenes, yet remains challenging due to the need for accurate spatial reasoning, physical feasibility, and multimodal scene understanding. Existing approaches often rely on 2D or partial 3D representations, limiting their ability to capture full scene geometry and constraining trajectory precision. We present GMT, a multimodal transformer framework that generates realistic and goal-directed object trajectories by jointly leveraging 3D bounding box geometry, point cloud context, semantic object categories, and target end poses. The model represents trajectories as continuous 6-DOF pose sequences and employs a tailored conditioning strategy that fuses geometric, semantic, contextual, and goaloriented information. Extensive experiments on synthetic and real-world benchmarks demonstrate that GMT outperforms state-of-the-art human motion and human-object interaction baselines, such as CHOIS and GIMO, achieving substantial gains in spatial accuracy and orientation control. Our method establishes a new benchmark for learningbased manipulation planning and shows strong generalization to diverse objects and cluttered 3D environments. Project page: https://huajian- zeng.github. io/projects/gmt/.

摘要（中文）: 在三维环境中合成可控的六自由度物体操作轨迹对于使机器人与复杂场景交互至关重要，但由于需要精确的空间推理、物理可行性和多模态场景理解，这仍然具有挑战性。现有方法通常依赖于二维或部分三维表示，限制了它们捕获完整场景几何形状的能力并约束了轨迹精度。我们提出了GMT，一个多模态Transformer框架，通过联合利用 3D 包围盒几何、点云环境、语义对象类别和目标终点姿态，生成逼真的和目标导向的物体轨迹。该模型将轨迹表示为连续的六自由度姿态序列，并采用定制的条件策略，融合几何、语义、环境和目标导向的信息。在合成和真实世界基准测试中进行的大量实验表明，GMT优于最先进的人体运动和人机交互基线，例如CHOIS和GIMO，在空间精度和方向控制方面取得了显著提升。我们的方法为基于学习的操纵规划建立了一个新的基准，并显示了对各种物体和杂乱的3D环境的强大泛化能力。项目主页：https://huajian- zeng.github. io/projects/gmt/.

TLDR: The paper introduces GMT, a multimodal transformer framework for generating controllable 6-DOF object manipulation trajectories in 3D scenes, outperforming state-of-the-art methods.

简要说明: 该论文介绍了GMT，一个多模态Transformer框架，用于生成3D场景中可控的6自由度物体操作轨迹，优于目前最先进的方法

Authors: Huajian Zeng, Abhishek Saroha, Daniel Cremers, Xi Wang

Specification-Aware Distribution Shaping for Robotics Foundation Models

Abstract (English): Robotics foundation models have demonstrated strong capabilities in executing natural language instructions across diverse tasks and environments. However, they remain largely data-driven and lack formal guarantees on safety and satisfaction of time-dependent specifications during deployment. In practice, robots often need to comply with operational constraints involving rich spatio-temporal requirements such as time-bounded goal visits, sequential objectives, and persistent safety conditions. In this work, we propose a specification-aware action distribution optimization framework that enforces a broad class of Signal Temporal Logic (STL) constraints during execution of a pretrained robotics foundation model without modifying its parameters. At each decision step, the method computes a minimally modified action distribution that satisfies a hard STL feasibility constraint by reasoning over the remaining horizon using forward dynamics propagation. We validate the proposed framework in simulation using a state-of-the-art robotics foundation model across multiple environments and complex specifications.

摘要（中文）: 机器人基础模型已展现出在不同任务和环境中执行自然语言指令的强大能力。然而，它们仍然主要由数据驱动，并且缺乏在部署期间对安全性和时间相关规范满足情况的形式化保证。在实践中，机器人通常需要遵守包含丰富的时空要求的操作约束，例如时间界定的目标访问、顺序目标和持续安全条件。在这项工作中，我们提出了一种规范感知的动作分布优化框架，该框架在预训练机器人基础模型的执行过程中，无需修改其参数即可强制执行广泛的信号时序逻辑 (STL) 约束。在每个决策步骤中，该方法通过使用前向动力学传播推理剩余时域，计算出满足硬STL可行性约束的最小修改动作分布。我们在仿真中使用最先进的机器人基础模型，在多个环境和复杂规范下验证了所提出的框架。

TLDR: This paper introduces a method to enforce Signal Temporal Logic (STL) constraints on the actions of pretrained robotics foundation models without retraining, ensuring safety and satisfaction of time-dependent specifications during execution.

简要说明: 本文提出了一种方法，可以在不重新训练的情况下，在预训练的机器人基础模型的动作上强制执行信号时序逻辑 (STL) 约束，从而确保执行期间的安全性和时间相关规范的满足。

Authors: Sadık Bera Yüksel, Derya Aksaray

RoboForge: Physically Optimized Text-guided Whole-Body Locomotion for Humanoids

Abstract (English): While generative models have become effective at producing human-like motions from text, transferring these motions to humanoid robots for physical execution remains challenging. Existing pipelines are often limited by retargeting, where kinematic quality is undermined by physical infeasibility, contact-transition errors, and the high cost of real-world dynamical data. We present a unified latent-driven framework that bridges natural language and whole-body humanoid locomotion through a retarget-free, physics-optimized pipeline. Rather than treating generation and control as separate stages, our key insight is to couple them bidirectionally under physical constraints.We introduce a Physical Plausibility Optimization (PP-Opt) module as the coupling interface. In the forward direction, PP-Opt refines a teacher-student distillation policy with a plausibility-centric reward to suppress artifacts such as floating, skating, and penetration. In the backward direction, it converts reward-optimized simulation rollouts into high-quality explicit motion data, which is used to fine-tune the motion generator toward a more physically plausible latent distribution. This bidirectional design forms a self-improving cycle: the generator learns a physically grounded latent space, while the controller learns to execute latent-conditioned behaviors with dynamical integrity.Extensive experiments on the Unitree G1 humanoid show that our bidirectional optimization improves tracking accuracy and success rates. Across IsaacLab and MuJoCo, the implicit latent-driven pipeline consistently outperforms conventional explicit retargeting baselines in both precision and stability. By coupling diffusion-based motion generation with physical plausibility optimization, our framework provides a practical path toward deployable text-guided humanoid intelligence.

摘要（中文）: 虽然生成模型在生成类似人类的文本驱动运动方面已变得有效，但将这些运动转移到人形机器人进行物理执行仍然具有挑战性。现有的流程通常受到重定向的限制，其运动学质量因物理不可行性、接触过渡错误以及高昂的真实世界动力学数据成本而受到损害。我们提出一个统一的潜在变量驱动框架，通过无重定向、物理优化的流程桥接自然语言和全身人形机器人运动。我们的核心思想不是将生成和控制视为单独的阶段，而是将它们在物理约束下双向耦合。我们引入了一个物理合理性优化（PP-Opt）模块作为耦合接口。在前向方向上，PP-Opt 使用以合理性为中心的奖励细化一个师生蒸馏策略，以抑制诸如漂浮、滑行和穿透等伪影。在后向方向上，它将奖励优化的模拟展开转化为高质量的显式运动数据，用于微调运动生成器，使其更接近于物理上合理的潜在分布。这种双向设计形成了一个自我完善的循环：生成器学习一个物理基础的潜在空间，而控制器学习以动态完整性执行潜在变量条件的行为。在宇树 G1 人形机器人上的大量实验表明，我们的双向优化提高了跟踪精度和成功率。在 IsaacLab 和 MuJoCo 中，隐式的潜在变量驱动流程在精度和稳定性方面始终优于传统的显式重定向基线。 通过将基于扩散的运动生成与物理合理性优化相结合，我们的框架为可部署的文本引导人形机器人智能提供了一条切实可行的途径。

TLDR: This paper introduces RoboForge, a framework that tightly couples text-based motion generation with physics optimization to achieve physically plausible and dynamically stable whole-body humanoid locomotion, outperforming traditional retargeting methods.

简要说明: 该论文介绍了RoboForge，一个将文本运动生成与物理优化紧密结合的框架，以实现物理上合理且动态稳定的全身人形机器人运动，优于传统的重定向方法。

Authors: Xichen Yuan, Zhe Li, Bofan Lyu, Kuangji Zuo, Yanshuo Lu, Gen Li, Jianfei Yang

DexViTac: Collecting Human Visuo-Tactile-Kinematic Demonstrations for Contact-Rich Dexterous Manipulation

Abstract (English): Large-scale, high-quality multimodal demonstrations are essential for robot learning of contact-rich dexterous manipulation. While human-centric data collection systems lower the barrier to scaling, they struggle to capture the tactile information during physical interactions. Motivated by this, we present DexViTac, a portable, human-centric data collection system tailored for contact-rich dexterous manipulation. The system enables the high-fidelity acquisition of first-person vision, high-density tactile sensing, end-effector poses, and hand kinematics within unstructured, in-the-wild environments. Building upon this hardware, we propose a kinematics-grounded tactile representation learning algorithm that effectively resolves semantic ambiguities within tactile signals. Leveraging the efficiency of DexViTac, we construct a multimodal dataset comprising over 2,400 visuo-tactile-kinematic demonstrations. Experiments demonstrate that DexViTac achieves a collection efficiency exceeding 248 demonstrations per hour and remains robust against complex visual occlusions. Real-world deployment confirms that policies trained with the proposed dataset and learning strategy achieve an average success rate exceeding 85% across four challenging tasks. This performance significantly outperforms baseline methods, thereby validating the substantial improvement the system provides for learning contact-rich dexterous manipulation. Project page: https://xitong-c.github.io/DexViTac/.

摘要（中文）: 大规模、高质量的多模态演示对于机器人学习富接触灵巧操作至关重要。虽然以人为中心的数据收集系统降低了扩展的门槛，但它们难以捕捉物理交互期间的触觉信息。为此，我们提出DexViTac，一个便携式、以人为中心的数据收集系统，专为富接触灵巧操作量身定制。该系统能够在非结构化的野外环境中高保真地获取第一人称视觉、高密度触觉传感、末端执行器姿态和手部运动学信息。在此硬件的基础上，我们提出了一种基于运动学的触觉表征学习算法，可以有效解决触觉信号中的语义模糊性。利用DexViTac的效率，我们构建了一个包含超过2400个视觉-触觉-运动学演示的多模态数据集。实验表明，DexViTac的收集效率超过每小时248个演示，并且对复杂的视觉遮挡具有鲁棒性。实际部署证实，使用所提出的数据集和学习策略训练的策略在四个具有挑战性的任务中实现了超过85%的平均成功率。这一性能显著优于基线方法，从而验证了该系统为学习富接触灵巧操作带来的显著改进。项目主页：https://xitong-c.github.io/DexViTac/。

TLDR: The paper introduces DexViTac, a portable system and dataset for collecting high-quality visuo-tactile-kinematic demonstrations of contact-rich dexterous manipulation, showing substantial improvements over baselines.

简要说明: 该论文介绍了一种名为DexViTac的便携系统和数据集，用于收集高质量的、富含触觉信息的灵巧操作演示，并在性能上显著优于基线方法。

Authors: Xitong Chen, Yifeng Pan, Min Li, Xiaotian Ding

Generative Control as Optimization: Time Unconditional Flow Matching for Adaptive and Robust Robotic Control

Abstract (English): Diffusion models and flow matching have become a cornerstone of robotic imitation learning, yet they suffer from a structural inefficiency where inference is often bound to a fixed integration schedule that is agnostic to state complexity. This paradigm forces the policy to expend the same computational budget on trivial motions as it does on complex tasks. We introduce Generative Control as Optimization (GeCO), a time-unconditional framework that transforms action synthesis from trajectory integration into iterative optimization. GeCO learns a stationary velocity field in the action-sequence space where expert behaviors form stable attractors. Consequently, test-time inference becomes an adaptive process that allocates computation based on convergence--exiting early for simple states while refining longer for difficult ones. Furthermore, this stationary geometry yields an intrinsic, training-free safety signal, as the field norm at the optimized action serves as a robust out-of-distribution (OOD) detector, remaining low for in-distribution states while significantly increasing for anomalies. We validate GeCO on standard simulation benchmarks and demonstrate seamless scaling to pi0-series Vision-Language-Action (VLA) models. As a plug-and-play replacement for standard flow-matching heads, GeCO improves success rates and efficiency with an optimization-native mechanism for safe deployment. Video and code can be found at https://hrh6666.github.io/GeCO/

摘要（中文）: 扩散模型和流动匹配已成为机器人模仿学习的基石，但它们存在结构性低效问题，即推理通常受限于与状态复杂度无关的固定积分调度。 这种范式迫使策略在简单运动和复杂任务上花费相同的计算预算。 我们引入了生成控制即优化 （GeCO），这是一个时间无条件的框架，它将动作合成从轨迹积分转换为迭代优化。 GeCO在动作序列空间中学习一个稳定的速度场，其中专家行为形成稳定的吸引子。 因此，测试时推理成为一个自适应过程，根据收敛情况分配计算资源——对简单状态提前退出，而对困难状态则进行更长时间的细化。 此外，这种静态几何结构产生了一种内在的、无需训练的安全信号，因为在优化动作下的场范数可以作为一种鲁棒的异于分布（OOD）检测器，在同分布状态下保持较低水平，而在异常情况下则显著增加。 我们在标准模拟基准上验证了GeCO，并展示了其向pi0系列视觉-语言-动作（VLA）模型的无缝扩展。 作为标准流动匹配头的即插即用替代品，GeCO通过一种原生优化的安全部署机制提高了成功率和效率。 视频和代码可以在https://hrh6666.github.io/GeCO/找到。

TLDR: The paper introduces Generative Control as Optimization (GeCO), a time-unconditional flow-matching framework for robotic control that adaptively allocates computation and provides a training-free safety signal, improving success rates and efficiency.

简要说明: 本文介绍了 Generative Control as Optimization (GeCO)，一种用于机器人控制的、时间无条件流匹配框架，它能自适应地分配计算资源，提供无需训练的安全信号，从而提高成功率和效率。

Authors: Zunzhe Zhang, Runhan Huang, Yicheng Liu, Shaoting Zhu, Linzhan Mou, Hang Zhao

EVA: Aligning Video World Models with Executable Robot Actions via Inverse Dynamics Rewards

Abstract (English): Video generative models are increasingly used as world models for robotics, where a model generates a future visual rollout conditioned on the current observation and task instruction, and an inverse dynamics model (IDM) converts the generated frames into executable robot actions. However, current video world models lack explicit executability constraints. As a result, visually coherent rollouts may still violate rigid-body and kinematic consistency, producing unstable or infeasible control commands when decoded by an IDM. We refer to this mismatch between visual generation and physically executable control as the executability gap. While this gap can be mitigated at inference time using techniques such as rejection sampling, such approaches are inefficient due to the high cost of video generation. In this paper, we leverage the executability gap as a training signal and introduce Executable Video Alignment (EVA), a reinforcement-learning post-training framework for aligning video world models. EVA trains an inverse dynamics model on real robot trajectories and repurposes it as a reward model that evaluates generated videos through the action sequences they induce, encouraging smooth motions measured by velocity, acceleration, and jerk while penalizing actions that violate embodiment constraints. Importantly, the reward remains informative even when generated videos contain severe visual artifacts, since such artifacts typically translate into unstable or out-of-bound actions. Experiments on the RoboTwin benchmark and a real bimanual robot show that EVA reduces embodiment-specific artifacts in generated rollouts and improves downstream task execution success.

摘要（中文）: 视频生成模型正越来越多地被用作机器人的世界模型，在该模型中，它根据当前观测和任务指令生成未来的视觉展开，然后逆动力学模型（IDM）将生成的帧转换为可执行的机器人动作。然而，当前的视频世界模型缺乏明确的可执行性约束。因此，视觉上连贯的展开仍然可能违反刚体和运动学一致性，从而在被IDM解码时产生不稳定或不可行的控制指令。我们将视觉生成和物理可执行控制之间的这种不匹配称为可执行性差距。虽然这种差距可以在推理时使用诸如拒绝采样等技术来缓解，但由于视频生成的高成本，这些方法效率低下。在本文中，我们利用可执行性差距作为训练信号，并引入可执行视频对齐（EVA），这是一个强化学习的后训练框架，用于对齐视频世界模型。EVA在真实机器人轨迹上训练一个逆动力学模型，并将其重新用作奖励模型，通过它引起的动作序列来评估生成的视频，鼓励由速度、加速度和加加速度测量的平滑运动，同时惩罚违反具身约束的动作。重要的是，即使生成的视频包含严重的视觉伪像，奖励仍然具有信息性，因为这些伪像通常会转化为不稳定或超出范围的动作。在RoboTwin基准测试和一个真实的双臂机器人上的实验表明，EVA减少了生成展开中特定于具身的伪像，并提高了下游任务执行的成功率。

TLDR: The paper introduces EVA, a reinforcement learning post-training framework, to align video world models with executable robot actions by using an inverse dynamics model as a reward function to penalize kinematic inconsistencies in generated videos, improving downstream task execution.

简要说明: 该论文介绍了EVA，一种强化学习后训练框架，通过使用逆动力学模型作为奖励函数来惩罚生成视频中的运动学不一致性，从而对齐视频世界模型和可执行机器人动作，提高下游任务的执行成功率。

Authors: Ruixiang Wang, Qingming Liu, Yueci Deng, Guiliang Liu, Zhen Liu, Kui Jia

VolumeDP: Modeling Volumetric Representation for Manipulation Policy Learning

Abstract (English): Imitation learning is a prominent paradigm for robotic manipulation. However, existing visual imitation methods map 2D image observations directly to 3D action outputs, imposing a 2D-3D mismatch that hinders spatial reasoning and degrades robustness. We present VolumeDP, a policy architecture that restores spatial alignment by explicitly reasoning in 3D. VolumeDP first lifts image features into a Volumetric Representation via cross-attention. It then selects task-relevant voxels with a learnable module and converts them into a compact set of spatial tokens, markedly reducing computation while preserving action-critical geometry. Finally, a multi-token decoder conditions on the entire token set to predict actions, thereby avoiding lossy aggregation that collapses multiple spatial tokens into a single descriptor. VolumeDP achieves a state-of-the-art average success rate of 88.8% on the LIBERO simulation benchmark, outperforming the strongest baseline by a substantial 14.8% improvement. It also delivers large performance gains over prior methods on the ManiSkill and LIBERO-Plus benchmarks. Real-world experiments further demonstrate higher success rates and robust generalization to novel spatial layouts, camera viewpoints, and environment backgrounds. Code will be released.

摘要（中文）: 模仿学习是机器人操作领域一种重要的范式。然而，现有的视觉模仿方法将2D图像观测直接映射到3D动作输出，造成2D-3D不匹配，阻碍了空间推理并降低了鲁棒性。我们提出VolumeDP，一种通过显式地在3D空间中进行推理来恢复空间对齐的策略架构。VolumeDP首先通过交叉注意力将图像特征提升到体素表示。然后，它利用一个可学习的模块选择与任务相关的体素，并将它们转换为一组紧凑的空间令牌，显著减少计算量，同时保留动作关键几何信息。最后，一个多令牌解码器以整个令牌集为条件来预测动作，从而避免了将多个空间令牌折叠成单个描述符的损耗性聚合。VolumeDP在LIBERO仿真基准测试上实现了88.8%的最先进平均成功率，比最强的基线提高了显著的14.8%。它还在ManiSkill和LIBERO-Plus基准测试上实现了相对于先前方法的大幅性能提升。真实世界实验进一步证明了更高的成功率和对新颖空间布局、相机视角和环境背景的稳健泛化能力。代码即将发布。

TLDR: The paper introduces VolumeDP, a novel policy architecture for robotic manipulation that uses a volumetric representation of visual input to improve spatial reasoning and performance, demonstrating state-of-the-art results in simulated and real-world environments.

简要说明: 该论文提出了 VolumeDP，一种新的机器人操作策略架构，它使用视觉输入的体积表示来提高空间推理和性能，并在模拟和真实环境中展示了最先进的结果。

Authors: Tianxing Zhou, Feiyang Xue, Zhangchen Ye, Tianyuan Yuan, Hang Zhao, Tao Jiang

AERR-Nav: Adaptive Exploration-Recovery-Reminiscing Strategy for Zero-Shot Object Navigation

Abstract (English): Zero-Shot Object Navigation (ZSON) in unknown multi-floor environments presents a significant challenge. Recent methods, mostly based on semantic value greedy waypoint selection, spatial topology-enhanced memory, and Multimodal Large Language Model (MLLM) as a decision-making framework, have led to improvements. However, these architectures struggle to balance exploration and exploitation for ZSON when encountering unseen environments, especially in multi-floor settings, such as robots getting stuck at narrow intersections, endlessly wandering, or failing to find stair entrances. To overcome these challenges, we propose AERR-Nav, a Zero-Shot Object Navigation framework that dynamically adjusts its state based on the robot's environment. Specifically, AERR-Nav has the following two key advantages: (1) An Adaptive Exploration-Recovery-Reminiscing Strategy, enables robots to dynamically transition between three states, facilitating specialized responses to diverse navigation scenarios. (2) An Adaptive Exploration State featuring Fast and Slow-Thinking modes helps robots better balance exploration, exploitation, and higher-level reasoning based on evolving environmental information. Extensive experiments on the HM3D and MP3D benchmarks demonstrate that our AERR-Nav achieves state-of-the-art performance among zero-shot methods. Comprehensive ablation studies further validate the efficacy of our proposed strategy and modules.

摘要（中文）: 在未知的多层环境中进行零样本物体导航（ZSON）是一项重大挑战。最近的研究方法，主要基于语义价值贪婪路径点选择、空间拓扑增强记忆以及多模态大型语言模型（MLLM）作为决策框架，取得了一定的进展。然而，这些架构在遇到未见过的环境时，难以平衡ZSON的探索与利用，尤其是在多层环境中，例如机器人卡在狭窄的交叉口、无休止地徘徊，或无法找到楼梯入口。为了克服这些挑战，我们提出了一种零样本物体导航框架AERR-Nav，它可以根据机器人的环境动态调整其状态。具体而言，AERR-Nav具有以下两个关键优势：（1）一种自适应探索-恢复-回顾策略，使机器人能够在三种状态之间动态转换，从而促进对各种导航场景的专门响应。（2）一种具有快速和慢速思考模式的自适应探索状态，帮助机器人更好地根据不断变化的环境信息来平衡探索、利用和更高层次的推理。在HM3D和MP3D基准上的大量实验表明，我们的AERR-Nav在零样本方法中实现了最先进的性能。全面的消融研究进一步验证了我们提出的策略和模块的有效性。

TLDR: The paper introduces AERR-Nav, a novel Zero-Shot Object Navigation framework that adaptively adjusts its state to balance exploration and exploitation using an Exploration-Recovery-Reminiscing strategy and Fast/Slow Thinking modes, achieving state-of-the-art performance on HM3D and MP3D benchmarks.

简要说明: 本文介绍AERR-Nav，一种新颖的零样本物体导航框架，它利用探索-恢复-回忆策略和快/慢思考模式自适应地调整其状态，以平衡探索和利用，并在HM3D和MP3D基准测试中实现了最先进的性能。

Authors: Jingzhi Huang, Junkai Huang, Haoyang Yang, Haoang Li, Yi Wang

REAL: Robust Extreme Agility via Spatio-Temporal Policy Learning and Physics-Guided Filtering

Abstract (English): Extreme legged parkour demands rapid terrain assessment and precise foot placement under highly dynamic conditions. While recent learning-based systems achieve impressive agility, they remain fundamentally fragile to perceptual degradation, where even brief visual noise or latency can cause catastrophic failure. To overcome this, we propose Robust Extreme Agility Learning (REAL), an end-to-end framework for reliable parkour under sensory corruption. Instead of relying on perfectly clean perception, REAL tightly couples vision, proprioceptive history, and temporal memory. We distill a cross-modal teacher policy into a deployable student equipped with a FiLM-modulated Mamba backbone to actively filter visual noise and build short-term terrain memory actively. Furthermore, a physics-guided Bayesian state estimator enforces rigid-body consistency during high-impact maneuvers. Validated on a Unitree Go2 quadruped, REAL successfully traverses extreme obstacles even with a 1-meter visual blind zone, while strictly satisfying real-time control constraints with a bounded 13.1 ms inference time.

摘要（中文）: 极端足式跑酷需要在高度动态的条件下进行快速的地形评估和精准的落脚点选择。尽管最近基于学习的系统实现了令人印象深刻的敏捷性，但它们在感知退化方面仍然存在根本性的脆弱性，即使是短暂的视觉噪声或延迟也可能导致灾难性的失败。为了克服这一点，我们提出了鲁棒极端敏捷学习（REAL），这是一个端到端的框架，用于在感官受损的情况下实现可靠的跑酷。REAL没有依赖于完美干净的感知，而是紧密地耦合了视觉、本体感受历史和时间记忆。我们将跨模态教师策略提炼成一个可部署的学生策略，该学生策略配备了FiLM调制的Mamba骨干网络，以主动过滤视觉噪声并积极构建短期地形记忆。此外，一个物理引导的贝叶斯状态估计器在高冲击机动期间强制刚体一致性。在宇树Go2四足机器人上的验证表明，即使存在1米的视觉盲区，REAL也能成功地穿越极端障碍物，同时严格满足实时控制约束，推理时间被限制在13.1毫秒内。

TLDR: The paper introduces REAL, a robust reinforcement learning framework for extreme legged parkour that combines vision, proprioception, temporal memory, and physics-guided filtering to achieve agility under sensory corruption, validated on a Unitree Go2.

简要说明: 该论文介绍了REAL，一个用于极端腿部跑酷的鲁棒强化学习框架，它结合了视觉、本体感受、时间记忆和物理引导滤波，从而在感觉退化的情况下实现敏捷性，并在Unitree Go2上进行了验证。

Authors: Jialong Liu, Dehan Shen, Yanbo Wen, Zeyu Jiang, Changhao Chen

VectorWorld: Efficient Streaming World Model via Diffusion Flow on Vector Graphs

Abstract (English): Closed-loop evaluation of autonomous-driving policies requires interactive simulation beyond log replay. However, existing generative world models often degrade in closed loop due to (i) history-free initialization that mismatches policy inputs, (ii) multi-step sampling latency that violates real-time budgets, and (iii) compounding kinematic infeasibility over long horizons. We propose VectorWorld, a streaming world model that incrementally generates ego-centric $64 \mathrm{m}\times 64\mathrm{m}$ lane--agent vector-graph tiles during rollout. VectorWorld aligns initialization with history-conditioned policies by producing a policy-compatible interaction state via a motion-aware gated VAE. It enables real-time outpainting via solver-free one-step masked completion with an edge-gated relational DiT trained with interval-conditioned MeanFlow and JVP-based large-step supervision. To stabilize long-horizon rollouts, we introduce $Δ$Sim, a physics-aligned non-ego (NPC) policy with hybrid discrete--continuous actions and differentiable kinematic logit shaping. On Waymo open motion and nuPlan, VectorWorld improves map-structure fidelity and initialization validity, and supports stable, real-time $1\mathrm{km}+$ closed-loop rollouts (\href{https://github.com/jiangchaokang/VectorWorld}{code}).

摘要（中文）: 自动驾驶策略的闭环评估需要在日志回放之外进行交互式仿真。然而，现有的生成世界模型在闭环中经常性能下降，原因包括：（i）无历史信息的初始化与策略输入不匹配；（ii）多步采样延迟违反实时性要求；以及（iii）长时程滚动中运动学不可行性的累积。我们提出了VectorWorld，一种流式世界模型，可以在rollout过程中增量生成以自我为中心的$64 \mathrm{m}\times 64\mathrm{m}$车道-代理向量图块。VectorWorld通过运动感知门控VAE生成与策略兼容的交互状态，从而使初始化与历史条件策略对齐。它通过无求解器的单步掩码补全实现实时外推，该补全基于使用区间条件MeanFlow和基于JVP的大步监督训练的边门控关系DiT。为了稳定长时程rollout，我们引入了$Δ$Sim，一种物理对齐的非自我（NPC）策略，具有混合离散-连续动作和可微运动学logit塑造。在Waymo open motion和nuPlan数据集上，VectorWorld提高了地图结构的保真度和初始化有效性，并支持稳定、实时的$1\mathrm{km}+$闭环rollout（\href{https://github.com/jiangchaokang/VectorWorld}{code}）。

TLDR: VectorWorld is a streaming world model for autonomous driving that addresses challenges in closed-loop simulation by using a diffusion flow model on vector graphs, enabling real-time and stable long-horizon rollouts. It improves map fidelity and initialization validity.

简要说明: VectorWorld是一个用于自动驾驶的流式世界模型，通过在向量图上使用扩散流模型解决了闭环仿真中的挑战，从而实现实时和稳定的长程模拟。 它提高了地图保真度和初始化有效性。

Authors: Chaokang Jiang, Desen Zhou, Jiuming Liu, Kevin Li Sun

HeiSD: Hybrid Speculative Decoding for Embodied Vision-Language-Action Models with Kinematic Awareness

Abstract (English): Vision-Language-Action (VLA) Models have become the mainstream solution for robot control, but suffer from slow inference speeds. Speculative Decoding (SD) is a promising acceleration method which can be divided into two categories: drafter-based SD and retrieval-based SD. Existing methods fail to analyze the advantages and disadvantages of these two types of SD in VLA models, leading to their sole application or optimization. In this paper, we analyze the trajectory patterns of robots controlled by the VLA model and derive a key insight: the two types of SD should be used in a hybrid manner. However, achieving hybrid SD in VLA models poses several challenges: (1) draft rejection and persistent errors in retrieval-based SD; (2) difficulty in determining the hybrid boundary. To address these, we propose the HeiSD framework. We propose a retrieval-based SD optimization method in HeiSD,which contains a verify-skip mechanism and a sequence-wise relaxed acceptance strategy. Moreover, we proposed a kinematic-based fused metric in HeiSD to automatically determine the hybrid boundary. Experimental results demonstrate that HeiSD attains a speedup of up to 2.45x in simulation benchmarks and 2.06x~2.41x in real-world scenarios, while sustaining a high task success rate.

摘要（中文）: 视觉-语言-动作 (VLA) 模型已成为机器人控制的主流解决方案，但存在推理速度慢的问题。推测解码 (SD) 是一种有前景的加速方法，可分为两类：基于起草器的 SD 和基于检索的 SD。现有方法未能分析这两种 SD 在 VLA 模型中的优缺点，导致它们仅被单独应用或优化。在本文中，我们分析了 VLA 模型控制的机器人的轨迹模式，并得出一个关键见解：这两种类型的 SD 应该以混合方式使用。然而，在 VLA 模型中实现混合 SD 面临着几个挑战：（1）基于检索的 SD 中的草稿拒绝和持续性错误；（2）难以确定混合边界。为了解决这些问题，我们提出了 HeiSD 框架。我们在 HeiSD 中提出了一种基于检索的 SD 优化方法，该方法包含验证-跳过机制和序列式松弛接受策略。此外，我们在 HeiSD 中提出了一种基于运动学的融合度量，以自动确定混合边界。实验结果表明，HeiSD 在模拟基准测试中获得了高达 2.45 倍的加速，在真实场景中获得了 2.06 倍 ~ 2.41 倍的加速，同时保持了较高的任务成功率。

TLDR: The paper introduces HeiSD, a hybrid speculative decoding framework for VLA models with kinematic awareness, achieving significant speedups in both simulation and real-world robot control while maintaining task success.

简要说明: 该论文介绍了 HeiSD，一个混合推测解码框架，用于具有运动学感知的 VLA 模型，在模拟和真实机器人控制中都实现了显著的加速，同时保持了任务的成功率。

Authors: Zihao Zheng, Zhihao Mao, Sicheng Tian, Maoliang Li, Jiayu Chen, Xinhao Sun, Zhaobo Zhang, Xuanzhe Liu, Donggang Cao, Hong Mei, Xiang Chen

KineVLA: Towards Kinematics-Aware Vision-Language-Action Models with Bi-Level Action Decomposition

Abstract (English): In this paper, we introduce a novel kinematics-rich vision-language-action (VLA) task, in which language commands densely encode diverse kinematic attributes (such as direction, trajectory, orientation, and relative displacement) from initiation through completion, at key moments, unlike existing action instructions that capture kinematics only coarsely or partially, thereby supporting fine-grained and personalized manipulation. In this setting, where task goals remain invariant while execution trajectories must adapt to instruction-level kinematic specifications. To address this challenge, we propose KineVLA, a vision-language-action framework that explicitly decouples goal-level invariance from kinematics-level variability through a bi-level action representation and bi-level reasoning tokens to serve as explicit, supervised intermediate variables that align language and action. To support this task, we construct the kinematics-aware VLA datasets spanning both simulation and real-world robotic platforms, featuring instruction-level kinematic variations and bi-level annotations. Extensive experiments on LIBERO and a Realman-75 robot demonstrate that KineVLA consistently outperforms strong VLA baselines on kinematics-sensitive benchmarks, achieving more precise, controllable, and generalizable manipulation behaviors.

摘要（中文）: 本文介绍了一种新型的富含运动学的视觉-语言-动作（VLA）任务，其中语言指令密集编码从启动到完成过程中的多种运动学属性（如方向、轨迹、姿态和相对位移），在关键时刻体现，这与现有仅粗略或部分捕捉运动学的动作指令不同，从而支持精细化和个性化的操作。在此设置下，任务目标保持不变，但执行轨迹必须适应指令级的运动学规范。为了应对这一挑战，我们提出了KineVLA，一个视觉-语言-动作框架，它通过双层动作表示和双层推理token，将目标层面的不变性与运动学层面的可变性显式地解耦，以此作为显式的、受监督的中间变量来对齐语言和动作。为了支持这项任务，我们构建了涵盖仿真和真实世界机器人平台的、具有运动学意识的VLA数据集，其特征是指令级的运动学变化和双层标注。在LIBERO和Realman-75机器人上的大量实验表明，KineVLA在运动学敏感的基准测试中始终优于强大的VLA基线，实现了更精确、可控和可泛化的操作行为。

TLDR: The paper introduces a kinematics-aware VLA task and framework (KineVLA) that explicitly decouples goal-level invariance from kinematics-level variability for more precise and controllable robotic manipulation, supported by new datasets in simulation and the real world.

Authors: Gaoge Han, Zhengqing Gao, Ziwen Li, Jiaxin Huang, Shaoli Huang, Fakhri Karray, Mingming Gong, Tongliang Liu

Interpreting Context-Aware Human Preferences for Multi-Objective Robot Navigation

Abstract (English): Robots operating in human-shared environments must not only achieve task-level navigation objectives such as safety and efficiency, but also adapt their behavior to human preferences. However, as human preferences are typically expressed in natural language and depend on environmental context, it is difficult to directly integrate them into low-level robot control policies. In this work, we present a pipeline that enables robots to understand and apply context-dependent navigation preferences by combining foundational models with a Multi-Objective Reinforcement Learning (MORL) navigation policy. Thus, our approach integrates high-level semantic reasoning with low-level motion control. A Vision-Language Model (VLM) extracts structured environmental context from onboard visual observations, while Large Language Models (LLM) convert natural language user feedback into interpretable, context-dependent behavioral rules stored in a persistent but updatable rule memory. A preference translation module then maps contextual information and stored rules into numerical preference vectors that parameterize a pretrained MORL policy for real-time navigation adaptation. We evaluate the proposed framework through quantitative component-level evaluations, a user study, and real-world robot deployments in various indoor environments. Our results demonstrate that the system reliably captures user intent, generates consistent preference vectors, and enables controllable behavior adaptation across diverse contexts. Overall, the proposed pipeline improves the adaptability, transparency, and usability of robots operating in shared human environments, while maintaining safe and responsive real-time control.

摘要（中文）: 运行于人机共享环境中的机器人不仅要实现安全性和效率等任务级别的导航目标，还要将其行为适应人类偏好。然而，由于人类偏好通常以自然语言表达并依赖于环境背景，因此很难将其直接整合到低层级的机器人控制策略中。在这项工作中，我们提出了一种流水线，它通过结合基础模型与多目标强化学习（MORL）导航策略，使机器人能够理解和应用与环境相关的导航偏好。因此，我们的方法将高层级的语义推理与低层级的运动控制相结合。视觉-语言模型（VLM）从车载视觉观测中提取结构化的环境背景，而大型语言模型（LLM）将自然语言用户反馈转化为可解释的、与环境相关的行为规则，并存储在持久但可更新的规则记忆中。然后，偏好转换模块将上下文信息和存储的规则映射到数值偏好向量，这些向量参数化了预训练的MORL策略，用于实时的导航适应。我们通过定量的组件级别评估、用户研究以及在各种室内环境中的真实世界机器人部署来评估所提出的框架。我们的结果表明，该系统能够可靠地捕捉用户意图，生成一致的偏好向量，并能在不同的背景下实现可控的行为适应。总而言之，所提出的流水线提高了运行于共享人类环境中的机器人的适应性、透明性和可用性，同时保持了安全和响应迅速的实时控制。

TLDR: This paper introduces a pipeline that combines VLMs and LLMs with MORL to enable robots to understand and apply context-dependent navigation preferences expressed in natural language, demonstrating improved adaptability and transparency in human-robot interaction.

简要说明: 本文介绍了一个结合 VLM、LLM 和 MORL 的流程，使机器人能够理解并应用以自然语言表达的、依赖于上下文的导航偏好，从而提高人机交互的适应性和透明度。

Authors: Tharun Sethuraman, Subham Agrawal, Nils Dengler, Jorge de Heuvel, Teena Hassan, Maren Bennewitz

P$^{3}$Nav: End-to-End Perception, Prediction and Planning for Vision-and-Language Navigation

Abstract (English): In Vision-and-Language Navigation (VLN), an agent is required to plan a path to the target specified by the language instruction, using its visual observations. Consequently, prevailing VLN methods primarily focus on building powerful planners through visual-textual alignment. However, these approaches often bypass the imperative of comprehensive scene understanding prior to planning, leaving the agent with insufficient perception or prediction capabilities. Thus, we propose P$^{3}$Nav, a novel end-to-end framework integrating perception, prediction, and planning in a unified pipeline to strengthen the VLN agent's scene understanding and boost navigation success. Specifically, P$^{3}$Nav augments perception by extracting complementary cues from object-level and map-level perspectives. Subsequently, our P$^{3}$Nav predicts waypoints to model the agent's potential future states, endowing the agent with intrinsic awareness of candidate positions during navigation. Conditioned on these future waypoints, P$^{3}$Nav further forecasts semantic map cues, enabling proactive planning and reducing the strict reliance on purely historical context. Integrating these perceptual and predictive cues, a holistic planning module finally carries out the VLN tasks. Extensive experiments demonstrate that our P$^{3}$Nav achieves new state-of-the-art performance on the REVERIE, R2R-CE, and RxR-CE benchmarks.

摘要（中文）: 在视觉-语言导航(VLN)中，智能体需要利用视觉观测，规划一条到达由语言指令指定的目标的路径。因此，目前主流的VLN方法主要集中于通过视觉-文本对齐来构建强大的规划器。然而，这些方法通常忽略了在规划之前进行全面的场景理解这一必要性，导致智能体感知或预测能力不足。因此，我们提出了P$^{3}$Nav，一种新颖的端到端框架，它在一个统一的流程中整合了感知、预测和规划，以增强VLN智能体的场景理解并提高导航成功率。具体来说，P$^{3}$Nav通过从物体级别和地图级别视角提取互补线索来增强感知能力。随后，我们的P$^{3}$Nav预测航路点，以建模智能体潜在的未来状态，赋予智能体在导航过程中对候选位置的内在感知。在这些未来航路点的基础上，P$^{3}$Nav进一步预测语义地图线索，从而实现主动规划，并减少对纯粹历史语境的严格依赖。结合这些感知和预测线索，一个整体的规划模块最终执行VLN任务。大量的实验表明，我们的P$^{3}$Nav在REVERIE、R2R-CE和RxR-CE基准测试上达到了新的最优性能。

TLDR: The paper introduces P$^{3}$Nav, a novel end-to-end framework for Vision-Language Navigation (VLN) that integrates perception, prediction, and planning to improve scene understanding and navigation success, achieving state-of-the-art results on multiple VLN benchmarks.

简要说明: 该论文介绍了P$^{3}$Nav，一种用于视觉-语言导航（VLN）的新型端到端框架，它集成了感知、预测和规划，以提高场景理解和导航成功率，并在多个VLN基准测试中实现了最先进的结果。

Authors: Tianfu Li, Wenbo Chen, Haoxuan Xu, Xinhu Zheng, Haoang Li

FloorPlan-VLN: A New Paradigm for Floor Plan Guided Vision-Language Navigation

Abstract (English): Existing Vision-Language Navigation (VLN) task requires agents to follow verbose instructions, ignoring some potentially useful global spatial priors, limiting their capability to reason about spatial structures. Although human-readable spatial schematics (e.g., floor plans) are ubiquitous in real-world buildings, current agents lack the cognitive ability to comprehend and utilize them. To bridge this gap, we introduce \textbf{FloorPlan-VLN}, a new paradigm that leverages structured semantic floor plans as global spatial priors to enable navigation with only concise instructions. We first construct the FloorPlan-VLN dataset, which comprises over 10k episodes across 72 scenes. It pairs more than 100 semantically annotated floor plans with Matterport3D-based navigation trajectories and concise instructions that omit step-by-step guidance. Then, we propose a simple yet effective method \textbf{FP-Nav} that uses a dual-view, spatio-temporally aligned video sequence, and auxiliary reasoning tasks to align observations, floor plans, and instructions. When evaluated under this new benchmark, our method significantly outperforms adapted state-of-the-art VLN baselines, achieving more than a 60\% relative improvement in navigation success rate. Furthermore, comprehensive noise modeling and real-world deployments demonstrate the feasibility and robustness of FP-Nav to actuation drift and floor plan distortions. These results validate the effectiveness of floor plan guided navigation and highlight FloorPlan-VLN as a promising step toward more spatially intelligent navigation.

摘要（中文）: 现有的视觉-语言导航 (VLN) 任务要求智能体遵循冗长的指令，忽略了一些潜在有用的全局空间先验，限制了其对空间结构进行推理的能力。尽管人类可读的空间示意图（例如，平面图）在现实世界的建筑中普遍存在，但当前的智能体缺乏理解和利用它们的认知能力。为了弥合这一差距，我们引入 \textbf{FloorPlan-VLN}，这是一种新的范式，它利用结构化的语义平面图作为全局空间先验，以实现仅需简洁指令的导航。我们首先构建了 FloorPlan-VLN 数据集，该数据集包含 72 个场景中超过 1 万个导航片段。它将 100 多个语义标注的平面图与基于 Matterport3D 的导航轨迹和省略逐步指导的简洁指令配对。然后，我们提出了一种简单而有效的方法 \textbf{FP-Nav}，该方法使用双视图、时空对齐的视频序列和辅助推理任务，来对齐观察结果、平面图和指令。在这个新的基准下进行评估时，我们的方法明显优于改进后的最先进的 VLN 基线方法，导航成功率相对提高了 60% 以上。此外，全面的噪声建模和现实世界的部署证明了 FP-Nav 对于执行偏差和平面图变形的可行性和鲁棒性。这些结果验证了平面图引导导航的有效性，并强调 FloorPlan-VLN 是朝着更具空间智能的导航迈出的有希望的一步。

TLDR: The paper introduces FloorPlan-VLN, a new VLN paradigm using floor plans as spatial priors, a corresponding dataset, and a novel method called FP-Nav, achieving significant improvements in navigation success. It addresses the limitation of current VLN approaches that ignore global spatial information.

简要说明: 该论文介绍了FloorPlan-VLN，一种使用楼层平面图作为空间先验的新的VLN范式，以及一个相应的基准数据集，并提出了一种名为FP-Nav的新方法，在导航成功率方面取得了显著提升。 该方法旨在解决当前VLN方法忽略全局空间信息的局限性。

Authors: Kehan Chen, Yan Huang, Dong An, Jiawei He, Yifei Su, Jing Liu, Nianfeng Liu, Liang Wang

SafeLand: Safe Autonomous Landing in Unknown Environments with Bayesian Semantic Mapping

Abstract (English): Autonomous landing of uncrewed aerial vehicles (UAVs) in unknown, dynamic environments poses significant safety challenges, particularly near people and infrastructure, as UAVs transition to routine urban and rural operations. Existing methods often rely on prior maps, heavy sensors like LiDAR, static markers, or fail to handle non-cooperative dynamic obstacles like humans, limiting generalization and real-time performance. To address these challenges, we introduce SafeLand, a lean, vision-based system for safe autonomous landing (SAL) that requires no prior information and operates only with a camera and a lightweight height sensor. Our approach constructs an online semantic ground map via deep learning-based semantic segmentation, optimized for embedded deployment and trained on a consolidation of seven curated public aerial datasets (achieving 70.22% mIoU across 20 classes), which is further refined through Bayesian probabilistic filtering with temporal semantic decay to robustly identify metric-scale landing spots. A behavior tree then governs adaptive landing, iteratively validates the spot, and reacts in real time to dynamic obstacles by pausing, climbing, or rerouting to alternative spots, maximizing human safety. We extensively evaluate our method in 200 simulations and 60 end-to-end field tests across industrial, urban, and rural environments at altitudes up to 100m, demonstrating zero false negatives for human detection. Compared to the state of the art, SafeLand achieves sub-second response latency, substantially lower than previous methods, while maintaining a superior success rate of 95%. To facilitate further research in aerial robotics, we release SafeLand's segmentation model as a plug-and-play ROS package, available at https://github.com/markus-42/SafeLand.

摘要（中文）: 在未知、动态环境中无人机（UAV）的自主着陆带来了严峻的安全挑战，尤其是在人员和基础设施附近，因为无人机正在向日常城乡运营过渡。现有方法通常依赖于先验地图、诸如激光雷达之类的重型传感器、静态标记，或者无法处理诸如人类之类的非合作动态障碍物，从而限制了泛化能力和实时性能。为了应对这些挑战，我们推出 SafeLand，一种轻量级的、基于视觉的安全自主着陆（SAL）系统，它不需要先验信息，仅使用摄像头和轻型高度传感器即可运行。我们的方法通过基于深度学习的语义分割构建在线语义地面地图，该语义分割针对嵌入式部署进行了优化，并在七个精心策划的公共航空数据集的整合上进行训练（在 20 个类别中实现 70.22% 的 mIoU），并通过具有时间语义衰减的贝叶斯概率滤波进一步细化，以稳健地识别度量尺度的着陆点。然后，行为树控制自适应着陆，迭代验证着陆点，并通过暂停、爬升或重新规划到备选着陆点来实时响应动态障碍物，从而最大限度地提高人员安全。我们通过 200 次模拟和 60 次端到端实地测试，在工业、城市和乡村环境中对我们的方法进行了广泛评估，高度达 100 米，证明人类检测的假阴性率为零。与最先进的方法相比，SafeLand 实现了亚秒级的响应延迟，远低于以前的方法，同时保持了 95% 的卓越成功率。为了促进航空机器人领域的进一步研究，我们将 SafeLand 的分割模型作为即插即用的 ROS 软件包发布，网址为 https://github.com/markus-42/SafeLand。

TLDR: SafeLand is a vision-based system for safe autonomous UAV landing in unknown environments using semantic segmentation and Bayesian filtering, achieving high success rates and low latency in diverse environments.

简要说明: SafeLand是一个基于视觉的安全自主无人机着陆系统，它利用语义分割和贝叶斯滤波技术在未知环境中实现着陆，并在各种环境下实现了高成功率和低延迟。

Authors: Markus Gross, Andreas Greiner, Sai Bharadhwaj Matha, Felix Soest, Daniel Cremers, Henri Meeß

OmniVLN: Omnidirectional 3D Perception and Token-Efficient LLM Reasoning for Visual-Language Navigation across Air and Ground Platforms

Abstract (English): Language-guided embodied navigation requires an agent to interpret object-referential instructions, search across multiple rooms, localize the referenced target, and execute reliable motion toward it. Existing systems remain limited in real indoor environments because narrow field-of-view sensing exposes only a partial local scene at each step, often forcing repeated rotations, delaying target discovery, and producing fragmented spatial understanding; meanwhile, directly prompting LLMs with dense 3D maps or exhaustive object lists quickly exceeds the context budget. We present OmniVLN, a zero-shot visual-language navigation framework that couples omnidirectional 3D perception with token-efficient hierarchical reasoning for both aerial and ground robots. OmniVLN fuses a rotating LiDAR and panoramic vision into a hardware-agnostic mapping stack, incrementally constructs a five-layer Dynamic Scene Graph (DSG) from mesh geometry to room- and building-level structure, and stabilizes high-level topology through persistent-homology-based room partitioning and hybrid geometric/VLM relation verification. For navigation, the global DSG is transformed into an agent-centric 3D octant representation with multi-resolution spatial attention prompting, enabling the LLM to progressively filter candidate rooms, infer egocentric orientation, localize target objects, and emit executable navigation primitives while preserving fine local detail and compact long-range memory. Experiments show that the proposed hierarchical interface improves spatial referring accuracy from 77.27\% to 93.18\%, reduces cumulative prompt tokens by up to 61.7\% in cluttered multi-room settings, and improves navigation success by up to 11.68\% over a flat-list baseline. We will release the code and an omnidirectional multimodal dataset to support reproducible research.

摘要（中文）: 语言引导的具身导航要求智能体解释指向对象的指令，跨多个房间搜索，定位参考目标，并执行可靠的运动到达目标。现有的系统在真实的室内环境中仍然有限制，因为窄视野的感知在每一步都只暴露局部场景的一部分，通常迫使重复旋转，延迟目标发现，并产生碎片化的空间理解；与此同时，直接用密集的3D地图或详尽的对象列表提示大型语言模型 (LLM) 会迅速超出上下文预算。我们提出了OmniVLN，这是一个零样本视觉-语言导航框架，它将全向3D感知与Token高效的分层推理相结合，适用于空中和地面机器人。OmniVLN将旋转激光雷达和全景视觉融合到一个硬件无关的建图堆栈中，从网格几何体到房间和建筑级别的结构，增量构建一个五层动态场景图（DSG），并通过基于持久同调的房间分割和混合几何/VLM关系验证来稳定高层拓扑结构。对于导航，全局DSG被转换为以智能体为中心的3D八分象限表示，并具有多分辨率空间注意力提示，使LLM能够逐步过滤候选房间，推断自我中心方向，定位目标对象，并发射可执行的导航原语，同时保留精细的局部细节和紧凑的长程记忆。实验表明，所提出的分层接口将空间指代准确率从77.27%提高到93.18%，在杂乱的多房间环境中将累积提示 Token 减少高达61.7%，并且相对于扁平列表基线，导航成功率提高了高达11.68%。我们将发布代码和一个全向多模态数据集，以支持可重复的研究。

TLDR: The paper introduces OmniVLN, a novel zero-shot visual-language navigation framework that uses omnidirectional 3D perception and token-efficient hierarchical reasoning with LLMs for both aerial and ground robots, demonstrating improved navigation success and reduced prompt tokens.

简要说明: 该论文介绍了OmniVLN，一种新颖的零样本视觉语言导航框架，它结合了全向3D感知和token高效的分层推理，利用大型语言模型(LLM)用于空中和地面机器人，展示了改进的导航成功率和减少的提示token。

Authors: Zhongyuang Liu, Min He, Shaonan Yu, Xinhang Xu, Muqing Cao, Jianping Li, Jianfei Yang, Lihua Xie

ReSteer: Quantifying and Refining the Steerability of Multitask Robot Policies

Abstract (English): Despite strong multi-task pretraining, existing policies often exhibit poor task steerability. For example, a robot may fail to respond to a new instruction ``put the bowl in the sink" when moving towards the oven, executing ``close the oven", even though it can complete both tasks when executed separately. We propose ReSteer, a framework to quantify and improve task steerability in multitask robot policies. We conduct an exhaustive evaluation of state-of-the-art policies, revealing a common lack of steerability. We find that steerability is associated with limited overlap among training task trajectory distributions, and introduce a proxy metric to measure this overlap from policy behavior. Building on this insight, ReSteer improves steerability via three components: (i) a steerability estimator that identifies low-steerability states without full-rollout evaluation, (ii) a steerable data generator that synthesizes motion segments from these states, and (iii) a self-refinement pipeline that improves policy steerability using the generated data. In simulation on LIBERO, ReSteer improves steerability by 11\% over 18k rollouts. In real-world experiments, we show that improved steerability is critical for interactive use, enabling users to instruct robots to perform any task at any time. We hope this work motivates further study on quantifying steerability and data collection strategies for large robot policies.

摘要（中文）: 尽管经过强大的多任务预训练，现有的策略往往表现出较差的任务可控性。例如，当机器人正朝着烤箱移动，执行“关上烤箱”时，即使它可以分别完成这两个任务，它也可能无法响应新的指令“把碗放到水槽里”。我们提出了ReSteer，一个用于量化和改进多任务机器人策略中任务可控性的框架。我们对最先进的策略进行了详尽的评估，揭示了普遍缺乏可控性。我们发现可控性与训练任务轨迹分布之间的有限重叠有关，并引入了一个代理指标来衡量策略行为中的这种重叠。基于这一观察，ReSteer通过三个组成部分来提高可控性：（i）一个可控性估计器，无需完整部署评估即可识别低可控性状态；（ii）一个可控数据生成器，可以从这些状态合成运动片段；以及（iii）一个自精化流水线，使用生成的数据来提高策略的可控性。在LIBERO模拟器中的18k次部署中，ReSteer将可控性提高了11%。在真实世界的实验中，我们表明，改进的可控性对于交互式使用至关重要，使用户能够随时指示机器人执行任何任务。我们希望这项工作能够激发人们对量化可控性和大数据机器人策略的数据收集策略的进一步研究。

TLDR: The paper introduces ReSteer, a framework to quantify and improve task steerability in multitask robot policies, addressing the issue of robots failing to respond to new instructions during task execution through a steerability estimator, data generator, and self-refinement pipeline.

简要说明: 本文介绍ReSteer，一个用于量化和提高多任务机器人策略中的任务可操纵性的框架。该框架通过可操纵性估计器、数据生成器和自优化流程，解决机器人在任务执行过程中无法响应新指令的问题。

Authors: Zhenyang Chen, Alan Tian, Liquan Wang, Benjamin Joffe, Yingyan Celine Lin, Yuxiao Chen, Siddharth Karamcheti, Danfei Xu

Shielded Reinforcement Learning Under Dynamic Temporal Logic Constraints

Abstract (English): Reinforcement Learning (RL) has shown promise in various robotics applications, yet its deployment on real systems is still limited due to safety and operational constraints. The safe RL field has gained considerable attention in recent years, which focuses on imposing safety constraints throughout the learning process. However, real systems often require more complex constraints than just safety, such as periodic recharging or time-bounded visits to specific regions. Imposing such spatio-temporal tasks during learning still remains a challenge. Signal Temporal Logic (STL) is a formal language for specifying temporal properties of real-valued signals and provides a way to express such complex tasks. In this paper, we propose a framework that leverages sequential control barrier functions and model-free RL to ensure that the given STL tasks are satisfied throughout the learning process. Our method extends beyond traditional safety constraints by enforcing rich STL specifications, which can involve visits to dynamic targets with unknown trajectories. We also demonstrate the effectiveness of our framework through various simulations.

摘要（中文）: 摘要： 强化学习(RL)在各种机器人应用中展现了潜力，但由于安全和操作约束，其在实际系统上的部署仍然有限。近年来，安全强化学习领域受到了广泛关注，该领域专注于在整个学习过程中施加安全约束。然而，实际系统通常需要比安全更复杂的约束，例如周期性充电或在有时间限制内访问特定区域。在学习过程中施加此类时空任务仍然是一个挑战。信号时序逻辑(STL)是一种用于指定实值信号时序属性的形式化语言，并提供了一种表达此类复杂任务的方法。在本文中，我们提出了一种框架，该框架利用序列控制障碍函数和免模型强化学习来确保在整个学习过程中满足给定的STL任务。我们的方法超越了传统的安全约束，通过强制执行丰富的STL规范，可以实现对具有未知轨迹的动态目标的访问。我们通过各种仿真也证明了我们框架的有效性。

TLDR: This paper presents a shielded reinforcement learning framework using sequential control barrier functions and model-free RL for satisfying Signal Temporal Logic (STL) constraints, enabling the handling of complex spatio-temporal tasks in robotics, including dynamic targets.

简要说明: 本文提出了一种屏蔽强化学习框架，该框架使用顺序控制屏障函数和无模型强化学习来满足信号时序逻辑（STL）约束，从而能够在机器人技术中处理复杂的时空任务，包括动态目标。

Authors: Sadık Bera Yüksel, Ali Tevfik Buyukkocak, Derya Aksaray

SLowRL: Safe Low-Rank Adaptation Reinforcement Learning for Locomotion

Abstract (English): Sim-to-real transfer of locomotion policies often leads to performance degradation due to the inevitable sim-to-real gap. Naively fine-tuning these policies directly on hardware is problematic, as it poses risks of mechanical failure and suffers from high sample inefficiency. In this paper, we address the challenge of safely and efficiently fine-tuning reinforcement learning (RL) policies for dynamic locomotion tasks. Specifically, we focus on fine-tuning policies learned in simulation directly on hardware, while explicitly enforcing safety constraints. In doing so, we introduce SLowRL, a framework that combines Low-Rank Adaptation (LoRA) with training-time safety enforcement via a recovery policy. We evaluate our method both in simulation and on a real Unitree Go2 quadruped robot for jump and trot tasks. Experimental results show that our method achieves a $46.5\%$ reduction in fine-tuning time and near-zero safety violations compared to standard proximal policy optimization (PPO) baselines. Notably, we find that a rank-1 adaptation alone is sufficient to recover pre-trained performance in the real world, while maintaining stable and safe real-world fine-tuning. These results demonstrate the practicality of safe, efficient fine-tuning for dynamic real-world robotic applications.

摘要（中文）: 动态步态策略的“仿真到真实”迁移常常因不可避免的“仿真到真实”差距而导致性能下降。直接在硬件上粗糙地微调这些策略存在问题，因为它会带来机械故障的风险，并遭受样本效率低下的困扰。在本文中，我们旨在解决安全高效地微调用于动态步态任务的强化学习（RL）策略的挑战。具体而言，我们专注于直接在硬件上微调在仿真中学习到的策略，同时显式地执行安全约束。为此，我们引入了SLowRL，一个结合低秩适配（LoRA）和通过恢复策略进行训练时安全执行的框架。我们在仿真和真实的宇树Go2四足机器人上，针对跳跃和跑步任务评估了我们的方法。实验结果表明，与标准近端策略优化（PPO）基线相比，我们的方法在微调时间上减少了46.5%，并实现了近零的安全违规。值得注意的是，我们发现仅使用秩为1的适配就足以恢复在真实世界中的预训练性能，同时保持稳定和安全的真实世界微调。这些结果证明了对动态真实世界机器人应用进行安全、高效微调的实用性。

TLDR: The paper introduces SLowRL, a method for safe and efficient fine-tuning of locomotion policies learned in simulation on real-world robots using Low-Rank Adaptation (LoRA) and a recovery policy, demonstrating significant improvements in fine-tuning time and safety on a Unitree Go2 robot.

简要说明: 该论文介绍了SLowRL，一种使用低秩适应（LoRA）和恢复策略，在真实机器人上安全有效地微调仿真中学习的运动策略的方法，并在Unitree Go2机器人上展示了微调时间和安全性方面的显著改进。

Authors: Elham Daneshmand, Shafeef Omar, Glen Berseth, Majid Khadiv, Hsiu-Chin Lin

Efficient and Reliable Teleoperation through Real-to-Sim-to-Real Shared Autonomy

Abstract (English): Fine-grained, contact-rich teleoperation remains slow, error-prone, and unreliable in real-world manipulation tasks, even for experienced operators. Shared autonomy offers a promising way to improve performance by combining human intent with automated assistance, but learning effective assistance in simulation requires a faithful model of human behavior, which is difficult to obtain in practice. We propose a real-to-sim-to-real shared autonomy framework that augments human teleoperation with learned corrective behaviors, using a simple yet effective k-nearest-neighbor (kNN) human surrogate to model operator actions in simulation. The surrogate is fit from less than five minutes of real-world teleoperation data and enables stable training of a residual copilot policy with model-free reinforcement learning. The resulting copilot is deployed to assist human operators in real-world fine-grained manipulation tasks. Through simulation experiments and a user study with sixteen participants on industry-relevant tasks, including nut threading, gear meshing, and peg insertion, we show that our system improves task success for novice operators and execution efficiency for experienced operators compared to direct teleoperation and shared-autonomy baselines that rely on expert priors or behavioral-cloning pilots. In addition, copilot-assisted teleoperation produces higher-quality demonstrations for downstream imitation learning.

摘要（中文）: 精细化、接触丰富的远程操作在现实世界操作任务中仍然缓慢、容易出错且不可靠，即使对于经验丰富的操作员也是如此。共享自主提供了一种通过结合人类意图与自动化辅助来提高性能的有前景的方法，但在模拟中学习有效的辅助需要一个忠实的人类行为模型，这在实践中难以获得。我们提出了一种实到模到实的共享自主框架，该框架通过学习到的纠正行为来增强人类远程操作，并使用简单而有效的k近邻（kNN）人类代理来建模模拟中的操作员动作。该代理由不到五分钟的真实世界远程操作数据拟合而成，并能够使用无模型强化学习稳定地训练残差副驾驶策略。生成的副驾驶部署用于辅助人类操作员执行现实世界中的精细化操作任务。通过模拟实验和一项包含十六名参与者针对行业相关任务（包括螺母穿线、齿轮啮合和插销插入）的用户研究，我们表明，与直接远程操作和依赖专家先验或行为克隆驾驶员的共享自主的基线方法相比，我们的系统提高了新手操作员的任务成功率和经验丰富的操作员的执行效率。此外，副驾驶辅助的远程操作为下游模仿学习产生了更高质量的演示。

TLDR: This paper presents a real-to-sim-to-real shared autonomy framework for improving teleoperation performance by learning corrective behaviors in simulation using a kNN-based human surrogate, demonstrating improved task success and efficiency in real-world manipulation tasks.

简要说明: 本文提出了一种实物到仿真到实物的共享自主框架，通过使用基于k近邻的人类代理在仿真中学习纠正行为，从而提高遥操作性能，并在实际操作任务中展示了更高的任务成功率和效率。

Authors: Shuo Sha, Yixuan Wang, Binghao Huang, Antonio Loquerico, Yunzhu Li

Loc3R-VLM: Language-based Localization and 3D Reasoning with Vision-Language Models

Abstract (English): Multimodal Large Language Models (MLLMs) have made impressive progress in connecting vision and language, but they still struggle with spatial understanding and viewpoint-aware reasoning. Recent efforts aim to augment the input representations with geometric cues rather than explicitly teaching models to reason in 3D space. We introduce Loc3R-VLM, a framework that equips 2D Vision-Language Models with advanced 3D understanding capabilities from monocular video input. Inspired by human spatial cognition, Loc3R-VLM relies on two joint objectives: global layout reconstruction to build a holistic representation of the scene structure, and explicit situation modeling to anchor egocentric perspective. These objectives provide direct spatial supervision that grounds both perception and language in a 3D context. To ensure geometric consistency and metric-scale alignment, we leverage lightweight camera pose priors extracted from a pre-trained 3D foundation model. Loc3R-VLM achieves state-of-the-art performance in language-based localization and outperforms existing 2D- and video-based approaches on situated and general 3D question-answering benchmarks, demonstrating that our spatial supervision framework enables strong 3D understanding. Project page: https://kevinqu7.github.io/loc3r-vlm

摘要（中文）: 多模态大型语言模型（MLLM）在连接视觉和语言方面取得了令人瞩目的进展，但它们仍然难以进行空间理解和视角感知的推理。最近的研究旨在通过几何线索来增强输入表示，而不是显式地教导模型在 3D 空间中进行推理。我们引入了 Loc3R-VLM，一个框架，它使 2D 视觉-语言模型具备了从单目视频输入获得的高级 3D 理解能力。受到人类空间认知的启发，Loc3R-VLM 依赖于两个联合目标：全局布局重建，以构建场景结构的整体表示；以及显式情境建模，以锚定以自我为中心的视角。这些目标提供了直接的空间监督，将感知和语言都扎根于 3D 环境中。为了确保几何一致性和度量尺度对齐，我们利用了从预训练的 3D 基础模型中提取的轻量级相机姿态先验。Loc3R-VLM 在基于语言的定位方面实现了最先进的性能，并在情境化和通用 3D 问答基准测试中优于现有的基于 2D 和视频的方法，表明我们的空间监督框架能够实现强大的 3D 理解能力。项目主页：https://kevinqu7.github.io/loc3r-vlm

TLDR: Loc3R-VLM enhances 2D Vision-Language Models with 3D understanding by incorporating global layout reconstruction and situation modeling with camera pose priors, achieving state-of-the-art results in language-based localization and 3D question answering.

Authors: Kevin Qu, Haozhe Qi, Mihai Dusmanu, Mahdi Rad, Rui Wang, Marc Pollefeys

AgentFactory: A Self-Evolving Framework Through Executable Subagent Accumulation and Reuse

Abstract (English): Building LLM-based agents has become increasingly important. Recent works on LLM-based agent self-evolution primarily record successful experiences as textual prompts or reflections, which cannot reliably guarantee efficient task re-execution in complex scenarios. We propose AgentFactory, a new self-evolution paradigm that preserves successful task solutions as executable subagent code rather than textual experience. Crucially, these subagents are continuously refined based on execution feedback, becoming increasingly robust and efficient as more tasks are encountered. Saved subagents are pure Python code with standardized documentation, enabling portability across any Python-capable system. We demonstrate that AgentFactory enables continuous capability accumulation: its library of executable subagents grows and improves over time, progressively reducing the effort required for similar tasks without manual intervention. Our implementation is open-sourced at https://github.com/zzatpku/AgentFactory, and our demonstration video is available at https://youtu.be/iKSsuAXJHW0.

摘要（中文）: 构建基于大型语言模型（LLM）的智能体变得日益重要。近期关于基于LLM智能体自我进化的工作主要将成功经验记录为文本提示或反思，这无法在复杂场景中可靠地保证高效的任务复现。我们提出了AgentFactory，一种新的自我进化范式，它将成功的任务解决方案保存为可执行的子智能体代码，而非文本经验。至关重要的是，这些子智能体基于执行反馈不断细化，随着遇到更多任务而变得越来越稳健和高效。保存的子智能体是具有标准化文档的纯Python代码，能够在任何支持Python的系统上实现可移植性。我们证明AgentFactory能够实现持续的能力积累：其可执行子智能体库随着时间的推移不断增长和改进，逐步减少类似任务所需的工作量，而无需人工干预。我们的实现已在https://github.com/zzatpku/AgentFactory开源，演示视频可在https://youtu.be/iKSsuAXJHW0观看。

TLDR: AgentFactory proposes a self-evolving agent framework that accumulates and reuses successful task solutions as executable Python subagents, improving efficiency and robustness over time through execution feedback.

简要说明: AgentFactory 提出了一个自进化代理框架，它将成功的任务解决方案积累并重用为可执行的 Python 子代理，通过执行反馈来提高效率和稳健性。

Authors: Zhang Zhang, Shuqi Lu, Hongjin Qian, Di He, Zheng Liu

VideoAtlas: Navigating Long-Form Video in Logarithmic Compute

Abstract (English): Extending language models to video introduces two challenges: representation, where existing methods rely on lossy approximations, and long-context, where caption- or agent-based pipelines collapse video into text and lose visual fidelity. To overcome this, we introduce \textbf{VideoAtlas}, a task-agnostic environment to represent video as a hierarchical grid that is simultaneously lossless, navigable, scalable, caption- and preprocessing-free. An overview of the video is available at a glance, and any region can be recursively zoomed into, with the same visual representation used uniformly for the video, intermediate investigations, and the agent's memory, eliminating lossy text conversion end-to-end. This hierarchical structure ensures access depth grows only logarithmically with video length. For long-context, Recursive Language Models (RLMs) recently offered a powerful solution for long text, but extending them to visual domain requires a structured environment to recurse into, which \textbf{VideoAtlas} provides. \textbf{VideoAtlas} as a Markov Decision Process unlocks Video-RLM: a parallel Master-Worker architecture where a Master coordinates global exploration while Workers concurrently drill into assigned regions to accumulate lossless visual evidence. We demonstrate three key findings: (1)~logarithmic compute growth with video duration, further amplified by a 30-60\% multimodal cache hit rate arising from the grid's structural reuse. (2)~environment budgeting, where bounding the maximum exploration depth provides a principled compute-accuracy hyperparameter. (3)~emergent adaptive compute allocation that scales with question granularity. When scaling from 1-hour to 10-hour benchmarks, Video-RLM remains the most duration-robust method with minimal accuracy degradation, demonstrating that structured environment navigation is a viable and scalable paradigm for video understanding.

摘要（中文）: 将语言模型扩展到视频领域面临两个挑战：表示，现有方法依赖于有损近似；以及长上下文，基于字幕或代理的流水线将视频压缩成文本，并丢失视觉保真度。为了克服这些问题，我们引入了 \textbf{VideoAtlas}，一个任务无关的环境，用于将视频表示为分层网格，该网格同时具有无损、可导航、可扩展、无需字幕和预处理的特性。视频概览一目了然，任何区域都可以递归放大，视频、中间调查和代理的记忆都使用统一的视觉表示，从而消除了端到端的有损文本转换。这种分层结构确保了访问深度仅随视频长度呈对数增长。对于长上下文，递归语言模型 (RLM) 最近为长文本提供了一个强大的解决方案，但将它们扩展到视觉领域需要一个结构化的环境来进行递归，而 \textbf{VideoAtlas} 提供了这一点。\textbf{VideoAtlas} 作为马尔可夫决策过程解锁了 Video-RLM：一种并行的主-从架构，其中主节点协调全局探索，而从节点并发地深入到分配的区域以积累无损的视觉证据。我们展示了三个关键发现：(1) 计算量随视频时长呈对数增长，并且由于网格的结构复用，多模态缓存命中率提高了 30-60\%，从而进一步放大。(2) 环境预算，其中限制最大探索深度提供了一个原则性的计算-精度超参数。(3) 涌现的自适应计算分配，其规模与问题粒度成正比。当从 1 小时扩展到 10 小时的基准测试时，Video-RLM 仍然是最具持续时间鲁棒性的方法，精度下降最小，这表明结构化环境导航是视频理解的一种可行且可扩展的范例。

TLDR: VideoAtlas introduces a hierarchical grid-based representation for long-form video, enabling logarithmic compute scaling for video understanding tasks by integrating with Recursive Language Models in a novel Master-Worker architecture. This allows improved duration robustness when scaling to longer videos.

简要说明: VideoAtlas 引入了一种分层网格的视频表示方法，通过与递归语言模型集成在一个新颖的 Master-Worker 架构中，实现了长视频理解任务的对数计算扩展。这提高了扩展到更长视频时的持续时间鲁棒性。

Authors: Mohamed Eltahir, Ali Habibullah, Yazan Alshoibi, Lama Ayash, Tanveer Hussain, Naeemullah Khan

Insight-V++: Towards Advanced Long-Chain Visual Reasoning with Multimodal Large Language Models

Abstract (English): Large Language Models (LLMs) have achieved remarkable reliability and advanced capabilities through extended test-time reasoning. However, extending these capabilities to Multi-modal Large Language Models (MLLMs) remains a significant challenge due to a critical scarcity of high-quality, long-chain reasoning data and optimized training pipelines. To bridge this gap, we present a unified multi-agent visual reasoning framework that systematically evolves from our foundational image-centric model, Insight-V, into a generalized spatial-temporal architecture, Insight-V++. We first propose a scalable data generation pipeline equipped with multi-granularity assessment that autonomously synthesizes structured, complex reasoning trajectories across image and video domains without human intervention. Recognizing that directly supervising MLLMs with such intricate data yields sub-optimal results, we design a dual-agent architecture comprising a reasoning agent to execute extensive analytical chains, and a summary agent to critically evaluate and distill final outcomes. While our initial framework utilized Direct Preference Optimization (DPO), its off-policy nature fundamentally constrained reinforcement learning potential. To overcome these limitations, particularly for long-horizon video understanding, Insight-V++ introduces two novel algorithms, ST-GRPO and J-GRPO, which enhance spatial-temporal reasoning and improve evaluative robustness. Crucially, by leveraging reliable feedback from the summary agent, we guide an iterative reasoning path generation process, retraining the entire multi-agent system in a continuous, self-improving loop. Extensive experiments on base models like LLaVA-NeXT and Qwen2.5-VL demonstrate significant performance gains across challenging image and video reasoning benchmarks while preserving strong capabilities on traditional perception-focused tasks.

摘要（中文）: 大型语言模型（LLM）通过扩展的测试时推理，实现了卓越的可靠性和先进能力。然而，由于高质量、长链推理数据和优化训练流程的严重匮乏，将这些能力扩展到多模态大型语言模型（MLLM）仍然是一个重大挑战。为了弥合这一差距，我们提出了一个统一的多Agent视觉推理框架，该框架系统地从我们以图像为中心的基础模型Insight-V演进为广义的时空架构Insight-V++。我们首先提出了一个可扩展的数据生成流程，该流程配备了多粒度评估，可以自主合成图像和视频领域中结构化的复杂推理轨迹，无需人工干预。考虑到使用如此复杂的数据直接监督MLLM会产生次优结果，我们设计了一个双Agent架构，包括一个推理Agent来执行广泛的分析链，以及一个摘要Agent来批判性地评估和提炼最终结果。虽然我们最初的框架使用了直接偏好优化（DPO），但其离策略性质从根本上限制了强化学习的潜力。为了克服这些局限性，特别是对于长时程视频理解，Insight-V++引入了两种新颖的算法，ST-GRPO和J-GRPO，它们增强了时空推理并提高了评估的鲁棒性。至关重要的是，通过利用来自摘要Agent的可靠反馈，我们引导迭代的推理路径生成过程，在一个连续的、自我改进的循环中重新训练整个多Agent系统。基于诸如LLaVA-NeXT和Qwen2.5-VL等基础模型的大量实验表明，在具有挑战性的图像和视频推理基准测试中，性能得到了显著提高，同时保持了在传统感知类任务上的强大能力。

TLDR: The paper introduces Insight-V++, a multi-agent visual reasoning framework for MLLMs that uses a novel data generation pipeline and reinforcement learning algorithms ST-GRPO and J-GRPO to improve long-chain visual reasoning in images and videos.

简要说明: 本文介绍了一个名为Insight-V++的多智能体视觉推理框架，该框架用于多模态大型语言模型（MLLM），它使用了一种新的数据生成流程和强化学习算法ST-GRPO和J-GRPO，以提高图像和视频中的长链视觉推理能力。

Authors: Yuhao Dong, Zuyan Liu, Shulin Tian, Yongming Rao, Ziwei Liu

RPMS: Enhancing LLM-Based Embodied Planning through Rule-Augmented Memory Synergy

Abstract (English): LLM agents often fail in closed-world embodied environments because actions must satisfy strict preconditions -- such as location, inventory, and container states -- and failure feedback is sparse. We identify two structurally coupled failure modes: (P1) invalid action generation and (P2) state drift, each amplifying the other in a degenerative cycle. We present RPMS, a conflict-managed architecture that enforces action feasibility via structured rule retrieval, gates memory applicability via a lightweight belief state, and resolves conflicts between the two sources via rules-first arbitration. On ALFWorld (134 unseen tasks), RPMS achieves 59.7% single-trial success with Llama 3.1 8B (+23.9 pp over baseline) and 98.5% with Claude Sonnet 4.5 (+11.9 pp); of the 8B gain, rule retrieval alone contributes +14.9 pp (statistically significant), making it the dominant factor. A key finding is that episodic memory is conditionally useful: it harms performance on some task types when used without grounding, but becomes a stable net positive once filtered by current state and constrained by explicit action rules. Adapting RPMS to ScienceWorld with GPT-4 yields consistent gains across all ablation conditions (avg. score 54.0 vs. 44.9 for the ReAct baseline), providing transfer evidence that the core mechanisms hold across structurally distinct environments.

摘要（中文）: 大型语言模型智能体在封闭世界的具身环境中常常失败，因为动作必须满足严格的先决条件（如位置、库存和容器状态），且失败反馈稀疏。我们识别出两种结构性耦合的失败模式：（P1）无效动作生成和（P2）状态漂移，它们在退化循环中相互放大。我们提出了 RPMS，一种冲突管理架构，它通过结构化的规则检索来强制执行动作可行性，通过轻量级的信念状态来控制记忆的适用性，并通过以规则优先的仲裁来解决这两种来源之间的冲突。在 ALFWorld 上（134 个未见过的任务），RPMS 使用 Llama 3.1 8B 实现了 59.7% 的单次尝试成功率（相较于基线提升 +23.9 个百分点），使用 Claude Sonnet 4.5 达到了 98.5%（+11.9 个百分点）；在 8B 模型的增益中，仅规则检索就贡献了 +14.9 个百分点（具有统计显著性），使其成为主要因素。一个关键的发现是情景记忆是有条件有用的：在没有依据的情况下使用时，它会损害某些任务类型的性能，但一旦通过当前状态进行过滤并受到显式动作规则的约束，它就会成为稳定的净收益。将 RPMS 适配到 ScienceWorld 并使用 GPT-4，在所有消融条件下都产生了持续的收益（平均得分 54.0，而 ReAct 基线为 44.9），提供了迁移证据，表明其核心机制在结构不同的环境中都有效。

TLDR: The paper introduces RPMS, a rule-augmented memory synergy architecture that enhances LLM-based embodied planning by addressing invalid action generation and state drift through rule retrieval and belief state filtering, showing significant performance gains on ALFWorld and ScienceWorld.

简要说明: 该论文介绍了RPMS，一种规则增强的记忆协同架构，通过规则检索和信念状态过滤来解决LLM在具身规划中遇到的无效动作生成和状态漂移问题，并在ALFWorld和ScienceWorld上取得了显著的性能提升。

Authors: Zhenhang Yuan, Shenghai Yuan, Lihua Xie

CoVerRL: Breaking the Consensus Trap in Label-Free Reasoning via Generator-Verifier Co-Evolution

Abstract (English): Label-free reinforcement learning enables large language models to improve reasoning capabilities without ground-truth supervision, typically by treating majority-voted answers as pseudo-labels. However, we identify a critical failure mode: as training maximizes self-consistency, output diversity collapses, causing the model to confidently reinforce systematic errors that evade detection. We term this the consensus trap. To escape it, we propose CoVerRL, a framework where a single model alternates between generator and verifier roles, with each capability bootstrapping the other. Majority voting provides noisy but informative supervision for training the verifier, while the improving verifier progressively filters self-consistent errors from pseudo-labels. This co-evolution creates a virtuous cycle that maintains high reward accuracy throughout training. Experiments across Qwen and Llama model families demonstrate that CoVerRL outperforms label-free baselines by 4.7-5.9\% on mathematical reasoning benchmarks. Moreover, self-verification accuracy improves from around 55\% to over 85\%, confirming that both capabilities genuinely co-evolve.

摘要（中文）: 无标签强化学习使大型语言模型能够在没有真实标签监督的情况下提高推理能力，通常将多数投票的答案作为伪标签。然而，我们发现了一个关键的失效模式：随着训练最大化自我一致性，输出的多样性会崩溃，导致模型自信地强化逃避检测的系统性错误。我们称之为共识陷阱。为了摆脱这个陷阱，我们提出了CoVerRL，一个框架，其中单个模型在生成器和验证器的角色之间交替，每一种能力都引导另一种能力。多数投票为训练验证器提供了噪声但信息丰富的监督，而不断改进的验证器逐步过滤掉伪标签中的自我一致性错误。这种共同进化创造了一个良性循环，在整个训练过程中保持较高的奖励准确率。在Qwen和Llama模型系列上的实验表明，CoVerRL在数学推理基准测试中优于无标签基线 4.7-5.9\%。此外，自我验证的准确率从大约 55\% 提高到 85\% 以上，证实了这两种能力确实实现了共同进化。

TLDR: The paper introduces CoVerRL, a label-free reinforcement learning framework for LLMs that breaks the 'consensus trap' by co-evolving a generator and verifier, improving reasoning capabilities and self-verification accuracy.

简要说明: 该论文介绍了一个名为CoVerRL的无标签强化学习框架，通过共同进化生成器和验证器来打破LLM中的“共识陷阱”，从而提高推理能力和自我验证准确性。

Authors: Teng Pan, Yuchen Yan, Zixuan Wang, Ruiqing Zhang, Gaiyang Han, Wanqi Zhang, Weiming Lu, Jun Xiao, Yongliang Shen

From Virtual Environments to Real-World Trials: Emerging Trends in Autonomous Driving

Abstract (English): Autonomous driving technologies have achieved significant advances in recent years, yet their real-world deployment remains constrained by data scarcity, safety requirements, and the need for generalization across diverse environments. In response, synthetic data and virtual environments have emerged as powerful enablers, offering scalable, controllable, and richly annotated scenarios for training and evaluation. This survey presents a comprehensive review of recent developments at the intersection of autonomous driving, simulation technologies, and synthetic datasets. We organize the landscape across three core dimensions: (i) the use of synthetic data for perception and planning, (ii) digital twin-based simulation for system validation, and (iii) domain adaptation strategies bridging synthetic and real-world data. We also highlight the role of vision-language models and simulation realism in enhancing scene understanding and generalization. A detailed taxonomy of datasets, tools, and simulation platforms is provided, alongside an analysis of trends in benchmark design. Finally, we discuss critical challenges and open research directions, including Sim2Real transfer, scalable safety validation, cooperative autonomy, and simulation-driven policy learning, that must be addressed to accelerate the path toward safe, generalizable, and globally deployable autonomous driving systems.

摘要（中文）: 近年来，自动驾驶技术取得了显著进展，但其实际应用仍受到数据稀缺、安全要求以及在各种环境中泛化需求的限制。为此，合成数据和虚拟环境已成为强大的推动因素，为训练和评估提供可扩展、可控且富含标注的场景。本文对自动驾驶、仿真技术和合成数据集交叉领域的最新进展进行了全面综述。我们将该领域划分为三个核心维度：（i）合成数据在感知和规划中的应用，（ii）基于数字孪生的系统验证仿真，以及（iii）桥接合成数据和真实世界数据的领域自适应策略。我们还重点强调了视觉-语言模型和仿真真实性在增强场景理解和泛化能力方面的作用。本文提供了数据集、工具和仿真平台的详细分类，并分析了基准设计的发展趋势。最后，我们讨论了关键的挑战和开放的研究方向，包括Sim2Real迁移、可扩展的安全验证、协同自动驾驶以及仿真驱动的策略学习，这些问题有待解决，从而加速实现安全、通用且可在全球部署的自动驾驶系统。

TLDR: This survey paper reviews the use of synthetic data and virtual environments in autonomous driving, focusing on perception, planning, validation, and domain adaptation, while also highlighting the role of vision-language models and future challenges.

Authors: A. Humnabadkar, A. Sikdar, B. Cave, H. Zhang, N. Bessis, A. Behera

Sensi: Learn One Thing at a Time -- Curriculum-Based Test-Time Learning for LLM Game Agents

Abstract (English): Large language model (LLM) agents deployed in unknown environments must learn task structure at test time, but current approaches require thousands of interactions to form useful hypotheses. We present Sensi, an LLM agent architecture for the ARC-AGI-3 game-playing challenge that introduces structured test-time learning through three mechanisms: (1) a two-player architecture separating perception from action, (2) a curriculum-based learning system managed by an external state machine, and (3) a database-as-control-plane that makes the agents context window programmatically steerable. We further introduce an LLM-as-judge component with dynamically generated evaluation rubrics to determine when the agent has learned enough about one topic to advance to the next. We report results across two iterations: Sensi v1 solves 2 game levels using the two-player architecture alone, while Sensi v2 adds curriculum learning and solves 0 levels - but completes its entire learning curriculum in approximately 32 action attempts, achieving 50-94x greater sample efficiency than comparable systems that require 1600-3000 attempts. We precisely diagnose the failure mode as a self-consistent hallucination cascade originating in the perception layer, demonstrating that the architectural bottleneck has shifted from learning efficiency to perceptual grounding - a more tractable problem.

摘要（中文）: 部署在未知环境中的大型语言模型（LLM）智能体必须在测试时学习任务结构，但当前方法需要数千次交互才能形成有效的假设。我们提出了 Sensi，一种用于 ARC-AGI-3 游戏挑战的 LLM 智能体架构，它通过三种机制引入结构化的测试时学习：（1）一个将感知和行动分离的双玩家架构，（2）一个由外部状态机管理的基于课程的学习系统，以及（3）一个将智能体上下文窗口进行编程控制的数据库作为控制平面。我们进一步引入了一个 LLM 作为评判组件，利用动态生成的评估准则来确定智能体在某个主题上学习了足够的知识以进入下一个主题。我们报告了两次迭代的结果：Sensi v1 仅使用双玩家架构解决了 2 个游戏关卡，而 Sensi v2 添加了课程学习，解决了 0 个关卡——但仅用约 32 次行动尝试就完成了整个学习课程，实现了比需要 1600-3000 次尝试的同类系统高出 50-94 倍的样本效率。我们精确地诊断了失败模式为源于感知层的一致性幻觉级联，表明架构瓶颈已从学习效率转移到感知接地——一个更易于解决的问题。

TLDR: The paper introduces Sensi, an LLM agent architecture with curriculum-based test-time learning for the ARC-AGI-3 challenge, achieving significantly improved sample efficiency despite a perceptual grounding bottleneck. It uses a two-player architecture, a curriculum managed by a state machine, and a database-as-control-plane.

简要说明: 该论文介绍了 Sensi，一种基于课程的测试时学习的 LLM 智能体架构，用于 ARC-AGI-3 挑战赛。虽然存在感知基础瓶颈，但它在样本效率方面取得了显著提升。它采用双人架构、由状态机管理的课程以及数据库即控制平面。
