Authors: Mohsen Arjmandi

VeriGrey: Greybox Agent Validation

Abstract (English): Agentic AI has been a topic of great interest recently. A Large Language Model (LLM) agent involves one or more LLMs in the back-end. In the front end, it conducts autonomous decision-making by combining the LLM outputs with results obtained by invoking several external tools. The autonomous interactions with the external environment introduce critical security risks. In this paper, we present a grey-box approach to explore diverse behaviors and uncover security risks in LLM agents. Our approach VeriGrey uses the sequence of tools invoked as a feedback function to drive the testing process. This helps uncover infrequent but dangerous tool invocations that cause unexpected agent behavior. As mutation operators in the testing process, we mutate prompts to design pernicious injection prompts. This is carefully accomplished by linking the task of the agent to an injection task, so that the injection task becomes a necessary step of completing the agent functionality. Comparing our approach with a black-box baseline on the well-known AgentDojo benchmark, VeriGrey achieves 33% additional efficacy in finding indirect prompt injection vulnerabilities with a GPT-4.1 back-end. We also conduct real-world case studies with the widely used coding agent Gemini CLI, and the well-known OpenClaw personal assistant. VeriGrey finds prompts inducing several attack scenarios that could not be identified by black-box approaches. In OpenClaw, by constructing a conversation agent which employs mutational fuzz testing as needed, VeriGrey is able to discover malicious skill variants from 10 malicious skills (with 10/10= 100% success rate on the Kimi-K2.5 LLM backend, and 9/10= 90% success rate on Opus 4.6 LLM backend). This demonstrates the value of a dynamic approach like VeriGrey to test agents, and to eventually lead to an agent assurance framework.

摘要（中文）: 智能体AI近来备受关注。大型语言模型（LLM）智能体在后端涉及一个或多个LLM。在前端，它通过将LLM输出与调用若干外部工具所获得的结果相结合，进行自主决策。与外部环境的自主交互引入了关键的安全风险。 在本文中，我们提出了一种灰盒方法来探索LLM智能体的多样化行为并揭示安全风险。我们的方法VeriGrey使用调用的工具序列作为反馈函数来驱动测试过程。这有助于发现不常见但危险的工具调用，这些调用会导致意想不到的智能体行为。作为测试过程中的变异算子，我们对提示语进行变异，以设计有害的注入提示语。这是通过将智能体的任务与注入任务联系起来来精心完成的，使得注入任务成为完成智能体功能的必要步骤。在著名的AgentDojo基准测试中，与黑盒基线相比，VeriGrey在使用GPT-4.1后端时，在发现间接提示注入漏洞方面的有效性提高了33%。 我们还对广泛使用的编码智能体Gemini CLI和著名的个人助理OpenClaw进行了真实世界的案例研究。VeriGrey发现了引发几种攻击场景的提示语，而这些场景无法通过黑盒方法识别。在OpenClaw中，通过构建一个根据需要采用变异模糊测试的对话智能体，VeriGrey能够从10个恶意技能中发现恶意技能变体（在使用Kimi-K2.5 LLM后端时，成功率为10/10=100%；在使用Opus 4.6 LLM后端时，成功率为9/10=90%）。这证明了像VeriGrey这样的动态方法在测试智能体方面的价值，并最终促成智能体保障框架的建立。

TLDR: The paper introduces VeriGrey, a grey-box testing approach that uses tool invocation sequences and prompt mutation to uncover security vulnerabilities in LLM agents, demonstrating improved efficacy over black-box methods on benchmarks and real-world agents.

简要说明: 本文介绍了一种名为VeriGrey的灰盒测试方法，该方法使用工具调用序列和提示突变来发现LLM Agent中的安全漏洞，并在基准测试和实际Agent上展示了优于黑盒方法的有效性。

Authors: Yuntong Zhang, Sungmin Kang, Ruijie Meng, Marcel Böhme, Abhik Roychoudhury

Benchmarking Reinforcement Learning via Stochastic Converse Optimality: Generating Systems with Known Optimal Policies

Abstract (English): The objective comparison of Reinforcement Learning (RL) algorithms is notoriously complex as outcomes and benchmarking of performances of different RL approaches are critically sensitive to environmental design, reward structures, and stochasticity inherent in both algorithmic learning and environmental dynamics. To manage this complexity, we introduce a rigorous benchmarking framework by extending converse optimality to discrete-time, control-affine, nonlinear systems with noise. Our framework provides necessary and sufficient conditions, under which a prescribed value function and policy are optimal for constructed systems, enabling the systematic generation of benchmark families via homotopy variations and randomized parameters. We validate it by automatically constructing diverse environments, demonstrating our framework's capacity for a controlled and comprehensive evaluation across algorithms. By assessing standard methods against a ground-truth optimum, our work delivers a reproducible foundation for precise and rigorous RL benchmarking.

摘要（中文）: 强化学习（RL）算法的客观比较是出了名的复杂，因为不同RL方法的成果和性能基准对环境设计、奖励结构以及算法学习和环境动力学中固有的随机性都非常敏感。为了应对这种复杂性，我们引入了一个严谨的基准测试框架，通过将逆最优性扩展到具有噪声的离散时间、控制仿射、非线性系统。我们的框架提供了必要且充分的条件，在该条件下，规定的价值函数和策略对于构建的系统是最优的，从而能够通过同伦变分和随机参数系统地生成基准测试系列。我们通过自动构建多样化的环境来验证它，展示了我们的框架在跨算法的受控和全面评估方面的能力。通过针对真值最优解评估标准方法，我们的工作为精确而严谨的RL基准测试提供了一个可复现的基础。

TLDR: This paper introduces a framework for generating reinforcement learning benchmarks with known optimal policies, allowing for rigorous and reproducible evaluation of RL algorithms against ground-truth optima.

简要说明: 该论文介绍了一种生成具有已知最优策略的强化学习基准的框架，从而可以针对真实最优解对强化学习算法进行严格且可重复的评估。

Authors: Sinan Ibrahim, Grégoire Ouerdane, Hadi Salloum, Henni Ouerdane, Stefan Streif, Pavel Osinenko

Edit-As-Act: Goal-Regressive Planning for Open-Vocabulary 3D Indoor Scene Editing

Abstract (English): Editing a 3D indoor scene from natural language is conceptually straightforward but technically challenging. Existing open-vocabulary systems often regenerate large portions of a scene or rely on image-space edits that disrupt spatial structure, resulting in unintended global changes or physically inconsistent layouts. These limitations stem from treating editing primarily as a generative task. We take a different view. A user instruction defines a desired world state, and editing should be the minimal sequence of actions that makes this state true while preserving everything else. This perspective motivates Edit-As-Act, a framework that performs open-vocabulary scene editing as goal-regressive planning in 3D space. Given a source scene and free-form instruction, Edit-As-Act predicts symbolic goal predicates and plans in EditLang, a PDDL-inspired action language that we design with explicit preconditions and effects encoding support, contact, collision, and other geometric relations. A language-driven planner proposes actions, and a validator enforces goal-directedness, monotonicity, and physical feasibility, producing interpretable and physically coherent transformations. By separating reasoning from low-level generation, Edit-As-Act achieves instruction fidelity, semantic consistency, and physical plausibility - three criteria that existing paradigms cannot satisfy together. On E2A-Bench, our benchmark of 63 editing tasks across 9 indoor environments, Edit-As-Act significantly outperforms prior approaches across all edit types and scene categories.

摘要（中文）: 从自然语言编辑3D室内场景在概念上很简单，但在技术上具有挑战性。现有的开放词汇系统通常会重新生成场景的大部分，或者依赖于破坏空间结构的图像空间编辑，导致意外的全局变化或物理不一致的布局。这些局限性源于主要将编辑视为一个生成任务。我们采取不同的观点。用户指令定义了期望的世界状态，而编辑应该是使该状态为真的最小动作序列，同时保留其他一切。这种视角促使我们提出了Edit-As-Act，一个在3D空间中执行目标回溯式规划的开放词汇场景编辑框架。给定一个源场景和自由形式的指令，Edit-As-Act预测符号目标谓词，并在EditLang中进行规划，EditLang是一种受PDDL启发的动作语言，我们设计它时考虑了显式的前提条件和效果，编码了支持、接触、碰撞和其他几何关系。一个语言驱动的规划器提出动作，一个验证器强制执行目标导向性、单调性和物理可行性，从而产生可解释的和物理连贯的变换。通过将推理与低级生成分离，Edit-As-Act实现了指令保真度、语义一致性和物理合理性——现有范式无法同时满足这三个标准。 在E2A-Bench上，我们的基准测试包含跨越9个室内环境的63个编辑任务，Edit-As-Act在所有编辑类型和场景类别中都明显优于以往的方法。

TLDR: The paper introduces Edit-As-Act, a framework using goal-regressive planning in 3D space to edit indoor scenes based on natural language instructions, achieving improved instruction fidelity, semantic consistency, and physical plausibility compared to existing approaches.

简要说明: 该论文介绍了Edit-As-Act，一个使用3D空间中的目标回归计划来根据自然语言指令编辑室内场景的框架，与现有方法相比，实现了更好的指令保真度、语义一致性和物理合理性。

Authors: Seongrae Noh, SeungWon Seo, Gyeong-Moon Park, HyeongYeop Kang

UniSAFE: A Comprehensive Benchmark for Safety Evaluation of Unified Multimodal Models

Abstract (English): Unified Multimodal Models (UMMs) offer powerful cross-modality capabilities but introduce new safety risks not observed in single-task models. Despite their emergence, existing safety benchmarks remain fragmented across tasks and modalities, limiting the comprehensive evaluation of complex system-level vulnerabilities. To address this gap, we introduce UniSAFE, the first comprehensive benchmark for system-level safety evaluation of UMMs across 7 I/O modality combinations, spanning conventional tasks and novel multimodal-context image generation settings. UniSAFE is built with a shared-target design that projects common risk scenarios across task-specific I/O configurations, enabling controlled cross-task comparisons of safety failures. Comprising 6,802 curated instances, we use UniSAFE to evaluate 15 state-of-the-art UMMs, both proprietary and open-source. Our results reveal critical vulnerabilities across current UMMs, including elevated safety violations in multi-image composition and multi-turn settings, with image-output tasks consistently more vulnerable than text-output tasks. These findings highlight the need for stronger system-level safety alignment for UMMs. Our code and data are publicly available at https://github.com/segyulee/UniSAFE

摘要（中文）: 统一多模态模型（UMM）提供了强大的跨模态能力，但也引入了在单任务模型中未观察到的新安全风险。尽管它们正在兴起，但现有的安全基准仍然分散在任务和模态中，这限制了对复杂系统级漏洞的全面评估。为了解决这一差距，我们引入了UniSAFE，这是第一个针对UMM的系统级安全评估的综合基准，覆盖了7种I/O模态组合，涵盖了传统任务和新颖的多模态上下文图像生成设置。UniSAFE采用共享目标设计，将常见的风险场景投射到特定任务的I/O配置中，从而能够对安全故障进行可控的跨任务比较。UniSAFE包含6,802个精选实例，我们使用它来评估15个最先进的UMM，包括专有模型和开源模型。我们的结果揭示了当前UMM存在的关键漏洞，包括在多图像合成和多轮设置中更高的安全违规率，并且图像输出任务始终比文本输出任务更容易受到攻击。这些发现突出了对UMM进行更强大的系统级安全对齐的必要性。我们的代码和数据已在https://github.com/segyulee/UniSAFE上公开。

TLDR: The paper introduces UniSAFE, a comprehensive benchmark for evaluating safety vulnerabilities in Unified Multimodal Models (UMMs) across various modalities and tasks, revealing critical safety issues in existing models.

简要说明: 该论文介绍了UniSAFE，一个综合性的基准，用于评估统一多模态模型（UMMs）在各种模态和任务中的安全漏洞，揭示了现有模型中存在的严重安全问题。

Authors: Segyu Lee, Boryeong Cho, Hojung Jung, Seokhyun An, Juhyeong Kim, Jaehyun Kwak, Yongjin Yang, Sangwon Jang, Youngrok Park, Wonjun Chang, Se-Young Yun

SLEA-RL: Step-Level Experience Augmented Reinforcement Learning for Multi-Turn Agentic Training

Abstract (English): Large Language Model (LLM) agents have shown strong results on multi-turn tool-use tasks, yet they operate in isolation during training, failing to leverage experiences accumulated across episodes. Existing experience-augmented methods address this by organizing trajectories into retrievable libraries, but they retrieve experiences only once based on the initial task description and hold them constant throughout the episode. In multi-turn settings where observations change at every step, this static retrieval becomes increasingly mismatched as episodes progress. We propose SLEA-RL (Step-Level Experience-Augmented Reinforcement Learning), a framework that retrieves relevant experiences at each decision step conditioned on the current observation. SLEA-RL operates through three components: (i) step-level observation clustering that groups structurally equivalent environmental states for efficient cluster-indexed retrieval; (ii) a self-evolving experience library that distills successful strategies and failure patterns through score-based admission and rate-limited extraction; and (iii) policy optimization with step-level credit assignment for fine-grained advantage estimation across multi-turn episodes. The experience library evolves alongside the policy through semantic analysis rather than gradient updates. Experiments on long-horizon multi-turn agent benchmarks demonstrate that SLEA-RL achieves superior performance compared to various reinforcement learning baselines.

摘要（中文）: 大型语言模型（LLM）智能体在多轮工具使用任务中表现出强大的能力，但它们在训练过程中独立运行，无法利用跨回合积累的经验。现有的经验增强方法通过将轨迹组织成可检索的库来解决这个问题，但它们仅基于初始的任务描述检索一次经验，并在整个回合中保持不变。在多轮设置中，观察结果在每一步都会发生变化，这种静态检索会随着回合的进行而变得越来越不匹配。我们提出了SLEA-RL（步级经验增强强化学习），这是一个框架，它在每个决策步骤中，有条件地基于当前观察结果检索相关经验。SLEA-RL通过三个组件运行：（i）步级观察聚类，它对结构等效的环境状态进行分组，以实现高效的聚类索引检索；（ii）一个自我演化的经验库，它通过基于分数的准入和速率限制提取来提炼成功的策略和失败的模式；以及（iii）策略优化，具有步级信用分配，可在多轮回合中进行细粒度的优势估计。经验库通过语义分析而非梯度更新与策略同步演化。在长视野多轮智能体基准测试上的实验表明，与各种强化学习基线方法相比，SLEA-RL实现了卓越的性能。

TLDR: The paper introduces SLEA-RL, a reinforcement learning framework that retrieves relevant experiences at each decision step conditioned on the current observation for multi-turn agentic training, demonstrating superior performance on long-horizon tasks.

简要说明: 本文介绍了一种名为SLEA-RL的强化学习框架，该框架在多轮Agent训练中，根据当前观察检索每个决策步骤的相关经验，并在长时程任务中表现出卓越的性能。

Authors: Prince Zizhuang Wang, Shuli Jiang

Lightweight Adaptation for LLM-based Technical Service Agent: Latent Logic Augmentation and Robust Noise Reduction

Abstract (English): Adapting Large Language Models in complex technical service domains is constrained by the absence of explicit cognitive chains in human demonstrations and the inherent ambiguity arising from the diversity of valid responses. These limitations severely hinder agents from internalizing latent decision dynamics and generalizing effectively. Moreover, practical adaptation is often impeded by the prohibitive resource and time costs associated with standard training paradigms. To overcome these challenges and guarantee computational efficiency, we propose a lightweight adaptation framework comprising three key contributions. (1) Latent Logic Augmentation: We introduce Planning-Aware Trajectory Modeling and Decision Reasoning Augmentation to bridge the gap between surface-level supervision and latent decision logic. These approaches strengthen the stability of Supervised Fine-Tuning alignment. (2) Robust Noise Reduction: We construct a Multiple Ground Truths dataset through a dual-filtering method to reduce the noise by validating diverse responses, thereby capturing the semantic diversity. (3) Lightweight Adaptation: We design a Hybrid Reward mechanism that fuses an LLM-based judge with a lightweight relevance-based Reranker to distill high-fidelity reward signals while reducing the computational cost compared to standard LLM-as-a-Judge reinforcement learning. Empirical evaluations on real-world Cloud service tasks, conducted across semantically diverse settings, demonstrate that our framework achieves stability and performance gains through Latent Logic Augmentation and Robust Noise Reduction. Concurrently, our Hybrid Reward mechanism achieves alignment comparable to standard LLM-as-a-judge methods with reduced training time, underscoring the practical value for deploying technical service agents.

摘要（中文）: 在复杂技术服务领域中，由于人工演示缺乏明确的认知链，以及有效响应的多样性带来的固有模糊性，导致大型语言模型的适应受到限制。这些限制严重阻碍了智能体对潜在决策动态的内化和有效泛化。此外，实际适应常常因标准训练范式相关的高昂资源和时间成本而受阻。为了克服这些挑战并保证计算效率，我们提出了一个轻量级适应框架，包含三个关键贡献。(1) 潜在逻辑增强：我们引入了规划感知轨迹建模和决策推理增强，以弥合表面监督和潜在决策逻辑之间的差距。这些方法增强了监督式微调对齐的稳定性。(2) 鲁棒噪声降低：我们通过双重过滤方法构建了一个多重标准答案数据集，通过验证多样化的响应来降低噪声，从而捕获语义多样性。(3) 轻量级适应：我们设计了一种混合奖励机制，该机制融合了基于LLM的裁判和一个基于相关性的轻量级重排序器，以提取高保真度的奖励信号，同时降低了与标准LLM-as-a-Judge强化学习相比的计算成本。 在真实世界云服务任务上进行的、跨语义多样性设置的实证评估表明，我们的框架通过潜在逻辑增强和鲁棒噪声降低实现了稳定性和性能提升。 同时，我们的混合奖励机制实现了与标准LLM-as-a-judge方法相当的对齐效果，并且训练时间缩短，突显了在部署技术服务智能体方面的实际价值。

TLDR: This paper presents a lightweight adaptation framework for LLMs in technical service domains, addressing limitations in cognitive chains and response ambiguity through latent logic augmentation, robust noise reduction, and a hybrid reward mechanism, achieving stable performance gains with reduced training time.

简要说明: 本文提出了一种用于技术服务领域LLM的轻量级自适应框架，通过潜在逻辑增强、鲁棒噪声降低和混合奖励机制解决认知链和响应模糊性方面的限制，实现了稳定的性能提升并减少了训练时间。

Authors: Yi Yu, Junzhuo Ma, Chenghuang Shen, Xingyan Liu, Jing Gu, Hangyi Sun, Guangquan Hu, Jianfeng Liu, Weiting Liu, Mingyue Pu, Yu Wang, Zhengdong Xiao, Rui Xie, Longjiu Luo, Qianrong Wang, Gurong Cui, Honglin Qiao, Wenlian Lu

WebPII: Benchmarking Visual PII Detection for Computer-Use Agents

Abstract (English): Computer use agents create new privacy risks: training data collected from real websites inevitably contains sensitive information, and cloud-hosted inference exposes user screenshots. Detecting personally identifiable information in web screenshots is critical for privacy-preserving deployment, but no public benchmark exists for this task. We introduce WebPII, a fine-grained synthetic benchmark of 44,865 annotated e-commerce UI images designed with three key properties: extended PII taxonomy including transaction-level identifiers that enable reidentification, anticipatory detection for partially-filled forms where users are actively entering data, and scalable generation through VLM-based UI reproduction. Experiments validate that these design choices improve layout-invariant detection across diverse interfaces and generalization to held-out page types. We train WebRedact to demonstrate practical utility, more than doubling text-extraction baseline accuracy (0.753 vs 0.357 mAP@50) at real-time CPU latency (20ms). We release the dataset and model to support privacy-preserving computer use research.

摘要（中文）: 摘要： 计算机使用代理会带来新的隐私风险：从真实网站收集的训练数据不可避免地包含敏感信息，而云端托管的推理会暴露用户屏幕截图。在网页截图中检测个人身份信息对于保护隐私的部署至关重要，但目前没有针对此任务的公开基准。我们引入了WebPII，一个细粒度的合成基准，包含44,865个带注释的电子商务UI图像，该基准设计具有三个关键特性：扩展的PII分类，包括支持重新识别的交易级标识符；对用户正在积极输入数据的部分填写表格的预测性检测；以及通过基于VLM的UI重现实现的可扩展生成。实验验证了这些设计选择能够提高跨多样化界面的布局不变检测能力，并改进对预留页面类型的泛化能力。我们训练了WebRedact来展示其实用性，在实时CPU延迟（20毫秒）下，文本提取基线准确率提高了两倍以上（0.753 vs 0.357 mAP@50）。我们发布数据集和模型，以支持保护隐私的计算机使用研究。

TLDR: The paper introduces WebPII, a synthetic benchmark dataset for detecting personally identifiable information (PII) in web screenshots, aimed at improving privacy in computer-use agents. They also present WebRedact, a model trained on WebPII that demonstrates improved accuracy and speed in PII detection.

Authors: Nathan Zhao

A Progressive Visual-Logic-Aligned Framework for Ride-Hailing Adjudication

Abstract (English): The efficient adjudication of responsibility disputes is pivotal for maintaining marketplace fairness. However, the exponential surge in ride-hailing volume renders manual review intractable, while conventional automated methods lack the reasoning transparency required for quasi-judicial decisions. Although Multimodal LLMs offer a promising paradigm, they fundamentally struggle to bridge the gap between general visual semantics and rigorous evidentiary protocols, often leading to perceptual hallucinations and logical looseness. To address these systemic misalignments, we introduce RideJudge, a Progressive Visual-Logic-Aligned Framework. Instead of relying on generic pre-training, we bridge the semantic gap via SynTraj, a synthesis engine that grounds abstract liability concepts into concrete trajectory patterns. To resolve the conflict between massive regulation volume and limited context windows, we propose an Adaptive Context Optimization strategy that distills expert knowledge, coupled with a Chain-of-Adjudication mechanism to enforce active evidentiary inquiry. Furthermore, addressing the inadequacy of sparse binary feedback for complex liability assessment, we implement a novel Ordinal-Sensitive Reinforcement Learning mechanism that calibrates decision boundaries against hierarchical severity. Extensive experiments show that our RideJudge-8B achieves 88.41\% accuracy, surpassing 32B-scale baselines and establishing a new standard for interpretable adjudication.

摘要（中文）: 高效裁决责任纠纷对于维护市场公平性至关重要。然而，网约车订单量的指数级增长使得人工审核变得难以处理，而传统的自动化方法缺乏准司法决策所需的推理透明度。尽管多模态LLM提供了一种很有前景的范式，但它们在根本上难以弥合通用视觉语义和严格证据协议之间的差距，经常导致感知幻觉和逻辑松散。为了解决这些系统性错位，我们引入了RideJudge，一个渐进式的视觉-逻辑对齐框架。我们没有依赖通用的预训练，而是通过SynTraj（一种将抽象责任概念转化为具体轨迹模式的合成引擎）来弥合语义鸿沟。为了解决海量监管规则和有限上下文窗口之间的冲突，我们提出了一种自适应上下文优化策略，该策略提炼专家知识，并结合链式裁决机制，以强制进行积极的证据调查。此外，针对复杂责任评估中稀疏二元反馈的不足，我们实施了一种新型的序数敏感强化学习机制，该机制根据分层严重程度校准决策边界。广泛的实验表明，我们的RideJudge-8B 达到了 88.41% 的准确率，超过了 32B 规模的基线模型，并为可解释的裁决确立了新的标准。

TLDR: The paper introduces RideJudge, a framework using a visual-logic-aligned approach with synthetic data, context optimization, and ordinal-sensitive reinforcement learning to improve the accuracy and interpretability of ride-hailing dispute adjudication.

Authors: Weiming Wu, Zi-Jian Cheng, Jie Meng, Peng Zhen, Shan Huang, Qun Li, Guobin Wu, Lan-Zhe Guo

Recurrent Reasoning with Vision-Language Models for Estimating Long-Horizon Embodied Task Progress

Abstract (English): Accurately estimating task progress is critical for embodied agents to plan and execute long-horizon, multi-step tasks. Despite promising advances, existing Vision-Language Models (VLMs) based methods primarily leverage their video understanding capabilities, while neglecting their complex reasoning potential. Furthermore, processing long video trajectories with VLMs is computationally prohibitive for real-world deployment. To address these challenges, we propose the Recurrent Reasoning Vision-Language Model ($\text{R}^2$VLM). Our model features a recurrent reasoning framework that processes local video snippets iteratively, maintaining a global context through an evolving Chain of Thought (CoT). This CoT explicitly records task decomposition, key steps, and their completion status, enabling the model to reason about complex temporal dependencies. This design avoids the high cost of processing long videos while preserving essential reasoning capabilities. We train $\text{R}^2$VLM on large-scale, automatically generated datasets from ALFRED and Ego4D. Extensive experiments on progress estimation and downstream applications, including progress-enhanced policy learning, reward modeling for reinforcement learning, and proactive assistance, demonstrate that $\text{R}^2$VLM achieves strong performance and generalization, achieving a new state-of-the-art in long-horizon task progress estimation. The models and benchmarks are publicly available at \href{https://huggingface.co/collections/zhangyuelin/r2vlm}{huggingface}.

摘要（中文）: 准确估计任务进度对于具身智能体规划和执行长时程、多步骤任务至关重要。尽管取得了可喜的进展，但现有的基于视觉-语言模型 (VLMs) 的方法主要利用其视频理解能力，而忽略了其复杂的推理潜力。此外，使用 VLM 处理长视频轨迹在计算上对于实际部署来说是难以承受的。为了解决这些挑战，我们提出了递归推理视觉-语言模型 ($\text{R}^2$VLM)。我们的模型采用了一种递归推理框架，该框架迭代地处理局部视频片段，并通过不断演进的思维链 (CoT) 维护全局上下文。该 CoT 显式地记录任务分解、关键步骤及其完成状态，使模型能够推理复杂的时序依赖关系。这种设计避免了处理长视频的高成本，同时保留了必要的推理能力。我们在来自 ALFRED 和 Ego4D 的大规模自动生成数据集上训练了 $\text{R}^2$VLM 。在进度估计和下游应用（包括进度增强策略学习、强化学习的奖励建模和主动辅助）上的大量实验表明，$\text{R}^2$VLM 实现了强大的性能和泛化能力，在长时程任务进度估计方面达到了新的最先进水平。模型和基准测试可在 \href{https://huggingface.co/collections/zhangyuelin/r2vlm}{huggingface} 公开获取。

TLDR: The paper introduces R^2VLM, a recurrent vision-language model that iteratively processes video snippets with a Chain of Thought (CoT) to estimate long-horizon embodied task progress, achieving state-of-the-art results and demonstrating improvements in downstream tasks.

简要说明: 该论文介绍了R^2VLM，一种循环视觉语言模型，通过迭代处理视频片段并结合思维链（CoT）来估计长程具身任务的进度，实现了最先进的结果，并在下游任务中展示了改进。

Authors: Yuelin Zhang, Sijie Cheng, Chen Li, Zongzhao Li, Yuxin Huang, Yang Liu, Wenbing Huang

HopChain: Multi-Hop Data Synthesis for Generalizable Vision-Language Reasoning

Abstract (English): Vision-language models (VLMs) show strong multimodal capabilities but still struggle with fine-grained vision-language reasoning. We find that long chain-of-thought (CoT) reasoning exposes diverse failure modes, including perception, reasoning, knowledge, and hallucination errors, which can compound across intermediate steps. However, most existing vision-language data used for reinforcement learning with verifiable rewards (RLVR) does not involve complex reasoning chains that rely on visual evidence throughout, leaving these weaknesses largely unexposed. We therefore propose HopChain, a scalable framework for synthesizing multi-hop vision-language reasoning data for RLVR training of VLMs. Each synthesized multi-hop query forms a logically dependent chain of instance-grounded hops, where earlier hops establish the instances, sets, or conditions needed for later hops, while the final answer remains a specific, unambiguous number suitable for verifiable rewards. We train Qwen3.5-35B-A3B and Qwen3.5-397B-A17B under two RLVR settings: the original data alone, and the original data plus HopChain's multi-hop data, and compare them across 24 benchmarks spanning STEM and Puzzle, General VQA, Text Recognition and Document Understanding, and Video Understanding. Although this multi-hop data is not synthesized for any specific benchmark, it improves 20 of 24 benchmarks on both models, indicating broad and generalizable gains. Consistently, replacing full chained queries with half-multi-hop or single-hop variants reduces the average score across five representative benchmarks from 70.4 to 66.7 and 64.3, respectively. Notably, multi-hop gains peak in long-CoT vision-language reasoning, exceeding 50 points in the ultra-long-CoT regime. These experiments establish HopChain as an effective, scalable framework for synthesizing multi-hop data that improves generalizable vision-language reasoning.

摘要（中文）: 视觉语言模型（VLMs）展现出强大的多模态能力，但在细粒度的视觉语言推理方面仍然面临挑战。我们发现，长链式思考（CoT）推理会暴露多种失败模式，包括感知、推理、知识和幻觉错误，这些错误可能会在中间步骤中累积。然而，大多数用于基于可验证奖励的强化学习（RLVR）的现有视觉语言数据并不涉及依赖贯穿整个推理过程的视觉证据的复杂推理链，这使得这些弱点在很大程度上未被暴露出来。因此，我们提出了 HopChain，一个可扩展的框架，用于合成多跳视觉语言推理数据，以进行 VLMs 的 RLVR 训练。每个合成的多跳查询都形成一个逻辑上依赖的实例对齐的跳跃链，其中较早的跳跃建立实例、集合或条件，以供后续跳跃使用，而最终答案仍然是一个具体、明确的数字，适合可验证的奖励。我们使用 Qwen3.5-35B-A3B 和 Qwen3.5-397B-A17B 在两种 RLVR 设置下进行训练：仅使用原始数据，以及原始数据加上 HopChain 的多跳数据，并在跨越 STEM 和拼图、通用 VQA、文本识别和文档理解以及视频理解的 24 个基准上进行比较。尽管这种多跳数据并非针对任何特定基准合成，但它提高了这两个模型在 24 个基准中的 20 个的表现，表明了广泛且可泛化的增益。相应地，将完全链式查询替换为半多跳或单跳变体会将五个代表性基准的平均分数从 70.4 分别降至 66.7 和 64.3。值得注意的是，多跳增益在长 CoT 视觉语言推理中达到峰值，在超长 CoT 领域超过 50 分。这些实验确立了 HopChain 作为一个有效、可扩展的框架，用于合成多跳数据，从而提高了可泛化的视觉语言推理能力。

TLDR: The paper introduces HopChain, a framework for synthesizing multi-hop vision-language reasoning data for RLVR training, showing broad performance improvements across various benchmarks by exposing failure modes in long CoT reasoning.

简要说明: 该论文介绍了HopChain，一个用于合成多跳视觉语言推理数据的框架，以用于RLVR训练。该框架通过暴露长CoT推理中的失败模式，在各种基准测试中显示出广泛的性能提升。

Authors: Shenzhi Wang, Shixuan Liu, Jing Zhou, Chang Gao, Xiong-Hui Chen, Binghai Wang, An Yang, Shiji Song, Bowen Yu, Gao Huang, Junyang Lin

Universal Skeleton Understanding via Differentiable Rendering and MLLMs

Abstract (English): Multimodal large language models (MLLMs) exhibit strong visual-language reasoning, yet remain confined to their native modalities and cannot directly process structured, non-visual data such as human skeletons. Existing methods either compress skeleton dynamics into lossy feature vectors for text alignment, or quantize motion into discrete tokens that generalize poorly across heterogeneous skeleton formats. We present SkeletonLLM, which achieves universal skeleton understanding by translating arbitrary skeleton sequences into the MLLM's native visual modality. At its core is DrAction, a differentiable, format-agnostic renderer that converts skeletal kinematics into compact image sequences. Because the pipeline is end-to-end differentiable, MLLM gradients can directly guide the rendering to produce task-informative visual tokens. To further enhance reasoning capabilities, we introduce a cooperative training strategy: Causal Reasoning Distillation transfers structured, step-by-step reasoning from a teacher model, while Discriminative Finetuning sharpens decision boundaries between confusable actions. SkeletonLLM demonstrates strong generalization on diverse tasks including recognition, captioning, reasoning, and cross-format transfer -- suggesting a viable path for applying MLLMs to non-native modalities. Code will be released upon acceptance.

摘要（中文）: 多模态大型语言模型（MLLMs）表现出强大的视觉-语言推理能力，但仍局限于其原生模态，无法直接处理结构化的非视觉数据，例如人体骨骼。现有方法要么将骨骼动态压缩为有损的特征向量以进行文本对齐，要么将运动量化为离散的token，这些token在异构骨骼格式之间泛化性较差。我们提出了SkeletonLLM，它通过将任意骨骼序列翻译成MLLM的原生视觉模态来实现通用骨骼理解。其核心是DrAction，一个可微的、格式无关的渲染器，可以将骨骼运动学转换为紧凑的图像序列。由于该流程是端到端可微的，MLLM梯度可以直接指导渲染，从而产生任务信息丰富的视觉token。为了进一步提高推理能力，我们引入了一种协同训练策略：因果推理蒸馏从教师模型迁移结构化的、逐步推理过程，而判别式微调能锐化易混淆动作之间的决策边界。SkeletonLLM在包括识别、描述、推理和跨格式迁移等多种任务上都表现出强大的泛化能力——为将MLLM应用于非原生模态提供了一条可行的路径。代码将在接收后发布。

TLDR: The paper introduces SkeletonLLM, a method for enabling MLLMs to understand arbitrary skeleton sequences by converting them into visual representations via a differentiable renderer, enhancing reasoning through cooperative training strategies.

简要说明: 本文介绍了SkeletonLLM，它通过可微渲染器将任意骨骼序列转换为视觉表示，使MLLM能够理解它们，并通过协作训练策略增强推理能力。

Authors: Ziyi Wang, Peiming Li, Xinshun Wang, Yang Tang, Kai-Kuang Ma, Mengyuan Liu

Feeling the Space: Egomotion-Aware Video Representation for Efficient and Accurate 3D Scene Understanding

Abstract (English): Recent Multimodal Large Language Models (MLLMs) have shown high potential for spatial reasoning within 3D scenes. However, they typically rely on computationally expensive 3D representations like point clouds or reconstructed Bird's-Eye View (BEV) maps, or lack physical grounding to resolve ambiguities in scale and size. This paper significantly enhances MLLMs with egomotion modality data, captured by Inertial Measurement Units (IMUs) concurrently with the video. In particular, we propose a novel framework, called Motion-MLLM, introducing two key components: (1) a cascaded motion-visual keyframe filtering module that leverages both IMU data and visual features to efficiently select a sparse yet representative set of keyframes, and (2) an asymmetric cross-modal fusion module where motion tokens serve as intermediaries that channel egomotion cues and cross-frame visual context into the visual representation. By grounding visual content in physical egomotion trajectories, Motion-MLLM can reason about absolute scale and spatial relationships across the scene. Our extensive evaluation shows that Motion-MLLM makes significant improvements in various tasks related to 3D scene understanding and spatial reasoning. Compared to state-of-the-art (SOTA) methods based on video frames and explicit 3D data, Motion-MLLM exhibits similar or even higher accuracy with significantly less overhead (i.e., 1.40$\times$ and 1.63$\times$ higher cost-effectiveness, respectively).

摘要（中文）: 最近的多模态大型语言模型（MLLM）在3D场景中的空间推理方面展现出巨大潜力。然而，它们通常依赖于计算成本高昂的3D表示，如点云或重建的鸟瞰图（BEV）地图，或者缺乏物理基础来解决尺度和尺寸上的歧义。本文通过惯性测量单元（IMU）与视频同步采集的自运动模态数据，显著增强了MLLM。具体而言，我们提出了一种名为Motion-MLLM的新颖框架，引入了两个关键组成部分：（1）一个级联式运动-视觉关键帧过滤模块，该模块利用IMU数据和视觉特征来高效地选择一个稀疏但具有代表性的关键帧集合；（2）一个非对称跨模态融合模块，其中运动令牌充当媒介，将自运动线索和跨帧视觉上下文引导到视觉表示中。通过将视觉内容与物理自运动轨迹相结合，Motion-MLLM可以推理场景中的绝对尺度和空间关系。我们的大量评估表明，Motion-MLLM在与3D场景理解和空间推理相关的各项任务中取得了显著改进。与基于视频帧和显式3D数据的最先进（SOTA）方法相比，Motion-MLLM表现出相似甚至更高的准确性，但开销显著降低（即，成本效益分别提高了1.40倍和1.63倍）。

TLDR: The paper introduces Motion-MLLM, a framework enhancing MLLMs with egomotion data (IMU) for improved 3D scene understanding, achieving higher cost-effectiveness compared to SOTA methods.

简要说明: 该论文介绍了Motion-MLLM，一个利用惯性测量单元(IMU)数据增强MLLM的框架，从而提升3D场景理解能力，并比现有最优方法更具成本效益。

Authors: Shuyao Shi, Kang G. Shin

Part-Aware Open-Vocabulary 3D Affordance Grounding via Prototypical Semantic and Geometric Alignment

Abstract (English): Grounding natural language questions to functionally relevant regions in 3D objects -- termed language-driven 3D affordance grounding -- is essential for embodied intelligence and human-AI interaction. Existing methods, while progressing from label-based to language-driven approaches, still face challenges in open-vocabulary generalization, fine-grained geometric alignment, and part-level semantic consistency. To address these issues, we propose a novel two-stage cross-modal framework that enhances both semantic and geometric representations for open-vocabulary 3D affordance grounding. In the first stage, large language models generate part-aware instructions to recover missing semantics, enabling the model to link semantically similar affordances. In the second stage, we introduce two key components: Affordance Prototype Aggregation (APA), which captures cross-object geometric consistency for each affordance, and Intra-Object Relational Modeling (IORM), which refines geometric differentiation within objects to support precise semantic alignment. We validate the effectiveness of our method through extensive experiments on a newly introduced benchmark, as well as two existing benchmarks, demonstrating superior performance in comparison with existing methods.

摘要（中文）: 将自然语言问题与3D对象中具备功能相关性的区域进行关联，即语言驱动的3D可供性区域定位，对于具身智能和人机交互至关重要。现有方法虽然从基于标签的方法发展到语言驱动的方法，但在开放词汇泛化、细粒度的几何对齐和部件级语义一致性方面仍然面临挑战。为了解决这些问题，我们提出了一种新颖的两阶段跨模态框架，该框架增强了开放词汇3D可供性区域定位的语义和几何表示。在第一阶段，大型语言模型生成部件感知指令以恢复缺失的语义信息，从而使模型能够连接语义上相似的可供性。在第二阶段，我们引入了两个关键组件：可供性原型聚合(APA)，它捕获了每个可供性的跨对象几何一致性；以及对象内关系建模(IORM)，它细化了对象内的几何差异以支持精确的语义对齐。我们通过在新引入的基准测试集以及两个现有基准测试集上进行的大量实验验证了我们方法的有效性，证明了与现有方法相比的卓越性能。

TLDR: This paper introduces a two-stage cross-modal framework for open-vocabulary 3D affordance grounding, leveraging part-aware instructions from LLMs and novel geometric alignment techniques to improve performance on existing and new benchmarks.

简要说明: 本文提出了一种用于开放词汇三维可供性接地的两阶段跨模态框架，利用来自大型语言模型的部分感知指令和新的几何对齐技术，提高了在现有和新基准测试上的性能。

Authors: Dongqiang Gou, Xuming He

ReLaGS: Relational Language Gaussian Splatting

Abstract (English): Achieving unified 3D perception and reasoning across tasks such as segmentation, retrieval, and relation understanding remains challenging, as existing methods are either object-centric or rely on costly training for inter-object reasoning. We present a novel framework that constructs a hierarchical language-distilled Gaussian scene and its 3D semantic scene graph without scene-specific training. A Gaussian pruning mechanism refines scene geometry, while a robust multi-view language alignment strategy aggregates noisy 2D features into accurate 3D object embeddings. On top of this hierarchy, we build an open-vocabulary 3D scene graph with Vision Language derived annotations and Graph Neural Network-based relational reasoning. Our approach enables efficient and scalable open-vocabulary 3D reasoning by jointly modeling hierarchical semantics and inter/intra-object relationships, validated across tasks including open-vocabulary segmentation, scene graph generation, and relation-guided retrieval. Project page: https://dfki-av.github.io/ReLaGS/

摘要（中文）: 在分割、检索和关系理解等任务中实现统一的3D感知与推理仍然具有挑战性，因为现有方法要么以对象为中心，要么依赖于昂贵的对象间推理训练。我们提出了一种新颖的框架，该框架构建了一个分层语言提炼的高斯场景及其3D语义场景图，而无需针对特定场景的训练。一种高斯修剪机制细化场景几何结构，而一种鲁棒的多视角语言对齐策略将嘈杂的2D特征聚合为精确的3D对象嵌入。在此层次结构之上，我们构建了一个具有视觉语言派生标注和基于图神经网络的关系推理的开放词汇3D场景图。我们的方法通过联合建模分层语义和对象内/对象间关系，实现了高效且可扩展的开放词汇3D推理，并在开放词汇分割、场景图生成和关系引导的检索等任务中得到了验证。项目主页：https://dfki-av.github.io/ReLaGS/

TLDR: The paper introduces ReLaGS, a framework for constructing a hierarchical language-distilled Gaussian scene and 3D semantic scene graph without scene-specific training, enabling open-vocabulary 3D reasoning across tasks like segmentation and retrieval.

简要说明: 该论文介绍了ReLaGS，一种用于构建分层语言提炼高斯场景和3D语义场景图的框架，无需特定于场景的训练，从而实现跨分割和检索等任务的开放词汇3D推理。

Authors: Yaxu Xie, Abdalla Arafa, Alireza Javanmardi, Christen Millerdurai, Jia Cheng Hu, Shaoxiang Wang, Alain Pagani, Didier Stricker

Temporal Gains, Spatial Costs: Revisiting Video Fine-Tuning in Multimodal Large Language Models

Abstract (English): Multimodal large language models (MLLMs) are typically trained in multiple stages, with video-based supervised fine-tuning (Video-SFT) serving as a key step for improving visual understanding. Yet its effect on the fine-grained evolution of visual capabilities, particularly the balance between spatial and temporal understanding, remains poorly understood. In this paper, we systematically study how Video-SFT reshapes visual capabilities in MLLMs. Across architectures, parameter scales, and frame sampling settings, we observe a consistent pattern: Video-SFT reliably improves video performance, but often yields limited gains or even degradation on static image benchmarks. We further show that this trade-off is closely tied to temporal budget: increasing the number of sampled frames generally improves video performance, but does not reliably improve static image performance. Motivated by this finding, we study an instruction-aware Hybrid-Frame strategy that adaptively allocates frame counts and partially mitigates the image-video trade-off. Our results indicate that Video-SFT is not a free lunch for MLLMs, and preserving spatial understanding remains a central challenge in joint image-video training.

摘要（中文）: 多模态大型语言模型（MLLM）通常经过多阶段训练，其中基于视频的监督微调（Video-SFT）是提升视觉理解的关键步骤。然而，其对视觉能力精细演化过程的影响，特别是空间理解和时间理解之间的平衡，仍然缺乏充分的理解。在本文中，我们系统地研究了Video-SFT如何重塑MLLM中的视觉能力。 在不同的架构、参数规模和帧采样设置下，我们观察到一个一致的模式：Video-SFT能够可靠地提升视频性能，但通常在静态图像基准测试上收益有限，甚至出现性能下降。我们进一步表明，这种权衡与时间预算密切相关：增加采样帧数通常会提高视频性能，但不能可靠地提高静态图像性能。受此发现的启发，我们研究了一种指令感知的混合帧策略，该策略自适应地分配帧数，并部分缓解了图像-视频之间的权衡。 我们的结果表明，Video-SFT对于MLLM而言并非免费午餐，并且在联合图像-视频训练中，保持空间理解仍然是一项核心挑战。

TLDR: This paper investigates the trade-offs between spatial and temporal understanding in MLLMs during video fine-tuning, showing that improving video performance can sometimes degrade static image performance and proposing a frame sampling strategy to mitigate this issue.

简要说明: 本文研究了多模态大型语言模型在视频微调过程中空间和时间理解之间的权衡，表明提高视频性能有时会降低静态图像性能，并提出了一种帧采样策略来缓解这个问题。

Authors: Linghao Zhang, Jungang Li, Yonghua Hei, Sicheng Tao, Song Dai, Yibo Yan, Zihao Dongfang, Weiting Liu, Chenxi Qin, Hanqian Li, Xin Zou, Jiahao Zhang, Shuhang Xun, Haiyun Jiang, Xuming Hu

Stereo World Model: Camera-Guided Stereo Video Generation

Abstract (English): We present StereoWorld, a camera-conditioned stereo world model that jointly learns appearance and binocular geometry for end-to-end stereo video generation.Unlike monocular RGB or RGBD approaches, StereoWorld operates exclusively within the RGB modality, while simultaneously grounding geometry directly from disparity. To efficiently achieve consistent stereo generation, our approach introduces two key designs: (1) a unified camera-frame RoPE that augments latent tokens with camera-aware rotary positional encoding, enabling relative, view- and time-consistent conditioning while preserving pretrained video priors via a stable attention initialization; and (2) a stereo-aware attention decomposition that factors full 4D attention into 3D intra-view attention plus horizontal row attention, leveraging the epipolar prior to capture disparity-aligned correspondences with substantially lower compute. Across benchmarks, StereoWorld improves stereo consistency, disparity accuracy, and camera-motion fidelity over strong monocular-then-convert pipelines, achieving more than 3x faster generation with an additional 5% gain in viewpoint consistency. Beyond benchmarks, StereoWorld enables end-to-end binocular VR rendering without depth estimation or inpainting, enhances embodied policy learning through metric-scale depth grounding, and is compatible with long-video distillation for extended interactive stereo synthesis.

摘要（中文）: 我们提出了StereoWorld，一种摄像机条件立体世界模型，它联合学习外观和双目几何，用于端到端立体视频生成。与单目RGB或RGBD方法不同，StereoWorld完全在RGB模态下运行，同时直接从视差中推导几何信息。为了有效地实现一致的立体生成，我们的方法引入了两个关键设计：（1）一种统一的摄像机帧RoPE，它使用摄像机感知的旋转位置编码来增强潜在token，从而实现相对的、视角和时间一致的条件化，同时通过稳定的注意力初始化保留预训练的视频先验；以及(2) 一种立体感知的注意力分解，它将完整的4D注意力分解为3D视图内注意力加上水平行注意力，利用极线先验来捕获视差对齐的对应关系，并显著降低计算量。在各个基准测试中，StereoWorld相对于强大的先单目后转换流水线，提高了立体一致性、视差精度和摄像机运动保真度，实现了超过3倍的生成速度，并在视点一致性方面额外提高了5%。除了基准测试之外，StereoWorld还支持无需深度估计或修复的端到端双目VR渲染，通过度量尺度的深度推导增强了具身策略学习，并且兼容于长视频蒸馏，用于扩展的交互式立体合成。

TLDR: StereoWorld is a novel camera-conditioned stereo world model for end-to-end stereo video generation, achieving faster generation, improved consistency, and enabling VR rendering and embodied policy learning.

简要说明: StereoWorld 是一种新型的相机条件立体世界模型，用于端到端立体视频生成，实现更快的生成速度、更高的连贯性，并支持 VR 渲染和具身策略学习。

Authors: Yang-Tian Sun, Zehuan Huang, Yifan Niu, Lin Ma, Yan-Pei Cao, Yuewen Ma, Xiaojuan Qi

EvoGuard: An Extensible Agentic RL-based Framework for Practical and Evolving AI-Generated Image Detection

Abstract (English): The rapid proliferation of AI-Generated Images (AIGIs) has introduced severe risks of misinformation, making AIGI detection a critical yet challenging task. While traditional detection paradigms mainly rely on low-level features, recent research increasingly focuses on leveraging the general understanding ability of Multimodal Large Language Models (MLLMs) to achieve better generalization, but still suffer from limited extensibility and expensive training data annotations. To better address complex and dynamic real-world environments, we propose EvoGuard, a novel agentic framework for AIGI detection. It encapsulates various state-of-the-art (SOTA) off-the-shelf MLLM and non-MLLM detectors as callable tools, and coordinates them through a capability-aware dynamic orchestration mechanism. Empowered by the agent's capacities for autonomous planning and reflection, it intelligently selects suitable tools for given samples, reflects intermediate results, and decides the next action, reaching a final conclusion through multi-turn invocation and reasoning. This design effectively exploits the complementary strengths among heterogeneous detectors, transcending the limits of any single model. Furthermore, optimized by a GRPO-based Agentic Reinforcement Learning algorithm using only low-cost binary labels, it eliminates the reliance on fine-grained annotations. Extensive experiments demonstrate that EvoGuard achieves SOTA accuracy while mitigating the bias between positive and negative samples. More importantly, it allows the plug-and-play integration of new detectors to boost overall performance in a train-free manner, offering a highly practical, long-term solution to ever-evolving AIGI threats. Source code will be publicly available upon acceptance.

摘要（中文）: 人工智能生成图像（AIGI）的迅速普及带来了严重的虚假信息风险，使得AIGI检测成为一项关键而又具有挑战性的任务。尽管传统的检测方法主要依赖于低层特征，但最近的研究越来越侧重于利用多模态大型语言模型（MLLM）的通用理解能力，以实现更好的泛化性，但仍然面临着有限的可扩展性和昂贵的训练数据标注问题。为了更好地应对复杂且动态的真实世界环境，我们提出了一种新颖的AIGI检测的智能体框架EvoGuard。它将各种最先进的（SOTA）现成MLLM和非MLLM检测器封装为可调用的工具，并通过一种能力感知的动态编排机制协调它们。凭借智能体自主规划和反思的能力，它智能地为给定的样本选择合适的工具，反思中间结果，并决定下一步行动，通过多轮调用和推理得出最终结论。这种设计有效地利用了异构检测器之间的互补优势，超越了任何单一模型的局限性。此外，通过仅使用低成本二元标签的基于GRPO的智能体强化学习算法进行优化，它消除了对细粒度标注的依赖。大量实验表明，EvoGuard实现了SOTA的准确率，同时减轻了正负样本之间的偏差。更重要的是，它允许以即插即用的方式集成新的检测器，以在无需训练的情况下提升整体性能，从而为不断演变的AIGI威胁提供了一种高度实用且长期的解决方案。源代码将在论文被接受后公开。

TLDR: The paper introduces EvoGuard, an agentic RL framework for AIGI detection that leverages MLLMs and other detectors, orchestrated by an RL agent, achieving SOTA accuracy with low-cost training and plug-and-play extensibility.

Authors: Chenyang Zhu, Maorong Wang, Jun Liu, Ching-Chun Chang, Isao Echizen

GigaWorld-Policy: An Efficient Action-Centered World--Action Model

Abstract (English): World-Action Models (WAM) initialized from pre-trained video generation backbones have demonstrated remarkable potential for robot policy learning. However, existing approaches face two critical bottlenecks that hinder performance and deployment. First, jointly reasoning over future visual dynamics and corresponding actions incurs substantial inference overhead. Second, joint modeling often entangles visual and motion representations, making motion prediction accuracy heavily dependent on the quality of future video forecasts. To address these issues, we introduce GigaWorld-Policy, an action-centered WAM that learns 2D pixel-action dynamics while enabling efficient action decoding, with optional video generation. Specifically, we formulate policy training into two coupled components: the model predicts future action sequences conditioned on the current observation, and simultaneously generates future videos conditioned on the predicted actions and the same observation. The policy is supervised by both action prediction and video generation, providing richer learning signals and encouraging physically plausible actions through visual-dynamics constraints. With a causal design that prevents future-video tokens from influencing action tokens, explicit future-video generation is optional at inference time, allowing faster action prediction during deployment. To support this paradigm, we curate a diverse, large-scale robot dataset to pre-train an action-centered video generation model, which is then adapted as the backbone for robot policy learning. Experimental results on real-world robotic platforms show that GigaWorld-Policy runs 9x faster than the leading WAM baseline, Motus, while improving task success rates by 7%. Moreover, compared with pi-0.5, GigaWorld-Policy improves performance by 95% on RoboTwin 2.0.

摘要（中文）: 从预训练的视频生成骨干网络初始化的世界-行动模型（WAM）已展现出在机器人策略学习方面的显著潜力。然而，现有方法面临两个阻碍性能和部署的关键瓶颈。首先，联合推理未来视觉动态和相应动作会导致巨大的推理开销。其次，联合建模通常会纠缠视觉和运动表征，使得运动预测精度严重依赖于未来视频预测的质量。为了解决这些问题，我们引入了GigaWorld-Policy，一种以动作为中心的WAM，其学习2D像素-动作动态，同时支持高效的动作解码，并可选择进行视频生成。具体而言，我们将策略训练构建为两个耦合的组件：模型在当前观测条件下预测未来的动作序列，并同时在预测的动作和相同观测条件下生成未来的视频。该策略受到动作预测和视频生成的双重监督，从而提供更丰富的学习信号并通过视觉-动态约束来鼓励物理上合理的动作。凭借防止未来视频token影响动作token的因果设计，显式的未来视频生成在推理时是可选的，从而允许在部署期间进行更快的动作预测。为了支持这种范式，我们策划了一个多样化的大规模机器人数据集，以预训练一个以动作为中心的视频生成模型，然后将其用作机器人策略学习的骨干网络。在真实机器人平台上的实验结果表明，GigaWorld-Policy的运行速度比领先的WAM基线Motus快9倍，同时任务成功率提高了7%。此外，与pi-0.5相比，GigaWorld-Policy在RoboTwin 2.0上的性能提高了95%。

TLDR: GigaWorld-Policy introduces an action-centered World-Action Model (WAM) that enhances robot policy learning by decoupling action prediction and video generation. It achieves significant speed improvements and higher task success rates compared to existing methods.

简要说明: GigaWorld-Policy 提出了一种以动作为中心的 World-Action Model (WAM)，通过解耦动作预测和视频生成来增强机器人策略学习。与现有方法相比，它在速度和任务成功率方面都有显著提高。

Authors: Angen Ye, Boyuan Wang, Chaojun Ni, Guan Huang, Guosheng Zhao, Hao Li, Hengtao Li, Jie Li, Jindi Lv, Jingyu Liu, Min Cao, Peng Li, Qiuping Deng, Wenjun Mei, Xiaofeng Wang, Xinze Chen, Xinyu Zhou, Yang Wang, Yifan Chang, Yifan Li, Yukun Zhou, Yun Ye, Zhichao Liu, Zheng Zhu

MosaicMem: Hybrid Spatial Memory for Controllable Video World Models

Abstract (English): Video diffusion models are moving beyond short, plausible clips toward world simulators that must remain consistent under camera motion, revisits, and intervention. Yet spatial memory remains a key bottleneck: explicit 3D structures can improve reprojection-based consistency but struggle to depict moving objects, while implicit memory often produces inaccurate camera motion even with correct poses. We propose Mosaic Memory (MosaicMem), a hybrid spatial memory that lifts patches into 3D for reliable localization and targeted retrieval, while exploiting the model's native conditioning to preserve prompt-following generation. MosaicMem composes spatially aligned patches in the queried view via a patch-and-compose interface, preserving what should persist while allowing the model to inpaint what should evolve. With PRoPE camera conditioning and two new memory alignment methods, experiments show improved pose adherence compared to implicit memory and stronger dynamic modeling than explicit baselines. MosaicMem further enables minute-level navigation, memory-based scene editing, and autoregressive rollout.

摘要（中文）: 视频扩散模型正从短小、看似合理的片段向世界模拟器发展，这些模拟器必须在相机运动、重访和干预下保持一致性。然而，空间记忆仍然是一个关键瓶颈：显式3D结构可以提高基于重投影的一致性，但在描绘移动对象方面存在困难，而隐式记忆即使在姿态正确的情况下也经常产生不准确的相机运动。我们提出了Mosaic Memory (MosaicMem)，这是一种混合空间记忆，将图像块提升到3D空间中，以实现可靠的定位和目标检索，同时利用模型的原生条件化来保持提示生成。MosaicMem通过图像块组合接口在查询视角中组合空间对齐的图像块，保留应该持久存在的内容，同时允许模型修复应该演变的内容。通过PRoPE相机条件化和两种新的记忆对齐方法，实验表明，与隐式记忆相比，姿态依从性得到了提高，并且动态建模也比显式基线更强。MosaicMem进一步实现了分钟级的导航、基于记忆的场景编辑和自回归展开。

TLDR: MosaicMem introduces a hybrid spatial memory for video world models, combining explicit 3D patch-based structures with implicit model conditioning for improved consistency, pose adherence, and dynamic modeling in long-horizon video generation and manipulation.

Authors: Wei Yu, Runjia Qian, Yumeng Li, Liquan Wang, Songheng Yin, Sri Siddarth Chakaravarthy P, Dennis Anthony, Yang Ye, Yidi Li, Weiwei Wan, Animesh Garg

LLM-Powered Flood Depth Estimation from Social Media Imagery: A Vision-Language Model Framework with Mechanistic Interpretability for Transportation Resilience

Abstract (English): Urban flooding poses an escalating threat to transportation network continuity, yet no operational system currently provides real-time, street-level flood depth information at the centimeter resolution required for dynamic routing, electric vehicle (EV) safety, and autonomous vehicle (AV) operations. This study presents FloodLlama, a fine-tuned open-source vision-language model (VLM) for continuous flood depth estimation from single street-level images, supported by a multimodal sensing pipeline using TikTok data. A synthetic dataset of approximately 190000 images was generated, covering seven vehicle types, four weather conditions, and 41 depth levels (0-40 cm at 1 cm resolution). Progressive curriculum training enabled coarse-to-fine learning, while LLaMA 3.2-11B Vision was fine-tuned using QLoRA. Evaluation across 34797 trials reveals a depth-dependent prompt effect: simple prompts perform better for shallow flooding, whereas chain-of-thought (CoT) reasoning improves performance at greater depths. FloodLlama achieves a mean absolute error (MAE) below 0.97 cm and Acc@5cm above 93.7% for deep flooding, exceeding 96.8% for shallow depths. A five-phase mechanistic interpretability framework identifies layer L23 as the critical depth-encoding transition and enables selective fine-tuning that reduces trainable parameters by 76-80% while maintaining accuracy. The Tier 3 configuration achieves 98.62% accuracy on real-world data and shows strong robustness under visual occlusion. A TikTok-based data pipeline, validated on 676 annotated flood frames from Detroit, demonstrates the feasibility of real-time, crowd-sourced flood sensing. The proposed framework provides a scalable, infrastructure-free solution with direct implications for EV safety, AV deployment, and resilient transportation management.

摘要（中文）: 城市洪水对交通网络连通性构成日益严重的威胁，但目前尚无运行系统能够提供厘米级精度的实时、街道级洪水深度信息，而这对于动态路径规划、电动汽车（EV）安全和自动驾驶汽车（AV）运行至关重要。本研究提出了 FloodLlama，一种微调的开源视觉语言模型（VLM），用于从单张街道级图像中连续估计洪水深度，并由利用 TikTok 数据的多模态传感管道提供支持。生成了约 19 万张图像的合成数据集，涵盖七种车辆类型、四种天气条件和 41 个深度级别（0-40 厘米，分辨率为 1 厘米）。渐进式课程学习实现了由粗到精的学习，同时使用 QLoRA 对 LLaMA 3.2-11B Vision 进行了微调。对 34797 次试验的评估揭示了一种深度相关的提示效应：简单的提示在浅水淹没时表现更好，而思维链（CoT）推理提高了在更大深度时的性能。FloodLlama 在深水淹没时实现了低于 0.97 厘米的平均绝对误差（MAE）和高于 93.7% 的 Acc@5cm，在浅水深度时超过 96.8%。一个五阶段的机理可解释性框架将第 L23 层识别为关键的深度编码转换层，并实现了选择性微调，在保持精度的同时减少了 76-80% 的可训练参数。三级配置在真实世界数据上实现了 98.62% 的准确率，并在视觉遮挡下表现出强大的鲁棒性。一个基于 TikTok 的数据管道，在来自底特律的 676 个带注释的洪水帧上进行了验证，证明了实时、众包洪水感知的可行性。所提出的框架提供了一种可扩展的、无需基础设施的解决方案，对电动汽车安全、自动驾驶汽车部署和弹性交通管理具有直接影响。

TLDR: This paper introduces FloodLlama, a fine-tuned vision-language model (VLM) using TikTok data for real-time, street-level flood depth estimation, achieving high accuracy and mechanistic interpretability with a focus on transportation resilience.

Authors: Nafis Fuad, Xiaodong Qian

Unified Policy Value Decomposition for Rapid Adaptation

Abstract (English): Rapid adaptation in complex control systems remains a central challenge in reinforcement learning. We introduce a framework in which policy and value functions share a low-dimensional coefficient vector - a goal embedding - that captures task identity and enables immediate adaptation to novel tasks without retraining representations. During pretraining, we jointly learn structured value bases and compatible policy bases through a bilinear actor-critic decomposition. The critic factorizes as Q = sum_k G_k(g) y_k(s,a), where G_k(g) is a goal-conditioned coefficient vector and y_k(s,a) are learned value basis functions. This multiplicative gating - where a context signal scales a set of state-dependent bases - is reminiscent of gain modulation observed in Layer 5 pyramidal neurons, where top-down inputs modulate the gain of sensory-driven responses without altering their tuning. Building on Successor Features, we extend the decomposition to the actor, which composes a set of primitive policies weighted by the same coefficients G_k(g). At test time the bases are frozen and G_k(g) is estimated zero-shot via a single forward pass, enabling immediate adaptation to novel tasks without any gradient update. We train a Soft Actor-Critic agent on the MuJoCo Ant environment under a multi-directional locomotion objective, requiring the agent to walk in eight directions specified as continuous goal vectors. The bilinear structure allows each policy head to specialize to a subset of directions, while the shared coefficient layer generalizes across them, accommodating novel directions by interpolating in goal embedding space. Our results suggest that shared low-dimensional goal embeddings offer a general mechanism for rapid, structured adaptation in high-dimensional control, and highlight a potentially biologically plausible principle for efficient transfer in complex reinforcement learning systems.

摘要（中文）: 复杂控制系统中快速适应仍然是强化学习领域的核心挑战。我们引入了一种框架，其中策略和价值函数共享一个低维系数向量——目标嵌入——它捕获任务标识，并能够在不重新训练表示的情况下立即适应新任务。在预训练过程中，我们通过双线性Actor-Critic分解联合学习结构化的价值基函数和兼容的策略基函数。Critic分解为 Q = sum_k G_k(g) y_k(s,a)，其中G_k(g)是一个目标条件化的系数向量，y_k(s,a)是学习到的价值基函数。这种乘法门控——其中上下文信号缩放一组状态相关的基函数——类似于在第5层锥体神经元中观察到的增益调制，其中自顶向下的输入在不改变其调谐特性的情况下调制感觉驱动响应的增益。基于后继特征，我们将这种分解扩展到Actor，后者组合了一组由相同的系数G_k(g)加权的原始策略。在测试时，基函数被冻结，G_k(g)通过单次前向传递以零样本的方式进行估计，从而无需任何梯度更新即可立即适应新任务。我们使用Soft Actor-Critic智能体在MuJoCo Ant环境下，以多方向运动为目标进行训练，这要求智能体在由连续目标向量指定的八个方向上行走。双线性结构允许每个策略头专注于方向的子集，而共享的系数层对其进行泛化，通过在目标嵌入空间中进行插值来适应新方向。我们的结果表明，共享的低维目标嵌入为高维控制中的快速、结构化适应提供了一种通用机制，并突出了复杂强化学习系统中有效迁移的一种潜在的生物学上合理的原则。

TLDR: This paper proposes a unified policy value decomposition framework using a shared low-dimensional goal embedding for rapid adaptation in reinforcement learning, demonstrating immediate adaptation to novel tasks without retraining.

简要说明: 本文提出了一种统一的策略价值分解框架，使用共享的低维目标嵌入，以实现强化学习中的快速适应，并展示了无需重新训练即可立即适应新任务的能力。

Authors: Cristiano Capone, Luca Falorsi, Andrea Ciardiello, Luca Manneschi

Operator-Theoretic Foundations and Policy Gradient Methods for General MDPs with Unbounded Costs

Abstract (English): Markov decision processes (MDPs) is viewed as an optimization of an objective function over certain linear operators over general function spaces. Using the well-established perturbation theory of linear operators, this viewpoint allows one to identify derivatives of the objective function as a function of the linear operators. This leads to generalization of many well-known results in reinforcement learning to cases with generate state and action spaces. Prior results of this type were only established in the finite-state finite-action MDP settings and in settings with certain linear function approximations. The framework also leads to new low-complexity PPO-type reinforcement learning algorithms for general state and action space MDPs.

摘要（中文）: 马尔可夫决策过程（MDP）被视为在一般函数空间上某些线性算子上优化目标函数的过程。利用成熟的线性算子扰动理论，这种观点允许将目标函数关于线性算子的导数识别出来。这使得强化学习中的许多众所周知的结果能够推广到一般状态和动作空间的情况。此前，这类结果仅在有限状态-有限动作MDP设置以及具有特定线性函数逼近的设置中得到验证。该框架还为通用状态和动作空间MDP带来了新的低复杂度PPO类型强化学习算法。

TLDR: This paper presents a novel operator-theoretic framework for analyzing and solving general MDPs with unbounded costs, leading to a generalized policy gradient method applicable to continuous state and action spaces without restrictive function approximation assumptions.

简要说明: 本文提出了一个新颖的算子理论框架，用于分析和解决具有无界成本的通用MDP，从而产生一种适用于连续状态和动作空间的通用策略梯度方法，而无需严格的函数逼近假设。

Authors: Abhishek Gupta, Aditya Mahajan

Flow Matching Policy with Entropy Regularization

Abstract (English): Diffusion-based policies have gained significant popularity in Reinforcement Learning (RL) due to their ability to represent complex, non-Gaussian distributions. Stochastic Differential Equation (SDE)-based diffusion policies often rely on indirect entropy control due to the intractability of the exact entropy, while also suffering from computationally prohibitive policy gradients through the iterative denoising chain. To overcome these issues, we propose Flow Matching Policy with Entropy Regularization (FMER), an Ordinary Differential Equation (ODE)-based online RL framework. FMER parameterizes the policy via flow matching and samples actions along a straight probability path, motivated by optimal transport. FMER leverages the model's generative nature to construct an advantage-weighted target velocity field from a candidate set, steering policy updates toward high-value regions. By deriving a tractable entropy objective, FMER enables principled maximum-entropy optimization for enhanced exploration. Experiments on sparse multi-goal FrankaKitchen benchmarks demonstrate that FMER outperforms state-of-the-art methods, while remaining competitive on standard MuJoco benchmarks. Moreover, FMER reduces training time by 7x compared to heavy diffusion baselines (QVPO) and 10-15% relative to efficient variants.

摘要（中文）: 基于扩散的策略因其表示复杂、非高斯分布的能力，在强化学习（RL）中获得了显著的关注。基于随机微分方程（SDE）的扩散策略通常依赖于间接的熵控制，因为精确熵难以处理，同时也面临着通过迭代去噪链计算代价极高的策略梯度。为了克服这些问题，我们提出了一种基于常微分方程（ODE）的在线强化学习框架：带有熵正则化的流匹配策略（FMER）。 FMER通过流匹配参数化策略，并沿着一条受最优传输启发的直线概率路径采样动作。FMER利用模型的生成特性，从候选集中构建一个优势加权的目标速度场，引导策略更新朝着高价值区域。通过推导出一个易于处理的熵目标，FMER能够实现有原则的最大熵优化，以增强探索。在稀疏的多目标FrankaKitchen基准测试上的实验表明，FMER优于最先进的方法，同时在标准的MuJoco基准测试上保持竞争力。 此外，FMER相比重型扩散基线（QVPO）减少了7倍的训练时间，并且相比高效变体减少了10-15%。

TLDR: The paper introduces Flow Matching Policy with Entropy Regularization (FMER), an ODE-based online RL framework that improves exploration and reduces training time compared to diffusion-based policies, as demonstrated on FrankaKitchen and MuJoCo benchmarks.

简要说明: 本文介绍了Flow Matching Policy with Entropy Regularization (FMER)，一种基于常微分方程的在线强化学习框架。该框架通过改进探索并缩短训练时间，优于扩散策略，并在FrankaKitchen和MuJoCo基准测试中得到了验证。

Authors: Ting Gao, Stavros Orfanoudakis, Nan Lin, Elvin Isufi, Winnie Daamen, Serge Hoogendoorn

Complementary Reinforcement Learning

Abstract (English): Reinforcement Learning (RL) has emerged as a powerful paradigm for training LLM-based agents, yet remains limited by low sample efficiency, stemming not only from sparse outcome feedback but also from the agent's inability to leverage prior experience across episodes. While augmenting agents with historical experience offers a promising remedy, existing approaches suffer from a critical weakness: the experience distilled from history is either stored statically or fail to coevolve with the improving actor, causing a progressive misalignment between the experience and the actor's evolving capability that diminishes its utility over the course of training. Inspired by complementary learning systems in neuroscience, we present Complementary RL to achieve seamless co-evolution of an experience extractor and a policy actor within the RL optimization loop. Specifically, the actor is optimized via sparse outcome-based rewards, while the experience extractor is optimized according to whether its distilled experiences demonstrably contribute to the actor's success, thereby evolving its experience management strategy in lockstep with the actor's growing capabilities. Empirically, Complementary RL outperforms outcome-based agentic RL baselines that do not learn from experience, achieving 10% performance improvement in single-task scenarios and exhibits robust scalability in multi-task settings. These results establish Complementary RL as a paradigm for efficient experience-driven agent learning.

摘要（中文）: 强化学习(RL)已成为训练基于大型语言模型(LLM)的智能代理的强大范式，但仍受限于低样本效率，这不仅源于稀疏的结果反馈，还源于智能代理无法利用跨episode的历史经验。尽管使用历史经验增强智能代理提供了一种有希望的补救措施，但现有方法存在一个关键弱点：从历史中提取的经验要么静态存储，要么无法与不断改进的行动者(actor)协同进化，导致经验与行动者不断发展的能力之间逐渐失调，从而降低了其在训练过程中的效用。受到神经科学中互补学习系统的启发，我们提出了互补强化学习(Complementary RL)，以实现强化学习优化循环中经验提取器和策略行动者之间的无缝协同进化。具体而言，行动者通过基于稀疏结果的奖励进行优化，而经验提取器则根据其提取的经验是否能显著促进行动者的成功进行优化，从而与行动者不断增长的能力保持同步地发展其经验管理策略。经验表明，互补强化学习优于不从经验中学习的基于结果的智能代理强化学习基线，在单任务场景中性能提高10%，并在多任务设置中表现出强大的可扩展性。这些结果确立了互补强化学习作为一种高效的经验驱动智能代理学习范式。

TLDR: This paper introduces Complementary RL, a new reinforcement learning method that addresses sample efficiency by co-evolving an experience extractor and a policy actor, leading to performance improvements in single and multi-task scenarios.

简要说明: 本文介绍了互补强化学习(Complementary RL)，这是一种新的强化学习方法，通过共同进化经验提取器和策略行动者来解决样本效率问题，从而在单任务和多任务场景中提高性能。

Authors: Dilxat Muhtar, Jiashun Liu, Wei Gao, Weixun Wang, Shaopan Xiong, Ju Huang, Siran Yang, Wenbo Su, Jiamang Wang, Ling Pan, Bo Zheng

Efficient Soft Actor-Critic with LLM-Based Action-Level Guidance for Continuous Control

Abstract (English): We present GuidedSAC, a novel reinforcement learning (RL) algorithm that facilitates efficient exploration in vast state-action spaces. GuidedSAC leverages large language models (LLMs) as intelligent supervisors that provide action-level guidance for the Soft Actor-Critic (SAC) algorithm. The LLM-based supervisor analyzes the most recent trajectory using state information and visual replays, offering action-level interventions that enable targeted exploration. Furthermore, we provide a theoretical analysis of GuidedSAC, proving that it preserves the convergence guarantees of SAC while improving convergence speed. Through experiments in both discrete and continuous control environments, including toy text tasks and complex MuJoCo benchmarks, we demonstrate that GuidedSAC consistently outperforms standard SAC and state-of-the-art exploration-enhanced variants (e.g., RND, ICM, and E3B) in terms of sample efficiency and final performance.

摘要（中文）: 我们提出了GuidedSAC，一种新型强化学习（RL）算法，能够促进在广阔状态-动作空间中的高效探索。GuidedSAC利用大型语言模型（LLMs）作为智能监督器，为软演员-评论家（SAC）算法提供动作级别的指导。基于LLM的监督器通过使用状态信息和视觉回放分析最近的轨迹，提供动作级别的干预，从而实现有针对性的探索。此外，我们对GuidedSAC进行了理论分析，证明其在保留SAC收敛保证的同时，提高了收敛速度。通过在离散和连续控制环境中的实验，包括玩具文本任务和复杂的MuJoCo基准测试，我们证明了GuidedSAC在样本效率和最终性能方面始终优于标准SAC和最先进的探索增强变体（例如，RND、ICM和E3B）。

TLDR: GuidedSAC improves Soft Actor-Critic (SAC) by using an LLM to provide action-level guidance for more efficient exploration, outperforming standard SAC and other exploration methods in continuous control tasks.

简要说明: GuidedSAC通过使用大型语言模型（LLM）提供动作级别的指导来改进软演员-评论家（SAC）算法，从而实现更高效的探索，并在连续控制任务中优于标准SAC和其他探索方法。

Authors: Hao Ma, Zhiqiang Pu, Xiaolin Ai, Huimu Wang

WINFlowNets: Warm-up Integrated Networks Training of Generative Flow Networks for Robotics and Machine Fault Adaptation

Abstract (English): Generative Flow Networks for continuous scenarios (CFlowNets) have shown promise in solving sequential decision-making tasks by learning stochastic policies using a flow and a retrieval network. Despite their demonstrated efficiency compared to state-of-the-art Reinforcement Learning (RL) algorithms, their practical application in robotic control tasks is constrained by the reliance on pre-training the retrieval network. This dependency poses challenges in dynamic robotic environments, where pre-training data may not be readily available or representative of the current environment. This paper introduces WINFlowNets, a novel CFlowNets framework that enables the co-training of flow and retrieval networks. WINFlowNets begins with a warm-up phase for the retrieval network to bootstrap its policy, followed by a shared training architecture and a shared replay buffer for co-training both networks. Experiments in simulated robotic environments demonstrate that WINFlowNets surpasses CFlowNets and state-of-the-art RL algorithms in terms of average reward and training stability. Furthermore, WINFlowNets exhibits strong adaptive capability in fault environments, making it suitable for tasks that demand quick adaptation with limited sample data. These findings highlight WINFlowNets' potential for deployment in dynamic and malfunction-prone robotic systems, where traditional pre-training or sample inefficient data collection may be impractical.

摘要（中文）: 用于连续场景的生成式流网络（CFlowNets）通过学习使用流网络和检索网络的随机策略，在解决序列决策任务方面展现出潜力。 尽管与最先进的强化学习（RL）算法相比，它们已显示出效率，但由于依赖于预训练检索网络，它们在机器人控制任务中的实际应用受到限制。这种依赖性给动态机器人环境带来了挑战，在这种环境中，预训练数据可能不易获得或无法代表当前环境。本文介绍了一种新的CFlowNets框架WINFlowNets，该框架能够共同训练流网络和检索网络。 WINFlowNets首先进行检索网络的预热阶段，以引导其策略，然后采用共享的训练架构和共享的重放缓冲区来共同训练这两个网络。在模拟机器人环境中的实验表明，WINFlowNets在平均奖励和训练稳定性方面均优于CFlowNets和最先进的RL算法。 此外，WINFlowNets在故障环境中表现出强大的自适应能力，使其适用于需要快速适应且样本数据有限的任务。 这些发现凸显了WINFlowNets在容易出现故障的动态机器人系统中部署的潜力，在这种系统中，传统的预训练或低效的样本数据收集可能不切实际。

TLDR: The paper introduces WINFlowNets, a Generative Flow Network framework that enables co-training of flow and retrieval networks, improving performance and adaptation in robotic control tasks compared to CFlowNets and RL algorithms, especially in fault environments.

简要说明: 该论文介绍了WINFlowNets，一种生成流网络框架，可以共同训练流网络和检索网络，与CFlowNets和强化学习算法相比，提高了机器人控制任务的性能和适应性，尤其是在故障环境中。

Authors: Zahin Sufiyan, Shadan Golestan, Yoshihiro Mitsuka, Shotaro Miwa, Osmar Zaiane

MetaClaw: Just Talk -- An Agent That Meta-Learns and Evolves in the Wild

Abstract (English): Large language model (LLM) agents are increasingly used for complex tasks, yet deployed agents often remain static, failing to adapt as user needs evolve. This creates a tension between the need for continuous service and the necessity of updating capabilities to match shifting task distributions. On platforms like OpenClaw, which handle diverse workloads across 20+ channels, existing methods either store raw trajectories without distilling knowledge, maintain static skill libraries, or require disruptive downtime for retraining. We present MetaClaw, a continual meta-learning framework that jointly evolves a base LLM policy and a library of reusable behavioral skills. MetaClaw employs two complementary mechanisms. Skill-driven fast adaptation analyzes failure trajectories via an LLM evolver to synthesize new skills, enabling immediate improvement with zero downtime. Opportunistic policy optimization performs gradient-based updates via cloud LoRA fine-tuning and Reinforcement Learning with a Process Reward Model (RL-PRM). This is triggered during user-inactive windows by the Opportunistic Meta-Learning Scheduler (OMLS), which monitors system inactivity and calendar data. These mechanisms are mutually reinforcing: a refined policy generates better trajectories for skill synthesis, while richer skills provide higher-quality data for policy optimization. To prevent data contamination, a versioning mechanism separates support and query data. Built on a proxy-based architecture, MetaClaw scales to production-size LLMs without local GPUs. Experiments on MetaClaw-Bench and AutoResearchClaw show that skill-driven adaptation improves accuracy by up to 32% relative. The full pipeline advances Kimi-K2.5 accuracy from 21.4% to 40.6% and increases composite robustness by 18.3%. Code is available at https://github.com/aiming-lab/MetaClaw.

摘要（中文）: 大型语言模型 (LLM) 智能体正被越来越多地用于复杂任务，但已部署的智能体常常保持静态，无法随着用户需求的变化而适应。 这在持续服务的需求与更新能力以匹配变化的任务分布的必要性之间造成了紧张关系。 在 OpenClaw 等处理跨 20 多个渠道的各种工作负载的平台上，现有方法要么存储原始轨迹而不提炼知识，要么维护静态技能库，要么需要中断停机时间来重新训练。 我们提出了 MetaClaw，这是一个持续元学习框架，可以联合演化基础 LLM 策略和一个可重用的行为技能库。 MetaClaw 采用了两种互补机制。 技能驱动的快速适应通过 LLM 进化器分析失败轨迹以合成新技能，从而实现零停机时间的即时改进。 机会主义策略优化通过云 LoRA 微调和带有过程奖励模型 (RL-PRM) 的强化学习来执行基于梯度的更新。 这由机会主义元学习调度器 (OMLS) 在用户非活跃窗口期间触发，该调度器监控系统非活跃时间和日历数据。 这些机制是相互促进的：精炼的策略为技能合成生成更好的轨迹，而更丰富的技能为策略优化提供更高质量的数据。 为了防止数据污染，版本控制机制分离了支持数据和查询数据。 MetaClaw 基于代理架构构建，无需本地 GPU 即可扩展到生产规模的 LLM。 在 MetaClaw-Bench 和 AutoResearchClaw 上的实验表明，技能驱动的适应使准确率相对提高了高达 32%。 完整的流水线将 Kimi-K2.5 的准确率从 21.4% 提高到 40.6%，并将综合鲁棒性提高了 18.3%。 代码可在 https://github.com/aiming-lab/MetaClaw 获取。

TLDR: MetaClaw is a continual meta-learning framework for LLM agents that combines skill-driven fast adaptation with opportunistic policy optimization to enable continuous improvement and adaptation in real-world deployments without downtime, showing significant accuracy and robustness gains.

简要说明: MetaClaw是一个LLM Agent的持续元学习框架，它结合了技能驱动的快速适应和机会主义策略优化，能够在现实部署中实现持续改进和适应，无需停机，并显示出显著的准确性和鲁棒性提升。

Authors: Peng Xia, Jianwen Chen, Xinyu Yang, Haoqin Tu, Jiaqi Liu, Kaiwen Xiong, Siwei Han, Shi Qiu, Haonian Ji, Yuyin Zhou, Zeyu Zheng, Cihang Xie, Huaxiu Yao

Real-Time Online Learning for Model Predictive Control using a Spatio-Temporal Gaussian Process Approximation

Abstract (English): Learning-based model predictive control (MPC) can enhance control performance by correcting for model inaccuracies, enabling more precise state trajectory predictions than traditional MPC. A common approach is to model unknown residual dynamics as a Gaussian process (GP), which leverages data and also provides an estimate of the associated uncertainty. However, the high computational cost of online learning poses a major challenge for real-time GP-MPC applications. This work presents an efficient implementation of an approximate spatio-temporal GP model, offering online learning at constant computational complexity. It is optimized for GP-MPC, where it enables improved control performance by learning more accurate system dynamics online in real-time, even for time-varying systems. The performance of the proposed method is demonstrated by simulations and hardware experiments in the exemplary application of autonomous miniature racing.

摘要（中文）: 基于学习的模型预测控制 (MPC) 可以通过校正模型的不精确性来提高控制性能，从而实现比传统 MPC 更精确的状态轨迹预测。一种常见的方法是将未知的残余动力学建模为高斯过程 (GP)，该方法利用数据并提供相关不确定性的估计。然而，在线学习的高计算成本对实时 GP-MPC 应用提出了重大挑战。本文提出了一种高效的近似时空 GP 模型实现，该模型提供恒定计算复杂度的在线学习。它针对 GP-MPC 进行了优化，即使对于时变系统，也能通过实时在线学习更精确的系统动力学来提高控制性能。 所提出的方法的性能通过自主微型赛车这一典型应用中的仿真和硬件实验得到验证。

TLDR: This paper introduces an efficient spatio-temporal Gaussian Process approximation for real-time online learning in Model Predictive Control, demonstrated in autonomous miniature racing.

简要说明: 该论文介绍了一种高效的时空高斯过程近似方法，用于模型预测控制中的实时在线学习，并在自主微型赛车中进行了演示。

Authors: Lars Bartels, Amon Lahr, Andrea Carron, Melanie N. Zeilinger

DexEXO: A Wearability-First Dexterous Exoskeleton for Operator-Agnostic Demonstration and Learning

Abstract (English): Scaling dexterous robot learning is constrained by the difficulty of collecting high-quality demonstrations across diverse operators. Existing wearable interfaces often trade comfort and cross-user adaptability for kinematic fidelity, while embodiment mismatch between demonstration and deployment requires visual post-processing before policy training. We present DexEXO, a wearability-first hand exoskeleton that aligns visual appearance, contact geometry, and kinematics at the hardware level. DexEXO features a pose-tolerant thumb mechanism and a slider-based finger interface analytically modeled to support hand lengths from 140~mm to 217~mm, reducing operator-specific fitting and enabling scalable cross-operator data collection. A passive hand visually matches the deployed robot, allowing direct policy training from raw wrist-mounted RGB observations. User studies demonstrate improved comfort and usability compared to prior wearable systems. Using visually aligned observations alone, we train diffusion policies that achieve competitive performance while substantially simplifying the end-to-end pipeline. These results show that prioritizing wearability and hardware-level embodiment alignment reduces both human and algorithmic bottlenecks without sacrificing task performance. Project Page: https://dexexo-research.github.io/

摘要（中文）: 摘要： 灵巧机器人学习的扩展受到跨多个操作员收集高质量演示数据的难度的限制。现有的可穿戴界面通常牺牲舒适性和跨用户适应性来换取运动学保真度，而演示和部署之间的具身差异需要在策略训练之前进行视觉后处理。我们提出了DexEXO，一种将可穿戴性放在首位的手部外骨骼，可在硬件层面校准视觉外观、接触几何形状和运动学。DexEXO具有姿态容错拇指机构和基于滑块的手指界面，经过解析建模以支持从140毫米到217毫米的手长，从而减少了特定于操作员的拟合，并实现了可扩展的跨操作员数据收集。被动手部在视觉上与部署的机器人匹配，从而可以直接从原始腕载RGB观察数据进行策略训练。用户研究表明，与之前的可穿戴系统相比，舒适性和可用性有所提高。仅使用视觉对齐的观察数据，我们训练的扩散策略在大幅简化端到端流程的同时，实现了具有竞争力的性能。这些结果表明，优先考虑可穿戴性和硬件层面的具身校准可以减少人为和算法瓶颈，而不会牺牲任务性能。项目页面：https://dexexo-research.github.io/

Authors: Alvin Zhu, Mingzhang Zhu, Beom Jun Kim, Jose Victor S. H. Ramos, Yike Shi, Yufeng Wu, Raayan Dhar, Fuyi Yang, Ruochen Hou, Hanzhang Fang, Quanyou Wang, Yuchen Cui, Dennis W. Hong

Physics-informed offline reinforcement learning eliminates catastrophic fuel waste in maritime routing

Abstract (English): International shipping produces approximately 3% of global greenhouse gas emissions, yet voyage routing remains dominated by heuristic methods. We present PIER (Physics-Informed, Energy-efficient, Risk-aware routing), an offline reinforcement learning framework that learns fuel-efficient, safety-aware routing policies from physics-calibrated environments grounded in historical vessel tracking data and ocean reanalysis products, requiring no online simulator. Validated on one full year (2023) of AIS data across seven Gulf of Mexico routes (840 episodes per method), PIER reduces mean CO2 emissions by 10% relative to great-circle routing. However, PIER's primary contribution is eliminating catastrophic fuel waste: great-circle routing incurs extreme fuel consumption (>1.5x median) in 4.8% of voyages; PIER reduces this to 0.5%, a 9-fold reduction. Per-voyage fuel variance is 3.5x lower (p<0.001), with bootstrap 95% CI for mean savings [2.9%, 15.7%]. Partial validation against observed AIS vessel behavior confirms consistency with the fastest real transits while exhibiting 23.1x lower variance. Crucially, PIER is forecast-independent: unlike A* path optimization whose wave protection degrades 4.5x under realistic forecast uncertainty, PIER maintains constant performance using only local observations. The framework combines physics-informed state construction, demonstration-augmented offline data, and a decoupled post-hoc safety shield, an architecture that transfers to wildfire evacuation, aircraft trajectory optimization, and autonomous navigation in unmapped terrain.

摘要（中文）: 国际航运产生约占全球温室气体排放量的3%，但航线规划仍主要依赖于启发式方法。我们提出了PIER（物理信息驱动、节能、风险意识的航线规划），一种离线强化学习框架，该框架从基于历史船舶跟踪数据和海洋再分析产品进行物理校准的环境中学习高燃油效率、安全意识的航线规划策略，无需在线仿真器。通过在墨西哥湾七条航线（每种方法840个片段）上对完整的一年（2023年）AIS数据进行验证，PIER相对于大圆航线规划平均降低了10%的CO2排放。然而，PIER的主要贡献是消除了灾难性的燃料浪费：大圆航线规划在4.8%的航程中会产生极高的燃料消耗（>1.5倍中位数）；而PIER将这一比例降低到0.5%，减少了9倍。单次航程的燃料方差降低了3.5倍（p<0.001），平均节省量的Bootstrap 95%置信区间为[2.9%, 15.7%]。针对观测到的AIS船舶行为的部分验证证实了与最快的实际运输的一致性，同时表现出23.1倍的方差降低。至关重要的是，PIER不依赖于预报：与A*路径优化在实际预报不确定性下波浪防护性能下降4.5倍不同，PIER仅使用局部观测即可保持恒定的性能。该框架结合了物理信息驱动的状态构建、示范增强的离线数据以及解耦的后验安全屏障，这种架构可以迁移到野火疏散、飞机轨迹优化以及未测绘制地形中的自主导航。

TLDR: The paper introduces PIER, a physics-informed offline reinforcement learning framework for maritime routing that significantly reduces fuel consumption and eliminates catastrophic fuel waste compared to traditional methods, while also being robust to forecast uncertainty.

简要说明: 该论文介绍了一个名为PIER的基于物理信息的离线强化学习框架，用于海上航线规划。与传统方法相比，该框架显著降低了燃料消耗，并消除了灾难性燃料浪费，同时对预测不确定性具有鲁棒性。

Authors: Aniruddha Bora, Julie Chalfant, Chryssostomos Chryssostomidis

Neural Radiance Maps for Extraterrestrial Navigation and Path Planning

Abstract (English): Autonomous vehicles such as the Mars rovers currently lead the vanguard of surface exploration on extraterrestrial planets and moons. In order to accelerate the pace of exploration and science objectives, it is critical to plan safe and efficient paths for these vehicles. However, current rover autonomy is limited by a lack of global maps which can be easily constructed and stored for onboard re-planning. Recently, Neural Radiance Fields (NeRFs) have been introduced as a detailed 3D scene representation which can be trained from sparse 2D images and efficiently stored. We propose to use NeRFs to construct maps for online use in autonomous navigation, and present a planning framework which leverages the NeRF map to integrate local and global information. Our approach interpolates local cost observations across global regions using kernel ridge regression over terrain features extracted from the NeRF map, allowing the rover to re-route itself around untraversable areas discovered during online operation. We validate our approach in high-fidelity simulation and demonstrate lower cost and higher percentage success rate path planning compared to various baselines.

摘要（中文）: 如火星探测车之类的自主车辆目前引领着对外星行星和卫星表面探索的前沿。为了加快探索步伐和科学目标实现，为这些车辆规划安全高效的路径至关重要。然而，当前探测车的自主能力受到缺乏易于构建和存储以供车载重规划的全局地图的限制。 近期，神经辐射场(NeRFs)作为一种详细的3D场景表示方法被引入，它可以从稀疏的2D图像中进行训练并高效地存储。 我们提出使用NeRFs来构建用于自主导航的在线地图，并提出一个利用NeRF地图整合局部和全局信息的规划框架。 我们的方法使用核岭回归对从NeRF地图中提取的地形特征进行回归，从而在全局区域内插值局部代价观测，使得探测车能够在在线操作过程中绕行发现的不可穿越区域。 我们在高保真仿真中验证了我们的方法，并证明与各种基线方法相比，其路径规划具有更低的代价和更高的成功率。

Authors: Adam Dai, Shubh Gupta, Grace Gao

Full Stack Navigation, Mapping, and Planning for the Lunar Autonomy Challenge

Abstract (English): We present a modular, full-stack autonomy system for lunar surface navigation and mapping developed for the Lunar Autonomy Challenge. Operating in a GNSS-denied, visually challenging environment, our pipeline integrates semantic segmentation, stereo visual odometry, pose graph SLAM with loop closures, and layered planning and control. We leverage lightweight learning-based perception models for real-time segmentation and feature tracking and use a factor-graph backend to maintain globally consistent localization. High-level waypoint planning is designed to promote mapping coverage while encouraging frequent loop closures, and local motion planning uses arc sampling with geometric obstacle checks for efficient, reactive control. We evaluate our approach in the competition's high-fidelity lunar simulator, demonstrating centimeter-level localization accuracy, high-fidelity map generation, and strong repeatability across random seeds and rock distributions. Our solution achieved first place in the final competition evaluation.

摘要（中文）: 我们提出了一个模块化的、全栈自主系统，用于月球表面导航和测绘，专为月球自主挑战赛开发。该系统在GNSS拒止且视觉环境具有挑战性的情况下运行，我们的流程集成了语义分割、立体视觉里程计、具有闭环的姿态图SLAM，以及分层规划和控制。我们利用轻量级的基于学习的感知模型进行实时分割和特征跟踪，并使用因子图后端来维持全局一致的定位。高级航点规划旨在提高测绘覆盖率，同时鼓励频繁的闭环，而局部运动规划则使用弧采样和几何障碍物检测来进行高效、反应式的控制。我们在比赛的高保真月球模拟器中评估了我们的方法，证明了厘米级的定位精度、高保真地图生成以及跨随机种子和岩石分布的强大可重复性。我们的解决方案在最终的比赛评估中获得了第一名。

Authors: Adam Dai, Asta Wu, Keidai Iiyama, Guillem Casadesus Vila, Kaila Coimbra, Thomas Deng, Grace Gao

Visual SLAM with DEM Anchoring for Lunar Surface Navigation

Abstract (English): Future lunar missions will require autonomous rovers capable of traversing tens of kilometers across challenging terrain while maintaining accurate localization and producing globally consistent maps. However, the absence of global positioning systems, extreme illumination, and low-texture regolith make long-range navigation on the Moon particularly difficult, as visual-inertial odometry pipelines accumulate drift over extended traverses. To address this challenge, we present a stereo visual simultaneous localization and mapping (SLAM) system that integrates learned feature detection and matching with global constraints from digital elevation models (DEMs). Our front-end employs learning-based feature extraction and matching to achieve robustness to illumination extremes and repetitive terrain, while the back-end incorporates DEM-derived height and surface-normal factors into a pose graph, providing absolute surface constraints that mitigate long-term drift. We validate our approach using both simulated lunar traverse data generated in Unreal Engine and real Moon/Mars analog data collected from Mt. Etna. Results demonstrate that DEM anchoring consistently reduces absolute trajectory error compared to baseline SLAM methods, lowering drift in long-range navigation even in repetitive or visually aliased terrain.

摘要（中文）: 未来月球任务需要能够在具有挑战性的地形上行驶数十公里，同时保持精确定位并生成全局一致地图的自主漫游车。然而，由于缺乏全球定位系统，极端光照条件以及低纹理的月壤，月球上的远程导航变得尤为困难，因为视觉惯性里程计管道会在扩展的遍历过程中积累漂移。为了应对这一挑战，我们提出了一种立体视觉同步定位与地图构建（SLAM）系统，该系统集成了学习到的特征检测与匹配以及来自数字高程模型（DEM）的全局约束。我们的前端采用基于学习的特征提取和匹配，以实现对极端光照和重复地形的鲁棒性，而后端将DEM导出的高度和表面法向量因子集成到姿态图中，提供绝对表面约束，从而减轻长期漂移。我们使用在虚幻引擎中生成的模拟月球遍历数据和从埃特纳火山收集的真实月球/火星模拟数据来验证我们的方法。结果表明，与基准SLAM方法相比，DEM锚定能够持续降低绝对轨迹误差，即使在重复或视觉混叠的地形中，也能降低远程导航中的漂移。

TLDR: This paper presents a stereo visual SLAM system for lunar rovers that integrates learned feature detection/matching with DEM-derived constraints to improve long-range navigation accuracy and robustness in challenging lunar conditions.

简要说明: 这篇论文提出了一个用于月球车的立体视觉SLAM系统，该系统集成了学习到的特征检测/匹配与DEM衍生的约束，以提高在具有挑战性的月球环境中的远程导航精度和鲁棒性。

BEV-SLD: Self-Supervised Scene Landmark Detection for Global Localization with LiDAR Bird's-Eye View Images

Abstract (English): We present BEV-SLD, a LiDAR global localization method building on the Scene Landmark Detection (SLD) concept. Unlike scene-agnostic pipelines, our self-supervised approach leverages bird's-eye-view (BEV) images to discover scene-specific patterns at a prescribed spatial density and treat them as landmarks. A consistency loss aligns learnable global landmark coordinates with per-frame heatmaps, yielding consistent landmark detections across the scene. Across campus, industrial, and forest environments, BEV-SLD delivers robust localization and achieves strong performance compared to state-of-the-art methods.

摘要（中文）: 我们提出了BEV-SLD，一种基于场景地标检测（SLD）概念的激光雷达全局定位方法。与场景无关的流水线不同，我们的自监督方法利用鸟瞰图（BEV）图像，以预定的空间密度发现场景特定的模式，并将其视为地标。一致性损失将可学习的全局地标坐标与每帧热图对齐，从而产生场景中一致的地标检测。在校园、工业和森林环境中，BEV-SLD 能够实现稳健的定位，并与最先进的方法相比，表现出强大的性能。
