Authors: David Skuddis, Vincent Ress, Wei Zhang, Vincent Ofosu Nyako, Norbert Haala

TrackDeform3D: Markerless and Autonomous 3D Keypoint Tracking and Dataset Collection for Deformable Objects

Abstract (English): Structured 3D representations such as keypoints and meshes offer compact, expressive descriptions of deformable objects, jointly capturing geometric and topological information useful for downstream tasks such as dynamics modeling and motion planning. However, robustly extracting such representations remains challenging, as current perception methods struggle to handle complex deformations. Moreover, large-scale 3D data collection remains a bottleneck: existing approaches either require prohibitive data collection efforts, such as labor-intensive annotation or expensive motion capture setups, or rely on simplifying assumptions that break down in unstructured environments. As a result, large-scale 3D datasets and benchmarks for deformable objects remain scarce. To address these challenges, this paper presents an affordable and autonomous framework for collecting 3D datasets of deformable objects using only RGB-D cameras. The proposed method identifies 3D keypoints and robustly tracks their trajectories, incorporating motion consistency constraints to produce temporally smooth and geometrically coherent data. TrackDeform3D is evaluated against several state-of-the-art tracking methods across diverse object categories and demonstrates consistent improvements in both geometric and tracking accuracy. Using this framework, this paper presents a high-quality, large-scale dataset consisting of 6 deformable objects, totaling 110 minutes of trajectory data.

摘要（中文）: 结构化的3D表示，如关键点和网格，为形变物体提供了紧凑、富有表现力的描述，共同捕捉了几何和拓扑信息，这些信息对于下游任务（如动力学建模和运动规划）非常有价值。然而，鲁棒地提取这种表示仍然具有挑战性，因为当前的感知方法难以处理复杂的形变。此外，大规模3D数据采集仍然是一个瓶颈：现有的方法要么需要极高的数据采集成本，例如劳动密集型标注或昂贵的动作捕捉设备，要么依赖于在非结构化环境中失效的简化假设。因此，针对形变物体的大规模3D数据集和基准仍然稀缺。为解决这些挑战，本文提出了一种经济且自主的框架，仅使用RGB-D相机即可采集形变物体的3D数据集。该方法识别3D关键点并鲁棒地跟踪它们的轨迹，结合运动一致性约束以生成时间上平滑且几何上连贯的数据。TrackDeform3D在多个对象类别上与几种最先进的跟踪方法进行了评估，并在几何和跟踪精度方面均表现出持续的改进。利用此框架，本文提出了一个高质量、大规模的数据集，包含6个形变物体，总计110分钟的轨迹数据。

TLDR: The paper presents TrackDeform3D, a markerless and autonomous RGB-D framework for 3D keypoint tracking and dataset collection of deformable objects, addressing the scarcity of large-scale 3D datasets for deformable object research.

简要说明: 该论文介绍了TrackDeform3D，一个无标记且自主的RGB-D框架，用于可变形物体的3D关键点跟踪和数据集收集，旨在解决可变形物体研究中大规模3D数据集稀缺的问题。

Authors: Yeheng Zong, Yizhou Chen, Alexander Bowler, Chia-Tung Yang, Ram Vasudevan

TeleDex: Accessible Dexterous Teleoperation

Abstract (English): Despite increasing dataset scale and model capacity, robot manipulation policies still struggle to generalize beyond their training distributions. As a result, deploying state-of-the-art policies in new environments, tasks, or robot embodiments often requires collecting additional demonstrations. Enabling this in real-world deployment settings requires tools that allow users to collect demonstrations quickly, affordably, and with minimal setup. We present TeleDex, an open-source system for intuitive teleoperation of dexterous hands and robotic manipulators using any readily available phone. The system streams low-latency 6-DoF wrist poses and articulated 21-DoF hand state estimates from the phone, which are retargeted to robot arms and multi-fingered hands without requiring external tracking infrastructure. TeleDex supports both a handheld phone-only mode and an optional 3D-printable hand-mounted interface for finger-level teleoperation. By lowering the hardware and setup barriers to dexterous teleoperation, TeleDex enables users to quickly collect demonstrations during deployment to support policy fine-tuning. We evaluate the system across simulation and real-world manipulation tasks, demonstrating its effectiveness as a unified scalable interface for robot teleoperation. All software and hardware designs, along with demonstration videos, are open-source and available at orayyan.com/teledex.

摘要（中文）: 尽管数据集规模和模型容量不断增加，但机器人操作策略仍然难以将其泛化能力扩展到训练分布之外。因此，在新的环境、任务或机器人本体中部署最先进的策略通常需要收集额外的演示数据。要在实际部署环境中实现这一点，需要工具能够让用户以快速、经济且设置最少的方式收集演示数据。我们提出TeleDex，这是一个开源系统，可以使用任何现成的手机对灵巧手和机器人操作器进行直观的遥操作。该系统从手机上流式传输低延迟的6自由度腕部姿态和铰接的21自由度手部状态估计，这些数据被重定向到机器人手臂和多指手上，无需外部跟踪基础设施。TeleDex同时支持仅手持手机模式，以及可选的3D打印的手部安装界面以实现指尖级别的遥操作。通过降低灵巧遥操作的硬件和设置门槛，TeleDex使用户能够在部署期间快速收集演示数据，以支持策略微调。我们在模拟和真实世界的操作任务中评估了该系统，证明了其作为机器人遥操作的统一可扩展接口的有效性。所有软件和硬件设计，以及演示视频，都是开源的，可在orayyan.com/teledex上获取。

TLDR: TeleDex is an open-source system using a phone for low-latency, 6-DoF wrist pose and 21-DoF hand state teleoperation, enabling quick and affordable data collection for robot manipulation policy fine-tuning, featuring both handheld and hand-mounted options.

Authors: Omar Rayyan, Maximilian Gillesm, Yuchen Cui

Contingency-Aware Planning via Certified Neural Hamilton-Jacobi Reachability

Abstract (English): Hamilton-Jacobi (HJ) reachability provides formal safety guarantees for dynamical systems, but solving high-dimensional HJ partial differential equations limits its use in real-time planning. This paper presents a contingency-aware multi-goal navigation framework that integrates learning-based reachability with sampling-based planning in unknown environments. We use Fourier Neural Operator (FNO) to approximate the solution operator of the Hamilton-Jacobi-Isaacs variational inequality under varying obstacle configurations. We first provide a theoretical under-approximation guarantee on the safe backward reach-avoid set, which enables formal safety certification of the learned reachable sets. Then, we integrate the certified reachable sets with an incremental multi-goal planner, which enforces reachable-set constraints and a recovery policy that guarantees finite-time return to a safe region. Overall, we demonstrate that the proposed framework achieves asymptotically optimal navigation with provable contingency behavior, and validate its performance through real-time deployment on KUKA's youBot in Webots simulation.

摘要（中文）: Hamilton-Jacobi (HJ)可达性为动力系统提供形式化的安全保证，但求解高维HJ偏微分方程限制了其在实时规划中的应用。本文提出了一种情境感知多目标导航框架，该框架将基于学习的可达性与基于采样的规划相结合，应用于未知环境。我们使用傅里叶神经算子(FNO)来近似 Hamilton-Jacobi-Isaacs变分不等式在不同障碍物配置下的解算子。我们首先提供安全后向可达避让集的理论下近似保证，从而能够对学习到的可达集进行形式化的安全认证。然后，我们将经过认证的可达集与增量式多目标规划器集成，该规划器强制执行可达集约束以及保证有限时间返回安全区域的恢复策略。总而言之，我们证明了所提出的框架实现了渐近最优的导航，并具有可证明的情境行为，并且通过在Webots仿真环境中于KUKA的youBot机器人的实时部署验证了其性能。

TLDR: This paper presents a framework for safe, asymptotically optimal navigation in unknown environments by integrating learning-based Hamilton-Jacobi reachability (using Fourier Neural Operators) with sampling-based planning, offering provable safety guarantees and demonstrated on a physical robot.

简要说明: 该论文提出了一个在未知环境中实现安全且渐近最优导航的框架，通过将基于学习的 Hamilton-Jacobi 可达性（使用傅里叶神经算子）与基于采样的规划相结合，提供可证明的安全保证，并在物理机器人上进行了演示。

Authors: Kasidit Muenprasitivej, Derya Aksaray

TDAD: Test-Driven Agentic Development - Reducing Code Regressions in AI Coding Agents via Graph-Based Impact Analysis

Abstract (English): AI coding agents can resolve real-world software issues, yet they frequently introduce regressions -- breaking tests that previously passed. Current benchmarks focus almost exclusively on resolution rate, leaving regression behavior under-studied. This paper presents TDAD (Test-Driven Agentic Development), an open-source tool that performs pre-change impact analysis for AI coding agents. TDAD builds a dependency map between source code and tests so that before committing a patch, the agent knows which tests to verify and can self-correct. The map is delivered as a lightweight agent skill -- a static text file the agent queries at runtime. Evaluated on SWE-bench Verified with two open-weight models running on consumer hardware (Qwen3-Coder 30B, 100 instances; Qwen3.5-35B-A3B, 25 instances), TDAD reduced regressions by 70% (6.08% to 1.82%) compared to a vanilla baseline. In contrast, adding TDD procedural instructions without targeted test context increased regressions to 9.94% -- worse than no intervention at all. When deployed as an agent skill with a different model and framework, TDAD improved issue-resolution rate from 24% to 32%, confirming that surfacing contextual information outperforms prescribing procedural workflows. All code, data, and logs are publicly available at https://github.com/pepealonso95/TDAD.

摘要（中文）: AI代码智能体能够解决现实世界的软件问题，但它们经常引入回归错误——导致之前通过的测试失败。目前的基准测试几乎只关注解决率，而对回归行为的研究不足。本文提出TDAD（测试驱动的智能体开发），这是一个开源工具，用于对AI代码智能体进行变更前的影响分析。TDAD构建了源代码和测试之间的依赖关系图，以便在提交补丁之前，智能体知道要验证哪些测试并进行自我纠正。该图以轻量级智能体技能的形式交付--一个静态文本文件，智能体在运行时查询。在SWE-bench Verified上，使用运行在消费级硬件上的两个开放权重模型(Qwen3-Coder 30B, 100个实例; Qwen3.5-35B-A3B, 25个实例)进行评估，与原始基线相比，TDAD将回归错误减少了70% (从6.08%降至1.82%)。相比之下，在没有针对性测试上下文的情况下添加TDD程序性指令，反而将回归错误增加到9.94%——比完全不干预更糟糕。当作为智能体技能部署到不同模型和框架上时，TDAD将问题解决率从24%提高到32%，证实了提供上下文信息优于规定程序化工作流程。所有代码、数据和日志都可以在https://github.com/pepealonso95/TDAD上公开获取。

TLDR: The paper introduces TDAD, a tool that reduces code regressions in AI coding agents by using graph-based impact analysis to inform test verification before code commitment, showing significant improvements in regression reduction and issue resolution.

简要说明: 该论文介绍了TDAD，一种通过图分析的影响分析来减少AI代码生成代理中代码回归的工具，该工具在代码提交前告知测试验证，并显示出回归减少和问题解决方面的显著改进。

Authors: Pepe Alonso, Sergio Yovine, Victor A. Braberman

Procedural Generation of Algorithm Discovery Tasks in Machine Learning

Abstract (English): Automating the development of machine learning algorithms has the potential to unlock new breakthroughs. However, our ability to improve and evaluate algorithm discovery systems has thus far been limited by existing task suites. They suffer from many issues, such as: poor evaluation methodologies; data contamination; and containing saturated or very similar problems. Here, we introduce DiscoGen, a procedural generator of algorithm discovery tasks for machine learning, such as developing optimisers for reinforcement learning or loss functions for image classification. Motivated by the success of procedural generation in reinforcement learning, DiscoGen spans millions of tasks of varying difficulty and complexity from a range of machine learning fields. These tasks are specified by a small number of configuration parameters and can be used to optimise algorithm discovery agents (ADAs). We present DiscoBench, a benchmark consisting of a fixed, small subset of DiscoGen tasks for principled evaluation of ADAs. Finally, we propose a number of ambitious, impactful research directions enabled by DiscoGen, in addition to experiments demonstrating its use for prompt optimisation of an ADA. DiscoGen is released open-source at https://github.com/AlexGoldie/discogen.

摘要（中文）: 自动化机器学习算法的开发具有释放新突破的潜力。然而，我们改进和评估算法发现系统的能力，迄今为止一直受到现有任务套件的限制。它们存在诸多问题，例如：评估方法不完善；数据污染；以及包含饱和或非常相似的问题。在此，我们介绍DiscoGen，一种用于机器学习算法发现任务的过程化生成器，例如开发用于强化学习的优化器或用于图像分类的损失函数。受到过程化生成在强化学习中取得成功的启发，DiscoGen涵盖了数百万个来自各种机器学习领域、难度和复杂度各异的任务。这些任务由少量配置参数指定，可用于优化算法发现代理（ADA）。我们提出DiscoBench，这是一个由DiscoGen任务的固定、小子集构成的基准测试，用于对 ADA 进行有原则的评估。最后，除了展示其用于ADA提示优化的实验外，我们还提出了由DiscoGen支持的若干雄心勃勃、具有影响力的研究方向。DiscoGen以开源形式发布于https://github.com/AlexGoldie/discogen。

TLDR: The paper introduces DiscoGen, a procedurally generated benchmark for evaluating algorithm discovery agents across diverse machine learning tasks, addressing limitations in existing task suites. It offers millions of tasks with varying difficulty and includes DiscoBench for standardized evaluation.

CodeScout: An Effective Recipe for Reinforcement Learning of Code Search Agents

Abstract (English): A prerequisite for coding agents to perform tasks on large repositories is code localization - the identification of relevant files, classes, and functions to work on. While repository-level code localization has been performed using embedding-based retrieval approaches such as vector search, recent work has focused on developing agents to localize relevant code either as a standalone precursor to or interleaved with performing actual work. Most prior methods on agentic code search equip the agent with complex, specialized tools, such as repository graphs derived from static analysis. In this paper, we demonstrate that, with an effective reinforcement learning recipe, a coding agent equipped with nothing more than a standard Unix terminal can be trained to achieve strong results. Our experiments on three benchmarks (SWE-Bench Verified, Pro, and Lite) reveal that our models consistently achieve superior or competitive performance over 2-18x larger base and post-trained LLMs and sometimes approach performance provided by closed models like Claude Sonnet, even when using specialized scaffolds. Our work particularly focuses on techniques for re-purposing existing coding agent environments for code search, reward design, and RL optimization. We release the resulting model family, CodeScout, along with all our code and data for the community to build upon.

摘要（中文）: 编码智能体在大规模代码仓库中执行任务的一个前提是代码定位——识别相关的文件、类和函数以便进行操作。虽然仓库级别的代码定位已经通过诸如向量搜索等基于嵌入的检索方法实现，但最近的工作集中于开发智能体以定位相关代码，无论作为独立的前置步骤，还是与实际工作交织进行。大多数先前关于智能体代码搜索的方法都为智能体配备了复杂、专门的工具，例如从静态分析导出的仓库图。在本文中，我们证明，通过有效的强化学习方案，仅配备标准 Unix 终端的编码智能体可以训练至取得优异的结果。我们在三个基准测试 (SWE-Bench Verified、Pro 和 Lite) 上的实验表明，我们的模型始终取得优于或可与 2-18 倍更大的基础和后训练 LLM 相媲美的性能，有时甚至接近诸如 Claude Sonnet 等封闭模型的性能，即使在使用专门的脚手架时也是如此。我们的工作特别关注于将现有编码智能体环境重新用于代码搜索、奖励设计和 RL 优化的技术。我们发布了由此产生的模型家族 CodeScout，以及我们所有的代码和数据，供社区在此基础上进行构建。

TLDR: The paper introduces CodeScout, a reinforcement learning-based code search agent using only a standard Unix terminal. It achieves strong performance on code search benchmarks, outperforming larger LLMs and approaching closed-source models without specialized tools.

FailureMem: A Failure-Aware Multimodal Framework for Autonomous Software Repair

Abstract (English): Multimodal Automated Program Repair (MAPR) extends traditional program repair by requiring models to jointly reason over source code, textual issue descriptions, and visual artifacts such as GUI screenshots. While recent LLM-based repair systems have shown promising results, existing approaches face several limitations: rigid workflow pipelines restrict exploration during debugging, visual reasoning is often performed over full-page screenshots without localized grounding, and failed repair attempts are rarely transformed into reusable knowledge. To address these challenges, we propose FailureMem, a multimodal repair framework that integrates three key mechanisms: a hybrid workflow-agent architecture that balances structured localization with flexible reasoning, active perception tools that enable region-level visual grounding, and a Failure Memory Bank that converts past repair attempts into reusable guidance. Experiments on SWE-bench Multimodal demonstrate FailureMem improves the resolved rate over GUIRepair by 3.7%.

Authors: Ruize Ma, Yilei Jiang, Shilin Zhang, Zheng Ma, Yi Feng, Vincent Ng, Zhi Wang, Xiangyu Yue, Chuanyi Li, Lewei Lu

Can Blindfolded LLMs Still Trade? An Anonymization-First Framework for Portfolio Optimization

Abstract (English): For LLM trading agents to be genuinely trustworthy, they must demonstrate understanding of market dynamics rather than exploitation of memorized ticker associations. Building responsible multi-agent systems demands rigorous signal validation: proving that predictions reflect legitimate patterns, not pre-trained recall. We address two sources of spurious performance: memorization bias from ticker-specific pre-training, and survivorship bias from flawed backtesting. Our approach is to blindfold the agents--anonymizing all identifiers--and verify whether meaningful signals persist. BlindTrade anonymizes tickers and company names, and four LLM agents output scores along with reasoning. We construct a GNN graph from reasoning embeddings and trade using PPO-DSR policy. On 2025 YTD (through 2025-08-01), we achieved Sharpe 1.40 +/- 0.22 across 20 seeds and validated signal legitimacy through negative control experiments. To assess robustness beyond a single OOS window, we additionally evaluate an extended period (2024--2025), revealing market-regime dependency: the policy excels in volatile conditions but shows reduced alpha in trending bull markets.

摘要（中文）: 为了使大型语言模型交易代理真正值得信赖，它们必须展现对市场动态的理解，而非利用记忆的股票代码关联。构建负责任的多代理系统需要严格的信号验证：证明预测反映了合理的模式，而不是预训练的记忆回溯。我们针对两个虚假性能来源进行了处理：来自特定股票代码预训练的记忆偏差，以及来自有缺陷的回测的幸存者偏差。我们的方法是蒙住代理的眼睛——匿名化所有标识符——并验证是否有意义的信号依旧存在。“盲交易”（BlindTrade）匿名化了股票代码和公司名称，而四个大型语言模型代理输出分数以及推理过程。我们从推理嵌入构建了一个图神经网络（GNN）图，并使用PPO-DSR策略进行交易。在2025年初至今（直至2025-08-01）的数据上，我们在20个随机种子中实现了1.40 +/- 0.22 的夏普比率，并通过负控制实验验证了信号的合法性。为了评估超出单个样本外窗口的稳健性，我们还评估了一个更长的时期（2024-2025），揭示了市场机制依赖性：该策略在波动条件下表现出色，但在趋势性牛市中显示出降低的阿尔法。

TLDR: The paper introduces BlindTrade, an anonymization-first framework for portfolio optimization using LLMs, demonstrating that these models can still generate meaningful trading signals even when blinded to ticker-specific information, suggesting genuine understanding of market dynamics.

简要说明: 本文介绍了一种名为 BlindTrade 的匿名化优先框架，用于使用 LLM 进行投资组合优化。该框架表明，即使 LLM 不知道股票代码的具体信息，也能生成有意义的交易信号，这表明 LLM 确实理解了市场动态。

Authors: Joohyoung Jeon, Hongchul Lee

Post-Training Local LLM Agents for Linux Privilege Escalation with Verifiable Rewards

Abstract (English): LLM agents are increasingly relevant to research domains such as vulnerability discovery. Yet, the strongest systems remain closed and cloud-only, making them resource-intensive, difficult to reproduce, and unsuitable for work involving proprietary code or sensitive data. Consequently, there is an urgent need for small, local models that can perform security tasks under strict resource budgets, but methods for developing them remain underexplored. In this paper, we address this gap by proposing a two-stage post-training pipeline. We focus on the problem of Linux privilege escalation, where success is automatically verifiable and the task requires multi-step interactive reasoning. Using an experimental setup that prevents data leakage, we post-train a 4B model in two stages: supervised fine-tuning on traces from procedurally generated privilege-escalation environments, followed by reinforcement learning with verifiable rewards. On a held-out benchmark of 12 Linux privilege-escalation scenarios, supervised fine-tuning alone more than doubles the baseline success rate at 20 rounds, and reinforcement learning further lifts our resulting model, PrivEsc-LLM, to 95.8%, nearly matching Claude Opus 4.6 at 97.5%. At the same time, the expected inference cost per successful escalation is reduced by over 100x.

摘要（中文）: LLM智能体在诸如漏洞发现等研究领域正变得越来越重要。然而，最强大的系统仍然是封闭的、仅限云端，这导致资源密集、难以复现，并且不适用于涉及专有代码或敏感数据的工作。因此，迫切需要能够在严格资源预算下执行安全任务的小型本地模型，但开发此类模型的方法仍未得到充分探索。在本文中，我们提出了一种两阶段的后训练流程来解决这一缺口。我们专注于Linux权限提升问题，该问题的成功案例可以自动验证，且该任务需要多步骤的交互式推理。通过使用一种防止数据泄露的实验设置，我们对一个40亿参数的模型进行两阶段的后训练：首先，在程序化生成的权限提升环境的轨迹上进行有监督的微调；然后，使用可验证的奖励进行强化学习。在一个包含12个Linux权限提升场景的保留基准测试中，仅有监督的微调就使20轮时的基线成功率提高了一倍多，而强化学习进一步提升了我们得到的模型PrivEsc-LLM，使其达到95.8%，几乎与Claude Opus 4.6的97.5%相匹配。与此同时，每次成功提升的预期推理成本降低了100倍以上。

TLDR: The paper presents a two-stage post-training pipeline (SFT + RL) for a 4B local LLM to achieve near state-of-the-art performance on Linux privilege escalation with verifiable rewards, while significantly reducing inference costs.

简要说明: 该论文提出一个两阶段后训练流程 (SFT + RL)，用于训练一个 4B 的本地 LLM，在 Linux 权限提升任务上实现接近最先进的性能，且具有可验证的奖励，同时显著降低了推理成本。

Authors: Philipp Normann, Andreas Happe, Jürgen Cito, Daniel Arp

Identifying Latent Actions and Dynamics from Offline Data via Demonstrator Diversity

Abstract (English): Can latent actions and environment dynamics be recovered from offline trajectories when actions are never observed? We study this question in a setting where trajectories are action-free but tagged with demonstrator identity. We assume that each demonstrator follows a distinct policy, while the environment dynamics are shared across demonstrators and identity affects the next observation only through the chosen action. Under these assumptions, the conditional next-observation distribution $p(o_{t+1}\mid o_t,e)$ is a mixture of latent action-conditioned transition kernels with demonstrator-specific mixing weights. We show that this induces, for each state, a column-stochastic nonnegative matrix factorization of the observable conditional distribution. Using sufficiently scattered policy diversity and rank conditions, we prove that the latent transitions and demonstrator policies are identifiable up to permutation of the latent action labels. We extend the result to continuous observation spaces via a Gram-determinant minimum-volume criterion, and show that continuity of the transition map over a connected state space upgrades local permutation ambiguities to a single global permutation. A small amount of labeled action data then suffices to fix this final ambiguity. These results establish demonstrator diversity as a principled source of identifiability for learning latent actions and dynamics from offline RL data.

摘要（中文）: 在动作从未被观察到的情况下，能否从离线轨迹中恢复潜在动作和环境动力学？我们研究了在轨迹无动作但标记有示范者身份的场景下的这个问题。我们假设每个示范者遵循不同的策略，而环境动力学在所有示范者之间共享，且身份仅通过所选动作影响下一个观测。在这些假设下，条件下一个观测分布$p(o_{t+1}\mid o_t,e)$是潜在动作条件转移核的混合，其具有示范者特定的混合权重。我们证明，这对于每个状态，都会诱导可观测条件分布的列随机非负矩阵分解。利用充分分散的策略多样性和秩条件，我们证明了潜在转移和示范者策略是可识别的，直至潜在动作标签的置换。 我们通过格拉姆行列式最小体积准则将结果推广到连续观测空间，并表明连通状态空间上转移映射的连续性将局部置换模糊性提升为单个全局置换。少量标记的动作数据就足以消除这最后的模糊性。这些结果确立了示范者多样性作为离线强化学习数据中学习潜在动作和动力学的一个原则性可识别性来源。

TLDR: This paper proposes a method to recover latent actions and environment dynamics from offline trajectory data by leveraging demonstrator diversity, proving identifiability under specific conditions and extending the result to continuous observation spaces.

简要说明: 该论文提出了一种利用演示者多样性从离线轨迹数据中恢复潜在动作和环境动态的方法。文章证明了在特定条件下可识别性，并将结果扩展到连续观测空间。

Authors: Felix Schur

Per-Domain Generalizing Policies: On Learning Efficient and Robust Q-Value Functions (Extended Version with Technical Appendix)

Abstract (English): Learning per-domain generalizing policies is a key challenge in learning for planning. Standard approaches learn state-value functions represented as graph neural networks using supervised learning on optimal plans generated by a teacher planner. In this work, we advocate for learning Q-value functions instead. Such policies are drastically cheaper to evaluate for a given state, as they need to process only the current state rather than every successor. Surprisingly, vanilla supervised learning of Q-values performs poorly as it does not learn to distinguish between the actions taken and those not taken by the teacher. We address this by using regularization terms that enforce this distinction, resulting in Q-value policies that consistently outperform state-value policies across a range of 10 domains and are competitive with the planner LAMA-first.

摘要（中文）: 学习特定领域泛化的策略是规划学习中的一个关键挑战。标准方法学习状态值函数，该函数用图神经网络表示，并使用教师规划器生成的最优计划进行监督学习。在这项工作中，我们提倡学习Q值函数。 对于给定的状态，评估这种策略的成本大大降低，因为它们只需要处理当前状态，而不需要处理每个后继状态。 令人惊讶的是，Q值的原始监督学习表现不佳，因为它无法区分教师采取的行动和未采取的行动。 我们通过使用正则化项来强制执行这种区分来解决这个问题，从而得到在一系列10个领域中始终优于状态值策略，并且与规划器LAMA-first具有竞争力的Q值策略。

TLDR: This paper explores learning per-domain generalizing policies using Q-value functions instead of state-value functions for more efficient planning, and introduces regularization techniques to improve Q-value learning performance to be competitive with a baseline planner.

简要说明: 本文探索了使用Q值函数代替状态值函数来学习每个领域的通用策略，以实现更有效的规划，并引入了正则化技术来提高Q值学习性能，使其与基线规划器具有竞争力。

Authors: Nicola J. Müller, Moritz Oster, Isabel Valera, Jörg Hoffmann, Timo P. Gros

Enhancing Reinforcement Learning Fine-Tuning with an Online Refiner

Abstract (English): Constraints are essential for stabilizing reinforcement learning fine-tuning (RFT) and preventing degenerate outputs, yet they inherently conflict with the optimization objective because stronger constraints limit the ability of a fine-tuned model to discover better solutions. We propose \textit{dynamic constraints} that resolve this tension by adapting to the evolving capabilities of the fine-tuned model based on the insight that constraints should only intervene when degenerate outputs occur. We implement this by using a reference model as an \textit{online refiner} that takes the response from the fine-tuned model and generates a minimally corrected version which preserves correct content verbatim while fixing errors. A supervised fine-tuning loss then trains the fine-tuned model to produce the refined output. This mechanism yields a constraint that automatically strengthens or relaxes based on output quality. Experiments on dialogue and code generation show that dynamic constraints outperform both KL regularization and unconstrained baselines, achieving substantially higher task rewards while maintaining training stability.

摘要（中文）: 约束对于稳定强化学习微调（RFT）和防止退化输出至关重要，但它们本质上与优化目标相冲突，因为更强的约束会限制微调模型发现更好解决方案的能力。我们提出了\textit{动态约束}，通过根据微调模型不断演化的能力进行调整来解决这种紧张关系，其依据是约束只应在发生退化输出时进行干预。我们通过使用参考模型作为\textit{在线精炼器}来实现这一点，该精炼器接收来自微调模型的响应，并生成一个最小修正的版本，该版本逐字保留正确内容，同时修复错误。然后，有监督的微调损失训练微调模型以产生精炼后的输出。这种机制产生了一个约束，该约束会根据输出质量自动加强或放松。在对话和代码生成方面的实验表明，动态约束优于KL正则化和无约束基线，在保持训练稳定性的同时，实现了显著更高的任务奖励。

TLDR: The paper introduces dynamic constraints for reinforcement learning fine-tuning (RFT) using an online refiner to adaptively strengthen or relax constraints based on output quality, outperforming traditional methods in dialogue and code generation.

简要说明: 该论文介绍了一种用于强化学习微调（RFT）的动态约束方法，该方法使用在线精炼器来根据输出质量自适应地加强或放松约束，在对话和代码生成方面优于传统方法。

Authors: Hao Ma, Zhiqiang Pu, Yang Liu, Xiaolin Ai

VirPro: Visual-referred Probabilistic Prompt Learning for Weakly-Supervised Monocular 3D Detection

Abstract (English): Monocular 3D object detection typically relies on pseudo-labeling techniques to reduce dependency on real-world annotations. Recent advances demonstrate that deterministic linguistic cues can serve as effective auxiliary weak supervision signals, providing complementary semantic context. However, hand-crafted textual descriptions struggle to capture the inherent visual diversity of individuals across scenes, limiting the model's ability to learn scene-aware representations. To address this challenge, we propose Visual-referred Probabilistic Prompt Learning (VirPro), an adaptive multi-modal pretraining paradigm that can be seamlessly integrated into diverse weakly supervised monocular 3D detection frameworks. Specifically, we generate a diverse set of learnable, instance-conditioned prompts across scenes and store them in an Adaptive Prompt Bank (APB). Subsequently, we introduce Multi-Gaussian Prompt Modeling (MGPM), which incorporates scene-based visual features into the corresponding textual embeddings, allowing the text prompts to express visual uncertainties. Then, from the fused vision-language embeddings, we decode a prompt-targeted Gaussian, from which we derive a unified object-level prompt embedding for each instance. RoI-level contrastive matching is employed to enforce modality alignment, bringing embeddings of co-occurring objects within the same scene closer in the latent space, thus enhancing semantic coherence. Extensive experiments on the KITTI benchmark demonstrate that integrating our pretraining paradigm consistently yields substantial performance gains, achieving up to a 4.8% average precision improvement than the baseline.

摘要（中文）: 单目3D目标检测通常依赖于伪标签技术来降低对真实世界标注的依赖。近期的进展表明，确定性的语言线索可以作为有效的辅助弱监督信号，提供互补的语义上下文。然而，手工设计的文本描述难以捕捉不同场景下个体的内在视觉多样性，限制了模型学习场景感知表示的能力。为了应对这一挑战，我们提出了一种视觉参照概率提示学习（VirPro），这是一种自适应的多模态预训练范式，可以无缝集成到各种弱监督单目3D检测框架中。具体来说，我们跨场景生成一组多样化的、可学习的、实例条件化的提示，并将它们存储在一个自适应提示库（APB）中。随后，我们引入多高斯提示建模（MGPM），将基于场景的视觉特征融合到相应的文本嵌入中，使文本提示能够表达视觉不确定性。然后，从融合的视觉-语言嵌入中，我们解码一个以提示为目标的高斯分布，从中为每个实例导出一个统一的目标级别提示嵌入。采用RoI级别的对比匹配来强制模态对齐，使同一场景中共现物体的嵌入在潜在空间中更接近，从而增强语义连贯性。在KITTI基准数据集上的大量实验表明，集成我们的预训练范式能够持续产生显著的性能提升，平均精度比基线模型提高了高达4.8%。

TLDR: This paper introduces VirPro, a visual-referred probabilistic prompt learning method for weakly-supervised monocular 3D object detection, leveraging scene-aware visual features to generate informative text prompts and improve performance on the KITTI benchmark.

简要说明: 本文介绍了一种名为 VirPro 的视觉引导概率提示学习方法，用于弱监督单目 3D 物体检测。该方法利用场景感知的视觉特征生成信息丰富的文本提示，并在 KITTI 基准测试中提高了性能。

Authors: Chupeng Liu, Jiyong Rao, Shangquan Sun, Runkai Zhao, Weidong Cai

AdaZoom-GUI: Adaptive Zoom-based GUI Grounding with Instruction Refinement

Abstract (English): GUI grounding is a critical capability for vision-language models (VLMs) that enables automated interaction with graphical user interfaces by locating target elements from natural language instructions. However, grounding on GUI screenshots remains challenging due to high-resolution images, small UI elements, and ambiguous user instructions. In this work, we propose AdaZoom-GUI, an adaptive zoom-based GUI grounding framework that improves both localization accuracy and instruction understanding. Our approach introduces an instruction refinement module that rewrites natural language commands into explicit and detailed descriptions, allowing the grounding model to focus on precise element localization. In addition, we design a conditional zoom-in strategy that selectively performs a second-stage inference on predicted small elements, improving localization accuracy while avoiding unnecessary computation and context loss on simpler cases. To support this framework, we construct a high-quality GUI grounding dataset and train the grounding model using Group Relative Policy Optimization (GRPO), enabling the model to predict both click coordinates and element bounding boxes. Experiments on public benchmarks demonstrate that our method achieves state-of-the-art performance among models with comparable or even larger parameter sizes, highlighting its effectiveness for high-resolution GUI understanding and practical GUI agent deployment.

摘要（中文）: GUI接驳是视觉-语言模型(VLMs)的一项关键能力，它通过从自然语言指令中定位目标元素，来实现与图形用户界面(GUI)的自动化交互。然而，由于高分辨率图像、微小的UI元素和含糊不清的用户指令，在GUI截图上进行接驳仍然具有挑战性。在这项工作中，我们提出了AdaZoom-GUI，一种基于自适应缩放的GUI接驳框架，可以提高定位精度和指令理解能力。我们的方法引入了一个指令细化模块，将自然语言命令重写为明确且详细的描述，从而使接驳模型能够专注于精确的元素定位。此外，我们设计了一种条件缩放策略，有选择地对预测的小元素执行第二阶段推理，提高定位精度的同时，避免了在较简单的情况下进行不必要的计算和上下文损失。为了支持此框架，我们构建了一个高质量的GUI接驳数据集，并使用组相对策略优化(GRPO)训练接驳模型，使模型能够预测点击坐标和元素bounding box。在公开基准测试上的实验表明，我们的方法在参数量相当甚至更大的模型中实现了最state-of-the-art的性能，突出了其在高分辨率GUI理解和实际GUI代理部署中的有效性。

TLDR: The paper introduces AdaZoom-GUI, an adaptive zoom-based GUI grounding framework with instruction refinement, achieving state-of-the-art performance on GUI grounding tasks by improving localization accuracy and instruction understanding.

简要说明: 该论文介绍了AdaZoom-GUI，一个基于自适应缩放的GUI基础框架，具有指令细化功能，通过提高定位精度和指令理解能力，在GUI基础任务上实现了最先进的性能。

Authors: Siqi Pei, Liang Tang, Tiaonan Duan, Long Chen, Shuxian Li, Kaer Huang, Yanzhe Jing, Yiqiang Yan, Bo Zhang, Chenghao Jiang, Borui Zhang, Jiwen Lu

Caging the Agents: A Zero Trust Security Architecture for Autonomous AI in Healthcare

Abstract (English): Autonomous AI agents powered by large language models are being deployed in production with capabilities including shell execution, file system access, database queries, and multi-party communication. Recent red teaming research demonstrates that these agents exhibit critical vulnerabilities in realistic settings: unauthorized compliance with non-owner instructions, sensitive information disclosure, identity spoofing, cross-agent propagation of unsafe practices, and indirect prompt injection through external resources [7]. In healthcare environments processing Protected Health Information, every such vulnerability becomes a potential HIPAA violation. This paper presents a security architecture deployed for nine autonomous AI agents in production at a healthcare technology company. We develop a six-domain threat model for agentic AI in healthcare covering credential exposure, execution capability abuse, network egress exfiltration, prompt integrity failures, database access risks, and fleet configuration drift. We implement four-layer defense in depth: (1) kernel level workload isolation using gVisor on Kubernetes, (2) credential proxy sidecars preventing agent containers from accessing raw secrets, (3) network egress policies restricting each agent to allowlisted destinations, and (4) a prompt integrity framework with structured metadata envelopes and untrusted content labeling. We report results from 90 days of deployment including four HIGH severity findings discovered and remediated by an automated security audit agent, progressive fleet hardening across three VM image generations, and defense coverage mapped to all eleven attack patterns from recent literature. All configurations, audit tooling, and the prompt integrity framework are released as open source.

摘要（中文）: 由大型语言模型驱动的自主AI智能体正在生产环境中部署，其能力包括shell执行、文件系统访问、数据库查询和多方通信。近期红队研究表明，这些智能体在现实环境中表现出严重的安全漏洞：未经授权地服从非所有者指令、敏感信息泄露、身份欺骗、跨智能体传播不安全行为以及通过外部资源进行间接的提示注入[7]。在处理受保护健康信息的医疗保健环境中，每一个此类漏洞都可能构成违反HIPAA的行为。本文提出了一种安全架构，已在一家医疗技术公司部署于九个生产环境中的自主AI智能体。我们为医疗保健领域的智能体Agentic AI开发了一个六域威胁模型，涵盖凭据暴露、执行能力滥用、网络出口数据渗漏、prompt完整性失败、数据库访问风险和集群配置漂移。我们实施了四层纵深防御：（1）在Kubernetes上使用gVisor进行内核级工作负载隔离，（2）凭据代理sidecar，防止智能体容器访问原始密钥，（3）网络出口策略，将每个智能体限制在允许列表中的目标，以及（4）具有结构化元数据信封和不受信任内容标签的prompt完整性框架。我们报告了90天部署的结果，包括由自动化安全审计智能体发现并修复的四个高危漏洞、跨三个VM镜像代的渐进式集群加固，以及防御覆盖映射到近期文献中的所有十一种攻击模式。所有配置、审计工具和prompt完整性框架均以开源形式发布。

TLDR: The paper presents a zero-trust security architecture for autonomous AI agents in healthcare, addressing critical vulnerabilities and potential HIPAA violations. It details a defense-in-depth implementation with open-sourced configurations and audit tooling.

简要说明: 该论文提出了一种用于医疗保健领域自主AI代理的零信任安全架构，解决了关键漏洞和潜在的HIPAA违规问题。它详细介绍了一个深度防御实施方案，并开源了配置和审计工具。

Authors: Saikat Maiti

Graph-Native Cognitive Memory for AI Agents: Formal Belief Revision Semantics for Versioned Memory Architectures

Abstract (English): While individual components for AI agent memory exist in prior systems, their architectural synthesis and formal grounding remain underexplored. We present Kumiho, a graph-native cognitive memory architecture grounded in formal belief revision semantics. The structural primitives required for cognitive memory -- immutable revisions, mutable tag pointers, typed dependency edges, URI-based addressing -- are identical to those required for managing agent-produced work as versionable assets, enabling a unified graph-native architecture that serves both purposes. The central formal contribution is a correspondence between the AGM belief revision framework and the operational semantics of a property graph memory system, proving satisfaction of the basic AGM postulates (K*2--K*6) and Hansson's belief base postulates (Relevance, Core-Retainment). The architecture implements a dual-store model (Redis working memory, Neo4j long-term graph) with hybrid fulltext and vector retrieval. On LoCoMo (token-level F1), Kumiho achieves 0.565 overall F1 (n=1,986) including 97.5% adversarial refusal accuracy. On LoCoMo-Plus, a Level-2 cognitive memory benchmark testing implicit constraint recall, Kumiho achieves 93.3% judge accuracy (n=401); independent reproduction by the benchmark authors yielded results in the mid-80% range, still substantially outperforming all published baselines (best: Gemini 2.5 Pro, 45.7%). Three architectural innovations drive the results: prospective indexing (LLM-generated future-scenario implications indexed at write time), event extraction (structured causal events preserved in summaries), and client-side LLM reranking. The architecture is model-decoupled: switching the answer model from GPT-4o-mini (~88%) to GPT-4o (93.3%) improves end-to-end accuracy without pipeline changes, at a total evaluation cost of ~$14 for 401 entries.

摘要（中文）: 尽管先前的系统中已存在用于AI代理记忆的各个组件，但它们的架构合成和形式化基础仍未得到充分探索。我们提出Kumiho，一种基于形式化信念修正语义的图原生认知记忆架构。认知记忆所需的结构原语——不可变修订、可变标签指针、类型化依赖边、基于URI的寻址——与管理代理生成的、可版本化资产的工作所需的结构原语相同，从而实现了一种统一的图原生架构，可同时服务于这两种目的。核心的形式化贡献是AGM信念修正框架与属性图记忆系统的操作语义之间的对应关系，证明了基本AGM公理(K*2--K*6)和Hansson信念基础公理(相关性、核心保留)的满足。该架构实现了一种双存储模型（Redis工作内存，Neo4j长期图），具有混合全文和向量检索功能。 在LoCoMo（token级别F1）上，Kumiho的总F1值达到0.565 (n=1,986)，包括97.5%的对抗性拒绝准确率。在LoCoMo-Plus上，这是一个测试隐式约束回忆的Level-2认知记忆基准，Kumiho达到了93.3%的评判准确率(n=401)；基准作者的独立复现结果在80%区间中段，仍然大幅超越所有已发表的基线（最佳：Gemini 2.5 Pro，45.7%）。 三项架构创新推动了这些结果：前瞻性索引（在写入时索引LLM生成的未来场景含义）、事件提取（保存在摘要中的结构化因果事件）和客户端LLM重新排序。该架构是模型解耦的：将答案模型从GPT-4o-mini（~88%）切换到GPT-4o（93.3%）无需更改管道即可提高端到端准确率，评估401个条目的总成本约为14美元。

TLDR: The paper introduces Kumiho, a graph-native cognitive memory architecture for AI agents that combines long-term and working memory with formal belief revision semantics, achieving state-of-the-art performance on cognitive memory benchmarks. The architecture leverages prospective indexing, event extraction, and client-side LLM reranking and is model-decoupled.

简要说明: 该论文介绍了一种名为Kumiho的图原生认知记忆架构，该架构结合了长期和工作记忆，并具有形式化的信念修正语义，在认知记忆基准测试中实现了最先进的性能。该架构利用前瞻性索引、事件提取和客户端LLM重新排序，并且模型解耦。

Authors: Young Bin Park

Interpretable Traffic Responsibility from Dashcam Video via Legal Multi Agent Reasoning

Abstract (English): The widespread adoption of dashcams has made video evidence in traffic accidents increasingly abundant, yet transforming "what happened in the video" into "who is responsible under which legal provisions" still relies heavily on human experts. Existing ego-view traffic accident studies mainly focus on perception and semantic understanding, while LLM-based legal methods are mostly built on textual case descriptions and rarely incorporate video evidence, leaving a clear gap between the two. We first propose C-TRAIL, a multimodal legal dataset that, under the Chinese traffic regulation system, explicitly aligns dashcam videos and textual descriptions with a closed set of responsibility modes and their corresponding Chinese traffic statutes. On this basis, we introduce a two-stage framework: (1) a traffic accident understanding module that generates textual video descriptions; and (2) a legal multi-agent framework that outputs responsibility modes, statute sets, and complete judgment reports. Experimental results on C-TRAIL and MM-AU show that our method outperforms general and legal LLMs, as well as existing agent-based approaches, while providing a transparent and interpretable legal reasoning process.

摘要（中文）: 行车记录仪的广泛应用使得交通事故中的视频证据日益丰富，然而将“视频中发生了什么”转化为“根据哪些法律条款谁应该负责任”仍然高度依赖于人类专家。现有的自视交通意外研究主要集中在感知和语义理解上，而基于大语言模型的法律方法则大多建立在文本案例描述之上，很少纳入视频证据，这二者之间存在明显的差距。我们首先提出了C-TRAIL，一个多模态法律数据集，它在中国交通法规体系下，将行车记录仪视频和文本描述与一组封闭的责任模式及其相应的中国交通法规明确对齐。在此基础上，我们引入了一个两阶段框架：（1）一个生成文本视频描述的交通事故理解模块；以及（2）一个输出责任模式、法规集合和完整判决报告的法律多智能体框架。在C-TRAIL和MM-AU上的实验结果表明，我们的方法优于通用和法律大语言模型，以及现有的基于智能体的方法，同时提供了一个透明且可解释的法律推理过程。

TLDR: This paper introduces a multimodal legal dataset (C-TRAIL) and a two-stage framework for inferring traffic responsibility from dashcam videos using legal multi-agent reasoning, outperforming existing methods.

Authors: Jingchun Yang, Jinchang Zhang

Exploring parameter-efficient fine-tuning (PEFT) of billion-parameter vision models with QLoRA and DoRA: insights into generalization for limited-data image classification under a 98:1 test-to-train regime

Abstract (English): Automated behavior classification is essential for precision livestock farming but faces challenges of high computational costs and limited labeled data. This study systematically compared three approaches: training from scratch (ResNet-18, ViT-Small), frozen feature extraction, and parameter-efficient fine-tuning (PEFT) of the DINOv3 foundation model (6.7 billion parameters). We evaluated QLoRA and DoRA across multiple configurations varying rank (8, 16, 64) and target modules (q_proj versus all-linear layers). With 2,160 verified training images, we assessed generalization of our model on 211,800 test samples, which is essentially a 98:1 test-to-train ratio. Results demonstrated that PEFT substantially outperformed alternatives, where the best QLoRA configuration (all-linear layers and rank=64) achieved 83.16% test accuracy with only 2.72% parameters (183.0M) in 5.8 hours, compared to 72.87% for ResNet-18 (16.8 hours), 61.91% for ViT-Small (18.7 hours), and 76.56% for frozen DINOv3 (17.5 hours). DoRA achieved comparable accuracy (83.14%) but with longer training time (11.0 hours). Notably, increasing adapter capacity consistently improved generalization while simultaneously not causing overfitting: reducing rank from 16 to 8 decreased test accuracy from 78.38% to 77.17%, while expanding from q_proj-only to all-linear layers with rank=64 improved accuracy from 78.38% to 83.16%. This suggests underfitting, instead of overfitting, is the primary challenge when adapting foundation models to agricultural imagery. Our findings provide guidelines for deploying billion-parameter vision models with PEFT in agricultural livestock applications.

摘要（中文）: 自动化行为分类对于精准畜牧业至关重要，但面临着计算成本高昂和标注数据有限的挑战。本研究系统地比较了三种方法：从头训练（ResNet-18，ViT-Small）、冻结特征提取以及DINOv3基础模型（67亿参数）的参数高效微调(PEFT)。我们评估了在不同配置下（秩为8、16、64）以及不同目标模块（q_proj与所有线性层）的QLoRA和DoRA。 在2160张经过验证的训练图像的基础上，我们评估了模型在211800个测试样本上的泛化能力，本质上测试集与训练集的比例为98:1。结果表明，PEFT明显优于其他方法，其中最佳QLoRA配置（所有线性层且秩=64）在5.8小时内仅用2.72%的参数（1.83亿）就达到了83.16%的测试准确率，而ResNet-18为72.87%（16.8小时），ViT-Small为61.91%（18.7小时），冻结DINOv3为76.56%（17.5小时）。DoRA获得了相当的准确率（83.14%），但训练时间更长（11.0小时）。 值得注意的是，增加适配器容量持续提高了泛化能力，同时没有导致过拟合：将秩从16降至8会导致测试准确率从78.38%降至77.17%，而将秩=64的适配层从仅q_proj扩展到所有线性层则将准确率从78.38%提高到83.16%。这表明，在将基础模型应用于农业图像时，欠拟合而非过拟合是主要挑战。我们的研究结果为在农业畜牧应用中部署具有PEFT的十亿参数视觉模型提供了指导。

TLDR: This paper explores parameter-efficient fine-tuning (PEFT) techniques, specifically QLoRA and DoRA, on a large vision model (DINOv3) for image classification in a limited-data agricultural livestock setting, demonstrating significant performance gains over traditional methods.

简要说明: 本文探讨了参数高效微调 (PEFT) 技术，特别是在大型视觉模型 (DINOv3) 上使用 QLoRA 和 DoRA，用于 ограниченные 数据农业畜牧环境下的图像分类，结果表明与传统方法相比性能显著提升。

Authors: Haiyu Yang, Sumit Sharma, Enhong Liu, Miel Hostens

PC-CrossDiff: Point-Cluster Dual-Level Cross-Modal Differential Attention for Unified 3D Referring and Segmentation

Abstract (English): 3D Visual Grounding (3DVG) aims to localize the referent of natural language referring expressions through two core tasks: Referring Expression Comprehension (3DREC) and Segmentation (3DRES). While existing methods achieve high accuracy in simple, single-object scenes, they suffer from severe performance degradation in complex, multi-object scenes that are common in real-world settings, hindering practical deployment. Existing methods face two key challenges in complex, multi-object scenes: inadequate parsing of implicit localization cues critical for disambiguating visually similar objects, and ineffective suppression of dynamic spatial interference from co-occurring objects, resulting in degraded grounding accuracy. To address these challenges, we propose PC-CrossDiff, a unified dual-task framework with a dual-level cross-modal differential attention architecture for 3DREC and 3DRES. Specifically, the framework introduces: (i) Point-Level Differential Attention (PLDA) modules that apply bidirectional differential attention between text and point clouds, adaptively extracting implicit localization cues via learnable weights to improve discriminative representation; (ii) Cluster-Level Differential Attention (CLDA) modules that establish a hierarchical attention mechanism to adaptively enhance localization-relevant spatial relationships while suppressing ambiguous or irrelevant spatial relations through a localization-aware differential attention block. Our method achieves state-of-the-art performance on the ScanRefer, NR3D, and SR3D benchmarks. Notably, on the Implicit subsets of ScanRefer, it improves the Overall@0.50 score by +10.16% for the 3DREC task, highlighting its strong ability to parse implicit spatial cues.

摘要（中文）: 3D视觉定位（3DVG）旨在通过两个核心任务：指代表达式理解（3DREC）和分割（3DRES），来定位自然语言指代表达式的所指对象。虽然现有方法在简单、单对象场景中实现了高精度，但在现实世界中常见的复杂、多对象场景中，性能会严重下降，从而阻碍了实际部署。在复杂、多对象场景中，现有方法面临两个关键挑战：对隐式定位线索的解析不足，而这些线索对于区分视觉上相似的对象至关重要；以及对来自共现对象的动态空间干扰抑制不足，导致定位精度降低。为了应对这些挑战，我们提出了PC-CrossDiff，一个统一的双任务框架，其具有双层跨模态差分注意力架构，用于3DREC和3DRES。具体来说，该框架引入了：（i）点级差分注意力（PLDA）模块，该模块在文本和点云之间应用双向差分注意力，通过可学习的权重自适应地提取隐式定位线索，以提高判别表示能力；（ii）聚类级差分注意力（CLDA）模块，该模块建立了一种分层注意力机制，通过一个定位感知的差分注意力块自适应地增强与定位相关的空间关系，同时抑制模糊或不相关的空间关系。我们的方法在ScanRefer、NR3D 和 SR3D 基准测试中均实现了最先进的性能。值得注意的是，在 ScanRefer 的隐式子集上，它将3DREC任务的 Overall@0.50 分数提高了 +10.16%，突显了其强大的解析隐式空间线索的能力。

TLDR: The paper introduces PC-CrossDiff, a novel point cloud-based method that uses dual-level cross-modal differential attention to improve 3D referring expression comprehension and segmentation, especially in complex scenes with multiple objects. It achieves state-of-the-art results on multiple benchmarks.

简要说明: 该论文介绍了PC-CrossDiff，一种新颖的点云方法，使用双层跨模态差分注意力来提升3D指代表达理解和分割能力，尤其是在复杂的多物体场景中。该方法在多个基准测试中取得了最优效果。

Authors: Wenbin Tan, Jiawen Lin, Fangyong Wang, Yuan Xie, Yong Xie, Yachao Zhang, Yanyun Qu

AR-CoPO: Align Autoregressive Video Generation with Contrastive Policy Optimization

Abstract (English): Streaming autoregressive (AR) video generators combined with few-step distillation achieve low-latency, high-quality synthesis, yet remain difficult to align via reinforcement learning from human feedback (RLHF). Existing SDE-based GRPO methods face challenges in this setting: few-step ODEs and consistency model samplers deviate from standard flow-matching ODEs, and their short, low-stochasticity trajectories are highly sensitive to initialization noise, rendering intermediate SDE exploration ineffective. We propose AR-CoPO (AutoRegressive Contrastive Policy Optimization), a framework that adapts the Neighbor GRPO contrastive perspective to streaming AR generation. AR-CoPO introduces chunk-level alignment via a forking mechanism that constructs neighborhood candidates at a randomly selected chunk, assigns sequence-level rewards, and performs localized GRPO updates. We further propose a semi-on-policy training strategy that complements on-policy exploration with exploitation over a replay buffer of reference rollouts, improving generation quality across domains. Experiments on Self-Forcing demonstrate that AR-CoPO improves both out-of-domain generalization and in-domain human preference alignment over the baseline, providing evidence of genuine alignment rather than reward hacking.

摘要（中文）: 流式自回归 (AR) 视频生成器与少步蒸馏相结合可以实现低延迟、高质量的合成，但仍然难以通过基于人类反馈的强化学习 (RLHF) 进行对齐。现有的基于 SDE 的 GRPO 方法在这种设置下面临挑战：少步 ODE 和一致性模型采样器偏离了标准流匹配 ODE，并且它们短的、低随机性的轨迹对初始化噪声高度敏感，导致中间 SDE 的探索无效。我们提出了 AR-CoPO（自回归对比策略优化），这是一个将邻域 GRPO 的对比视角应用于流式 AR 生成的框架。AR-CoPO 通过一种分叉机制引入了块级别对齐，该机制在随机选择的块处构建邻域候选，分配序列级别奖励，并执行局部 GRPO 更新。我们进一步提出了一种半在策略训练策略，通过在策略探索与对参考推出回放缓冲区的利用相结合，从而提高跨领域的生成质量。在 Self-Forcing 上的实验表明，与基线相比，AR-CoPO 提高了域外泛化能力和域内人类偏好对齐，提供了真实对齐而非奖励破解的证据。

TLDR: The paper introduces AR-CoPO, a contrastive policy optimization framework for aligning autoregressive video generation with human feedback, addressing the limitations of existing reinforcement learning methods in this setting by improving both out-of-domain generalization and in-domain human preference alignment.

简要说明: 该论文介绍了AR-CoPO，一种对比策略优化框架，用于将自回归视频生成与人类反馈对齐。它通过改善域外泛化能力和域内人类偏好对齐来解决现有强化学习方法在此设置中的局限性。

Authors: Dailan He, Guanlin Feng, Xingtong Ge, Yi Zhang, Bingqi Ma, Guanglu Song, Yu Liu, Hongsheng Li

VisionNVS: Self-Supervised Inpainting for Novel View Synthesis under the Virtual-Shift Paradigm

Abstract (English): A fundamental bottleneck in Novel View Synthesis (NVS) for autonomous driving is the inherent supervision gap on novel trajectories: models are tasked with synthesizing unseen views during inference, yet lack ground truth images for these shifted poses during training. In this paper, we propose VisionNVS, a camera-only framework that fundamentally reformulates view synthesis from an ill-posed extrapolation problem into a self-supervised inpainting task. By introducing a ``Virtual-Shift'' strategy, we use monocular depth proxies to simulate occlusion patterns and map them onto the original view. This paradigm shift allows the use of raw, recorded images as pixel-perfect supervision, effectively eliminating the domain gap inherent in previous approaches. Furthermore, we address spatial consistency through a Pseudo-3D Seam Synthesis strategy, which integrates visual data from adjacent cameras during training to explicitly model real-world photometric discrepancies and calibration errors. Experiments demonstrate that VisionNVS achieves superior geometric fidelity and visual quality compared to LiDAR-dependent baselines, offering a robust solution for scalable driving simulation.

摘要（中文）: 用于自动驾驶的新视角合成(NVS)的一个根本瓶颈在于新型轨迹上固有的监督差距：模型需要在推理时合成未见过的视角，但在训练过程中，这些偏移姿态却缺乏真实的地面实况图像。在本文中，我们提出VisionNVS，一个纯视觉框架，从根本上将视角合成从一个不适定的外推问题，重新定义为一个自监督的图像修复任务。通过引入“虚拟偏移”策略，我们使用单目深度代理来模拟遮挡模式，并将它们映射到原始视角。这种范式转变允许使用原始记录的图像作为像素级完美监督，有效消除了先前方法中固有的领域差距。此外，我们通过伪3D缝合合成策略来解决空间一致性问题，该策略在训练期间整合来自相邻摄像头的视觉数据，以明确地建模真实世界的光度差异和校准误差。实验表明，与依赖激光雷达的基线方法相比，VisionNVS实现了卓越的几何保真度和视觉质量，为可扩展的驾驶模拟提供了一种强大的解决方案。

TLDR: VisionNVS introduces a self-supervised novel view synthesis framework that converts the problem into an inpainting task using a 'Virtual-Shift' strategy and pseudo-3D seam synthesis, achieving superior performance compared to LiDAR-dependent baselines.

简要说明: VisionNVS 提出了一个自监督的新视角合成框架，通过使用“虚拟位移”策略和伪 3D 接缝合成，将问题转化为修复任务，与依赖激光雷达的基线相比，实现了卓越的性能。

Authors: Hongbo Lu, Liang Yao, Chenghao He, Fan Liu, Wenlong Liao, Tao He, Pai Peng

OnlineHMR: Video-based Online World-Grounded Human Mesh Recovery

Abstract (English): Human mesh recovery (HMR) models 3D human body from monocular videos, with recent works extending it to world-coordinate human trajectory and motion reconstruction. However, most existing methods remain offline, relying on future frames or global optimization, which limits their applicability in interactive feedback and perception-action loop scenarios such as AR/VR and telepresence. To address this, we propose OnlineHMR, a fully online framework that jointly satisfies four essential criteria of online processing, including system-level causality, faithfulness, temporal consistency, and efficiency. Built upon a two-branch architecture, OnlineHMR enables streaming inference via a causal key-value cache design and a curated sliding-window learning strategy. Meanwhile, a human-centric incremental SLAM provides online world-grounded alignment under physically plausible trajectory correction. Experimental results show that our method achieves performance comparable to existing chunk-based approaches on the standard EMDB benchmark and highly dynamic custom videos, while uniquely supporting online processing. Page and code are available at https://tsukasane.github.io/Video-OnlineHMR/.

摘要（中文）: 人类网格恢复 (HMR) 模型从单目视频中重建 3D 人体，最近的研究将其扩展到世界坐标的人体轨迹和运动重建。然而，大多数现有方法仍然是离线的，依赖于未来的帧或全局优化，这限制了它们在交互式反馈和感知-行动循环场景中的应用，例如增强现实/虚拟现实和远程呈现。为了解决这个问题，我们提出了 OnlineHMR，一个完全在线的框架，它共同满足了在线处理的四个基本标准，包括系统级的因果性、保真性、时间一致性和效率。基于一个双分支架构，OnlineHMR 通过因果键值缓存设计和精选的滑动窗口学习策略来实现流式推理。同时，以人为中心的增量 SLAM 提供了物理上合理的轨迹校正下的在线世界坐标对齐。实验结果表明，我们的方法在标准的 EMDB 基准测试和高度动态的自定义视频上实现了与现有基于分块的方法相当的性能，同时独特地支持在线处理。网页和代码可在 https://tsukasane.github.io/Video-OnlineHMR/ 获取。

TLDR: The paper introduces OnlineHMR, a novel online framework for world-grounded human mesh recovery from monocular videos, addressing the limitations of existing offline methods in interactive applications.

简要说明: 本文介绍了OnlineHMR，一种新颖的在线框架，用于从单目视频中进行世界坐标下的人体网格重建，解决了现有离线方法在交互式应用中的局限性。

Authors: Yiwen Zhao, Ce Zheng, Yufu Wang, Hsueh-Han Daniel Yang, Liting Wen, Laszlo A. Jeni

DesertFormer: Transformer-Based Semantic Segmentation for Off-Road Desert Terrain Classification in Autonomous Navigation Systems

Abstract (English): Reliable terrain perception is a fundamental requirement for autonomous navigation in unstructured, off-road environments. Desert landscapes present unique challenges due to low chromatic contrast between terrain categories, extreme lighting variability, and sparse vegetation that defy the assumptions of standard road-scene segmentation models. We present DesertFormer, a semantic segmentation pipeline for off-road desert terrain analysis based on SegFormer B2 with a hierarchical Mix Transformer (MiT-B2) backbone. The system classifies terrain into ten ecologically meaningful categories -- Trees, Lush Bushes, Dry Grass, Dry Bushes, Ground Clutter, Flowers, Logs, Rocks, Landscape, and Sky -- enabling safety-aware path planning for ground robots and autonomous vehicles. Trained on a purpose-built dataset of 4,176 annotated off-road images at 512x512 resolution, DesertFormer achieves a mean Intersection-over-Union (mIoU) of 64.4% and pixel accuracy of 86.1%, representing a +24.2% absolute improvement over a DeepLabV3 MobileNetV2 baseline (41.0% mIoU). We further contribute a systematic failure analysis identifying the primary confusion patterns -- Ground Clutter to Landscape and Dry Grass to Landscape -- and propose class-weighted training and copy-paste augmentation for rare terrain categories. Code, checkpoints, and an interactive inference dashboard are released at https://github.com/Yasaswini-ch/Vision-based-Desert-Terrain-Segmentation-using-SegFormer.

摘要（中文）: 可靠的地形感知是在非结构化越野环境中实现自主导航的基本要求。沙漠景观由于地形类别之间色度对比度低、极端的光照变化以及稀疏的植被，对标准的道路场景分割模型提出了独特的挑战，这些挑战否定了其假设。我们提出了DesertFormer，一种用于越野沙漠地形分析的语义分割流水线，基于SegFormer B2架构，采用层次化的Mix Transformer (MiT-B2) 作为骨干网络。该系统将地形分为十种生态学上有意义的类别——树木、繁茂灌木、干草、干燥灌木、地表杂物、花卉、木材、岩石、景观和天空——从而为地面机器人和自动驾驶车辆实现安全感知的路径规划。 DesertFormer在专门构建的包含4176张512x512分辨率的带标注越野图像的数据集上进行训练，实现了64.4%的平均交并比(mIoU)和86.1%的像素精度，相比于DeepLabV3 MobileNetV2基线模型(41.0% mIoU)有+24.2%的绝对提升。我们进一步贡献了一个系统的失败分析，识别了主要的混淆模式——地表杂物到景观以及干草到景观——并提出了针对罕见地形类别的类别加权训练和复制粘贴增强方法。代码、模型检查点和一个交互式推理仪表板已在https://github.com/Yasaswini-ch/Vision-based-Desert-Terrain-Segmentation-using-SegFormer上发布。

TLDR: DesertFormer is a semantic segmentation pipeline utilizing SegFormer for classifying desert terrain into ecologically meaningful categories, achieving significant performance improvements over a DeepLabV3 baseline. They also release code, checkpoints, and an interactive dashboard.

简要说明: DesertFormer是一个语义分割流水线，利用SegFormer将沙漠地形分类为具有生态意义的类别，相对于DeepLabV3基线实现了显著的性能提升。 同时，他们发布了代码、检查点和一个交互式推理面板。

Authors: Yasaswini Chebolu

PaAgent: Portrait-Aware Image Restoration Agent via Subjective-Objective Reinforcement Learning

Abstract (English): Image Restoration (IR) agents, leveraging multimodal large language models to perceive degradation and invoke restoration tools, have shown promise in automating IR tasks. However, existing IR agents typically lack an insight summarization mechanism for past interactions, which results in an exhaustive search for the optimal IR tool. To address this limitation, we propose a portrait-aware IR agent, dubbed PaAgent, which incorporates a self-evolving portrait bank for IR tools and Retrieval-Augmented Generation (RAG) to select a suitable IR tool for input. Specifically, to construct and evolve the portrait bank, the PaAgent continuously enriches it by summarizing the characteristics of various IR tools with restored images, selected IR tools, and degraded images. In addition, the RAG is employed to select the optimal IR tool for the input image by retrieving relevant insights from the portrait bank. Furthermore, to enhance PaAgent's ability to perceive degradation in complex scenes, we propose a subjective-objective reinforcement learning strategy that considers both image quality scores and semantic insights in reward generation, which accurately provides the degradation information even under partial and non-uniform degradation. Extensive experiments across 8 IR benchmarks, covering six single-degradation and eight mixed-degradation scenarios, validate PaAgent's superiority in addressing complex IR tasks. Our project page is \href{https://wyjgr.github.io/PaAgent.html}{PaAgent}.

摘要（中文）: 图像修复 (IR) 智能体，利用多模态大型语言模型感知图像退化并调用修复工具，已在自动化IR任务中展现出潜力。然而，现有的IR智能体通常缺乏针对过往交互的洞察总结机制，导致对最优IR工具的穷举搜索。为了解决这个局限性，我们提出了一个面向肖像的IR智能体，命名为PaAgent，它整合了一个自演化的IR工具肖像库和检索增强生成 (RAG) 来为输入选择合适的IR工具。 具体而言，为了构建和演化肖像库，PaAgent通过总结各种IR工具在处理修复后的图像、选定的IR工具和退化图像时的特性，持续丰富该库。 此外，RAG被用于通过从肖像库中检索相关洞察，为输入图像选择最优的IR工具。 此外，为了增强PaAgent在复杂场景中感知退化的能力，我们提出了一种主观-客观强化学习策略，该策略在奖励生成中同时考虑图像质量评分和语义洞察，从而即使在局部和非均匀退化下也能准确提供退化信息。 在涵盖六种单退化和八种混合退化场景的8个IR基准测试上进行的大量实验验证了PaAgent在解决复杂IR任务方面的优越性。 我们的项目主页是 \href{https://wyjgr.github.io/PaAgent.html}{PaAgent}。

TLDR: The paper introduces PaAgent, a portrait-aware image restoration agent that uses a self-evolving portrait bank and Retrieval-Augmented Generation (RAG) to select optimal restoration tools, enhanced with subjective-objective reinforcement learning for improved degradation perception.

简要说明: 该论文介绍了PaAgent，一个肖像感知图像修复代理，它使用自进化的肖像库和检索增强生成（RAG）来选择最佳修复工具，并通过主观-客观强化学习来增强降级感知。

Authors: Yijian Wang, Qingsen Yan, Jiantao Zhou, Duwei Dai, Wei Dong

Astrolabe: Steering Forward-Process Reinforcement Learning for Distilled Autoregressive Video Models

Abstract (English): Distilled autoregressive (AR) video models enable efficient streaming generation but frequently misalign with human visual preferences. Existing reinforcement learning (RL) frameworks are not naturally suited to these architectures, typically requiring either expensive re-distillation or solver-coupled reverse-process optimization that introduces considerable memory and computational overhead. We present Astrolabe, an efficient online RL framework tailored for distilled AR models. To overcome existing bottlenecks, we introduce a forward-process RL formulation based on negative-aware fine-tuning. By contrasting positive and negative samples directly at inference endpoints, this approach establishes an implicit policy improvement direction without requiring reverse-process unrolling. To scale this alignment to long videos, we propose a streaming training scheme that generates sequences progressively via a rolling KV-cache, applying RL updates exclusively to local clip windows while conditioning on prior context to ensure long-range coherence. Finally, to mitigate reward hacking, we integrate a multi-reward objective stabilized by uncertainty-aware selective regularization and dynamic reference updates. Extensive experiments demonstrate that our method consistently enhances generation quality across multiple distilled AR video models, serving as a robust and scalable alignment solution.

摘要（中文）: 蒸馏自回归（AR）视频模型能够实现高效的流式生成，但常常与人类的视觉偏好不符。现有的强化学习（RL）框架并不自然地适用于这些架构，通常需要昂贵的重新蒸馏，或者与求解器耦合的反向过程优化，这会引入大量的内存和计算开销。我们提出了Astrolabe，一个为蒸馏AR模型量身定制的高效在线RL框架。为了克服现有的瓶颈，我们引入了一种基于负例感知微调的前向过程RL公式。通过在推理端点直接对比正负样本，该方法建立了一个隐式的策略提升方向，而无需反向过程展开。为了将这种对齐扩展到长视频，我们提出了一种流式训练方案，该方案通过滚动KV缓存逐步生成序列，仅将RL更新应用于局部片段窗口，同时以先前的上下文为条件，以确保长程连贯性。最后，为了缓解奖励作弊，我们集成了一个多奖励目标，该目标通过不确定性感知选择性正则化和动态参考更新来稳定。大量的实验表明，我们的方法始终如一地提高了跨多种蒸馏AR视频模型的生成质量，成为一种鲁棒且可扩展的对齐解决方案。

TLDR: The paper introduces Astrolabe, a forward-process reinforcement learning framework for aligning distilled autoregressive video models with human preferences, featuring negative-aware fine-tuning, streaming training, and multi-reward objective stabilization.

简要说明: 该论文介绍了一种名为Astrolabe的强化学习框架，它采用正向过程强化学习的方式，使提炼后的自回归视频模型与人类视觉偏好对齐。该框架包含负感知微调、流式训练和多奖励目标稳定等特性。

Authors: Songchun Zhang, Zeyue Xue, Siming Fu, Jie Huang, Xianghao Kong, Y Ma, Haoyang Huang, Nan Duan, Anyi Rao

OpenQlaw: An Agentic AI Assistant for Analysis of 2D Quantum Materials

Abstract (English): The transition from optical identification of 2D quantum materials to practical device fabrication requires dynamic reasoning beyond the detection accuracy. While recent domain-specific Multimodal Large Language Models (MLLMs) successfully ground visual features using physics-informed reasoning, their outputs are optimized for step-by-step cognitive transparency. This yields verbose candidate enumerations followed by dense reasoning that, while accurate, may induce cognitive overload and lack immediate utility for real-world interaction with researchers. To address this challenge, we introduce OpenQlaw, an agentic orchestration system for analyzing 2D materials. The architecture is built upon NanoBot, a lightweight agentic framework inspired by OpenClaw, and QuPAINT, one of the first Physics-Aware Instruction Multi-modal platforms for Quantum Material Discovery. This allows accessibility to the lab floor via a variety of messaging channels. OpenQlaw allows the core Large Language Model (LLM) agent to orchestrate a domain-expert MLLM,with QuPAINT, as a specialized node, successfully decoupling visual identification from reasoning and deterministic image rendering. By parsing spatial data from the expert, the agent can dynamically process user queries, such as performing scale-aware physical computation or generating isolated visual annotations, and answer in a naturalistic manner. Crucially, the system features a persistent memory that enables the agent to save physical scale ratios (e.g., 1 pixel = 0.25 μm) for area computations and store sample preparation methods for efficacy comparison. The application of an agentic architecture, together with the extension that uses the core agent as an orchestrator for domain-specific experts, transforms isolated inferences into a context-aware assistant capable of accelerating high-throughput device fabrication.

摘要（中文）: 从二维量子材料的光学识别到实际器件制造的转变，需要超越检测精度的动态推理。虽然最近特定领域的多模态大型语言模型（MLLM）已成功地利用物理信息推理对视觉特征进行了基础性研究，但它们的输出针对逐步认知透明度进行了优化。这导致语句冗长的候选枚举，然后是密集的推理，虽然准确，但可能导致认知超载，并且缺乏与研究人员进行现实世界交互的直接效用。为了应对这一挑战，我们引入了OpenQlaw，一个用于分析二维材料的代理编排系统。该架构建立在NanoBot（一个受OpenClaw启发的轻量级代理框架）和QuPAINT（首批用于量子材料发现的物理感知指令多模态平台之一）之上。这使得可以通过各种消息传递渠道访问实验室现场。OpenQlaw允许核心大型语言模型（LLM）代理编排一个领域专家MLLM（QuPAINT），将其作为一个专门的节点，成功地将视觉识别与推理和确定性图像渲染分离。通过解析来自专家的空间数据，代理可以动态处理用户查询，例如执行尺度感知的物理计算或生成隔离的视觉注释，并以自然的方式回答。至关重要的是，该系统具有持久内存，使代理能够保存物理尺度比例（例如，1像素=0.25微米）以进行面积计算，并存储样品制备方法以进行功效比较。代理架构的应用，以及使用核心代理作为领域特定专家编排器的扩展，将孤立的推理转变为一个上下文感知的助手，能够加速高通量器件制造。

Authors: Sankalp Pandey, Xuan-Bac Nguyen, Hoang-Quan Nguyen, Tim Faltermeier, Nicholas Borys, Hugh Churchill, Khoa Luu

Federated Distributional Reinforcement Learning with Distributional Critic Regularization

Abstract (English): Federated reinforcement learning typically aggregates value functions or policies by parameter averaging, which emphasizes expected return and can obscure statistical multimodality and tail behavior that matter in safety-critical settings. We formalize federated distributional reinforcement learning (FedDistRL), where clients parametrize quantile value function critics and federate these networks only. We also propose TR-FedDistRL, which builds a per client, risk-aware Wasserstein barycenter over a temporal buffer. This local barycenter provides a reference region to constrain the parameter averaged critic, ensuring necessary distributional information is not averaged out during the federation process. The distributional trust region is implemented as a shrink-squash step around this reference. Under fixed-policy evaluation, the feasibility map is nonexpansive and the update is contractive in a probe-set Wasserstein metric under evaluation. Experiments on a bandit, multi-agent gridworld, and continuous highway environment show reduced mean-smearing, improved safety proxies (catastrophe/accident rate), and lower critic/policy drift versus mean-oriented and non-federated baselines.

摘要（中文）: 联邦强化学习通常通过参数平均来聚合价值函数或策略，这强调期望回报，并可能掩盖在安全关键环境中重要的统计多模态和尾部行为。我们形式化了联邦分布强化学习(FedDistRL)，其中客户端参数化分位数价值函数评论家，并仅联邦这些网络。我们还提出了TR-FedDistRL，它基于每个客户端，构建一个关于时间缓冲区的风险感知Wasserstein重心。这个局部重心提供了一个参考区域来约束参数平均的评论家，确保必要的分布信息在联邦过程中不会被平均掉。分布式的信任区域被实现为围绕这个参考的收缩-挤压步骤。在固定策略评估下，可行性映射是非扩张的，并且在评估的探测集Wasserstein度量下，更新是收缩的。在老虎机、多智能体网格世界和连续高速公路环境中的实验表明，与面向均值和非联邦的基线相比，减少了均值涂抹、改善了安全代理(灾难/事故率)，并降低了评论家/策略漂移。

TLDR: This paper introduces Federated Distributional Reinforcement Learning (FedDistRL) with a distributional critic regularization method to improve safety and reduce mean-smearing in federated RL, particularly in safety-critical environments.

Authors: David Millard, Cecilia Alm, Rashid Ali, Pengcheng Shi, Ali Baheri

Towards Infinitely Long Neural Simulations: Self-Refining Neural Surrogate Models for Dynamical Systems

Abstract (English): Recent advances in autoregressive neural surrogate models have enabled orders-of-magnitude speedups in simulating dynamical systems. However, autoregressive models are generally prone to distribution drift: compounding errors in autoregressive rollouts that severely degrade generation quality over long time horizons. Existing work attempts to address this issue by implicitly leveraging the inherent trade-off between short-time accuracy and long-time consistency through hyperparameter tuning. In this work, we introduce a unifying mathematical framework that makes this tradeoff explicit, formalizing and generalizing hyperparameter-based strategies in existing approaches. Within this framework, we propose a robust, hyperparameter-free model implemented as a conditional diffusion model that balances short-time fidelity with long-time consistency by construction. Our model, Self-refining Neural Surrogate model (SNS), can be implemented as a standalone model that refines its own autoregressive outputs or as a complementary model to existing neural surrogates to ensure long-time consistency. We also demonstrate the numerical feasibility of SNS through high-fidelity simulations of complex dynamical systems over arbitrarily long time horizons.

摘要（中文）: 自回归神经代理模型近期的进展显著加速了动态系统的模拟速度，可达数量级提升。然而，自回归模型通常容易产生分布漂移：自回归展开中误差的累积会严重降低长时间范围内的生成质量。现有工作试图通过超参数调整来隐式利用短时精度和长时一致性之间的内在权衡来解决这个问题。本文中，我们引入了一个统一的数学框架，使这种权衡显式化，形式化并推广了现有方法中基于超参数的策略。在这个框架内，我们提出了一种鲁棒的、无超参数的模型，该模型实现为一个条件扩散模型，通过构建来平衡短时保真度和长时一致性。我们的模型，即自精炼神经代理模型（SNS），既可以作为独立模型来精炼其自身的自回归输出，也可以作为现有神经代理模型的补充模型，以确保长时一致性。我们还通过复杂动态系统在任意长时间范围内的高保真模拟，证明了SNS在数值上的可行性。

TLDR: This paper introduces a self-refining neural surrogate model (SNS) based on conditional diffusion models to address the distribution drift problem in autoregressive models, enabling stable and accurate long-term simulations of dynamical systems without hyperparameter tuning.

简要说明: 本文提出了一种基于条件扩散模型的自精炼神经替代模型（SNS），旨在解决自回归模型中的分布漂移问题，无需超参数调整即可实现动态系统的长期稳定和精确模拟。

Authors: Qi Liu, Laure Zanna, Joan Bruna

In Trust We Survive: Emergent Trust Learning

Abstract (English): We introduce Emergent Trust Learning (ETL), a lightweight, trust-based control algorithm that can be plugged into existing AI agents. It enables these to reach cooperation in competitive game environments under shared resources. Each agent maintains a compact internal trust state, which modulates memory, exploration, and action selection. ETL requires only individual rewards and local observations and incurs negligible computational and communication overhead. We evaluate ETL in three environments: In a grid-based resource world, trust-based agents reduce conflicts and prevent long-term resource depletion while achieving competitive individual returns. In a hierarchical Tower environment with strong social dilemmas and randomised floor assignments, ETL sustains high survival rates and recovers cooperation even after extended phases of enforced greed. In the Iterated Prisoner's Dilemma, the algorithm generalises to a strategic meta-game, maintaining cooperation with reciprocal opponents while avoiding long-term exploitation by defectors. Code will be released upon publication.

Authors: Qianpu Chen, Giulio Barbero, Mike Preuss, Derya Soydaner

SENSE: Efficient EEG-to-Text via Privacy-Preserving Semantic Retrieval

Abstract (English): Decoding brain activity into natural language is a major challenge in AI with important applications in assistive communication, neurotechnology, and human-computer interaction. Most existing Brain-Computer Interface (BCI) approaches rely on memory-intensive fine-tuning of Large Language Models (LLMs) or encoder-decoder models on raw EEG signals, resulting in expensive training pipelines, limited accessibility, and potential exposure of sensitive neural data. We introduce SENSE (SEmantic Neural Sparse Extraction), a lightweight and privacy-preserving framework that translates non-invasive electroencephalography (EEG) into text without LLM fine-tuning. SENSE decouples decoding into two stages: on-device semantic retrieval and prompt-based language generation. EEG signals are locally mapped to a discrete textual space to extract a non-sensitive Bag-of-Words (BoW), which conditions an off-the-shelf LLM to synthesize fluent text in a zero-shot manner. The EEG-to-keyword module contains only ~6M parameters and runs fully on-device, ensuring raw neural signals remain local while only abstract semantic cues interact with language models. Evaluated on a 128-channel EEG dataset across six subjects, SENSE matches or surpasses the generative quality of fully fine-tuned baselines such as Thought2Text while substantially reducing computational overhead. By localizing neural decoding and sharing only derived textual cues, SENSE provides a scalable and privacy-aware retrieval-augmented architecture for next-generation BCIs.

摘要（中文）: 将大脑活动解码成自然语言是人工智能领域的一项重大挑战，在辅助沟通、神经技术和人机交互方面具有重要应用。目前大多数脑机接口（BCI）方法依赖于对大型语言模型（LLM）或编码器-解码器模型在原始脑电（EEG）信号上进行耗费大量内存的微调，导致训练流程昂贵、可访问性受限，并可能暴露敏感的神经数据。我们引入了一种轻量级且保护隐私的框架SENSE（语义神经稀疏提取），它无需LLM微调即可将非侵入式脑电图（EEG）翻译成文本。SENSE将解码解耦为两个阶段：设备端语义检索和基于提示的语言生成。脑电信号在本地映射到一个离散的文本空间，以提取一个非敏感的词袋（BoW），从而以零样本方式调节一个现成的LLM来合成流畅的文本。脑电图到关键词模块仅包含约600万个参数，并且完全在设备上运行，确保原始神经信号保留在本地，只有抽象的语义线索与语言模型交互。在包含六名受试者的128通道脑电数据集上进行评估，SENSE在生成质量上与诸如Thought2Text等完全微调的基线模型相匹配或超越，同时显著降低了计算开销。通过本地化神经解码并仅共享导出的文本线索，SENSE为下一代BCI提供了一个可扩展且具备隐私意识的检索增强型架构。

TLDR: The paper introduces SENSE, a privacy-preserving and efficient framework for EEG-to-text translation that avoids fine-tuning LLMs by using on-device semantic retrieval and prompt-based language generation. It achieves comparable performance to fine-tuned baselines with significantly reduced computational cost and improved privacy.

Authors: Akshaj Murhekar, Christina Liu, Abhijit Mishra, Shounak Roychowdhury, Jacek Gwizdka

Bringing Network Coding into Multi-Robot Systems: Interplay Study for Autonomous Systems over Wireless Communications

Abstract (English): Communication is a core enabler for multi-robot systems (MRS), providing the mechanism through which robots exchange state information, coordinate actions, and satisfy safety constraints. While many MRS autonomy algorithms assume reliable and timely message delivery, realistic wireless channels introduce delay, erasures, and ordering stalls that can degrade performance and compromise safety-critical decisions of the robot task. In this paper, we investigate how transport-layer reliability mechanisms that mitigate communication losses and delays shape the autonomy-communication loop. We show that conventional non-coded retransmission-based protocols introduce long delays that are misaligned with the timeliness requirements of MRS applications, and may render the received data irrelevant. As an alternative, we advocate for adaptive and causal network coding, which proactively injects coded redundancy to achieve the desired delay and throughput that enable relevant data delivery to the robotic task. Specifically, this method adapts to channel conditions between robots and causally tunes the communication rates via efficient algorithms. We present two case studies: cooperative localization under delayed and lossy inter-robot communication, and a safety-critical overtaking maneuver where timely vehicle-to-vehicle message availability determines whether an ego vehicle can abort to avoid a crash. Our results demonstrate that coding-based communication significantly reduces in-order delivery stalls, preserves estimation consistency under delay, and improves deadline reliability relative to retransmission-based transport. Overall, the study highlights the need to jointly design autonomy algorithms and communication mechanisms, and positions network coding as a principled tool for dependable multi-robot operation over wireless networks.

摘要（中文）: 通信是多机器人系统（MRS）的核心赋能要素，它提供了一种机制，使机器人能够通过该机制交换状态信息、协调行动并满足安全约束。虽然许多 MRS 自主算法都假设可靠和及时的消息传递，但现实的无线信道会引入延迟、擦除和乱序停顿，从而降低性能并危及机器人任务的安全攸关决策。在本文中，我们研究了用于减轻通信丢失和延迟的传输层可靠性机制如何塑造自主-通信回路。我们表明，传统的基于非编码重传的协议会引入与 MRS 应用的实时性要求不符的长延迟，并可能导致接收到的数据失去关联性。作为一种替代方案，我们提倡自适应和因果网络编码，它主动注入编码冗余，以实现所需的延迟和吞吐量，从而能够将相关数据传递到机器人任务。具体来说，该方法适用于机器人之间的信道条件，并通过高效的算法因果地调整通信速率。我们提出了两个案例研究：在延迟和有损的机器人间通信下的协同定位，以及一个安全攸关的超车动作，其中及时的车 - 车消息可用性决定了自车能否中止以避免碰撞。我们的结果表明，基于编码的通信显著减少了按序交付停顿，在延迟下保持了估计一致性，并提高了相对于基于重传传输的截止期限可靠性。总而言之，该研究强调了联合设计自主算法和通信机制的必要性，并将网络编码定位为通过无线网络实现可靠多机器人操作的原则性工具。

TLDR: This paper explores the application of network coding to improve communication reliability and reduce delays in multi-robot systems, demonstrating its benefits in cooperative localization and safety-critical maneuvers.

Authors: Anil Zaher, Kiril Solovey, Alejandro Cohen

Uncovering Latent Phase Structures and Branching Logic in Locomotion Policies: A Case Study on HalfCheetah

Abstract (English): In locomotion control tasks, Deep Reinforcement Learning (DRL) has demonstrated high performance; however, the decision-making process of the learned policy remains a black box, making it difficult for humans to understand. On the other hand, in periodic motions such as walking, it is well known that implicit motion phases exist, such as the stance phase and the swing phase. Focusing on this point, this study hypothesizes that a policy trained for locomotion control may also represent a phase structure that is interpretable by humans. To examine this hypothesis in a controlled setting, we consider a locomotion task that is amenable to observing whether a policy autonomously acquires temporally structured phases through interaction with the environment. To verify this hypothesis, in the MuJoCo locomotion benchmark HalfCheetah-v5, the state transition sequences acquired by a policy trained for walking control through interaction with the environment were aggregated into semantic phases based on state similarity and consistency of subsequent transitions. As a result, we demonstrated that the state sequences generated by the trained policy exhibit periodic phase transition structures as well as phase branching. Furthermore, by approximating the states and actions corresponding to each semantic phase using Explainable Boosting Machines (EBMs), we analyzed phase-dependent decision making-namely, which state features the policy function attends to and how it controls action outputs in each phase. These results suggest that neural network-based policies, which are often regarded as black boxes, can autonomously acquire interpretable phase structures and logical branching mechanisms.

摘要（中文）: 在运动控制任务中，深度强化学习（DRL）已展现出高性能；然而，所学习策略的决策过程仍然是一个黑箱，人类难以理解。另一方面，在诸如步行的周期性运动中，众所周知存在隐式的运动相位，例如支撑相和摆动相。基于这一点，本研究假设，为运动控制训练的策略也可能呈现出可被人理解的相位结构。为了在可控的环境中检验该假设，我们考虑一个运动任务，它易于观察策略是否通过与环境的交互自主地获得时序结构化的相位。为了验证这个假设，在MuJoCo运动基准测试HalfCheetah-v5中，通过与环境交互为步行控制训练的策略所获得的状态转移序列，基于状态相似性和后续转移的一致性被聚合成语义相位。结果表明，训练后的策略生成的状态序列表现出周期性的相位转移结构以及相位分支。此外，通过使用可解释的增强机器（EBMs）逼近每个语义相位对应的状态和动作，我们分析了依赖于相位的决策过程——即策略函数在每个相位关注哪些状态特征以及如何控制动作输出。这些结果表明，通常被视为黑箱的基于神经网络的策略可以自主地获得可解释的相位结构和逻辑分支机制。

TLDR: This paper investigates whether DRL policies in locomotion tasks learn interpretable phase structures and branching logic, finding evidence of periodic phase transitions and logical branching mechanisms in HalfCheetah-v5.

Authors: Daisuke Yasui, Toshitaka Matsuki, Hiroshi Sato

SLAM Adversarial Lab: An Extensible Framework for Visual SLAM Robustness Evaluation under Adverse Conditions

Abstract (English): We present SAL (SLAM Adversarial Lab), a modular framework for evaluating visual SLAM systems under adversarial conditions such as fog and rain. SAL represents each adversarial condition as a perturbation that transforms an existing dataset into an adversarial dataset. When transforming a dataset, SAL supports severity levels using easily-interpretable real-world units such as meters for fog visibility. SAL's extensible architecture decouples datasets, perturbations, and SLAM algorithms through common interfaces, so users can add new components without rewriting integration code. Moreover, SAL includes a search procedure that finds the severity level of a perturbation at which a SLAM system fails. To showcase the capabilities of SAL, our evaluation integrates seven SLAM algorithms and evaluates them across three datasets under weather, camera, and video transport perturbations.

摘要（中文）: 我们提出了SAL（SLAM对抗实验室），这是一个模块化框架，用于在诸如雾和雨等对抗性条件下评估视觉SLAM系统。SAL将每种对抗性条件表示为一种扰动，该扰动将现有数据集转换为对抗性数据集。在转换数据集时，SAL支持使用易于理解的真实世界单位（如雾能见度的米数）来表示的严重程度等级。SAL的可扩展架构通过通用接口解耦了数据集、扰动和SLAM算法，因此用户无需重写集成代码即可添加新组件。此外，SAL还包含一个搜索程序，用于查找SLAM系统失效的扰动严重程度等级。为了展示SAL的功能，我们的评估集成了七种SLAM算法，并在天气、相机和视频传输扰动下，跨三个数据集对它们进行了评估。

TLDR: The paper introduces SLAM Adversarial Lab (SAL), a modular framework for evaluating visual SLAM robustness under adversarial conditions by transforming datasets with perturbations and searching for failure points.

Authors: Mohamed Hefny, Karthik Dantu, Steven Y. Ko

ChopGrad: Pixel-Wise Losses for Latent Video Diffusion via Truncated Backpropagation

Abstract (English): Recent video diffusion models achieve high-quality generation through recurrent frame processing where each frame generation depends on previous frames. However, this recurrent mechanism means that training such models in the pixel domain incurs prohibitive memory costs, as activations accumulate across the entire video sequence. This fundamental limitation also makes fine-tuning these models with pixel-wise losses computationally intractable for long or high-resolution videos. This paper introduces ChopGrad, a truncated backpropagation scheme for video decoding, limiting gradient computation to local frame windows while maintaining global consistency. We provide a theoretical analysis of this approximation and show that it enables efficient fine-tuning with frame-wise losses. ChopGrad reduces training memory from scaling linearly with the number of video frames (full backpropagation) to constant memory, and compares favorably to existing state-of-the-art video diffusion models across a suite of conditional video generation tasks with pixel-wise losses, including video super-resolution, video inpainting, video enhancement of neural-rendered scenes, and controlled driving video generation.

摘要（中文）: 近期视频扩散模型通过循环帧处理实现高质量的生成，其中每一帧的生成都依赖于之前的帧。然而，这种循环机制意味着在像素域训练此类模型会产生非常高的内存成本，因为激活值会累积在整个视频序列中。这种根本性的限制也使得对于长视频或高分辨率视频，使用像素级损失微调这些模型在计算上变得难以处理。本文介绍ChopGrad，一种用于视频解码的截断反向传播方案，它将梯度计算限制在局部帧窗口内，同时保持全局一致性。我们对这种近似方法进行了理论分析，并表明它能够通过逐帧损失进行高效微调。ChopGrad将训练内存从与视频帧数量呈线性增长（完全反向传播）降低到恒定的内存，并且在一系列使用像素级损失的条件视频生成任务中，与现有最先进的视频扩散模型相比表现良好，这些任务包括视频超分辨率、视频修复、神经渲染场景的视频增强以及受控的驾驶视频生成。

TLDR: The paper introduces ChopGrad, a truncated backpropagation method for efficiently training latent video diffusion models with pixel-wise losses, overcoming memory limitations and enabling fine-tuning for long videos.

简要说明: 该论文介绍了ChopGrad，一种截断反向传播方法，用于高效训练具有像素级损失的潜在视频扩散模型，克服了内存限制并实现了对长视频的微调。
