Authors: Dmitriy Rivkin, Parker Ewen, Lili Gao, Julian Ost, Stefanie Walz, Rasika Kangutkar, Mario Bijelic, Felix Heide

Learning Coordinate-based Convolutional Kernels for Continuous SE(3) Equivariant and Efficient Point Cloud Analysis

Abstract (English): A symmetry on rigid motion is one of the salient factors in efficient learning of 3D point cloud problems. Group convolution has been a representative method to extract equivariant features, but its realizations have struggled to retain both rigorous symmetry and scalability simultaneously. We advocate utilizing the intertwiner framework to resolve this trade-off, but previous works on it, which did not achieve complete SE(3) symmetry or scalability to large-scale problems, necessitate a more advanced kernel architecture. We present Equivariant Coordinate-based Kernel Convolution, or ECKConv. It acquires SE(3) equivariance from the kernel domain defined in a double coset space, and its explicit kernel design using coordinate-based networks enhances its learning capability and memory efficiency. The experiments on diverse point cloud tasks, e.g., classification, pose registration, part segmentation, and large-scale semantic segmentation, validate the rigid equivariance, memory scalability, and outstanding performance of ECKConv compared to state-of-the-art equivariant methods.

摘要（中文）: 刚性运动的对称性是高效学习3D点云问题的关键因素之一。群卷积作为一种提取等变特征的代表性方法，但其实现始终难以兼顾严格的对称性和可扩展性。我们提倡利用交织算子框架来解决这一权衡，但之前基于此框架的工作未能实现完整的SE(3)对称性或大规模问题的可扩展性，有必要采用更高级的核架构。我们提出了等变坐标基核卷积 (ECKConv)。它从定义在双陪集空间中的核域获取SE(3)等变性，并且其使用坐标基网络的显式核设计增强了其学习能力和内存效率。在多样化的点云任务（例如，分类、姿态配准、部件分割和大规模语义分割）上的实验验证了，与最先进的等变方法相比，ECKConv具有刚性等变性、内存可扩展性和卓越的性能。

TLDR: The paper introduces Equivariant Coordinate-based Kernel Convolution (ECKConv) for SE(3) equivariant point cloud analysis, claiming improved scalability, memory efficiency, and performance compared to existing methods.

简要说明: 本文介绍了一种名为Equivariant Coordinate-based Kernel Convolution (ECKConv) 的 SE(3) 等变点云分析方法，声称与现有方法相比，它具有更高的可扩展性、内存效率和性能。

Authors: Jaein Kim, Hee Bin Yoo, Dong-Sig Han, Byoung-Tak Zhang

How Clued up are LLMs? Evaluating Multi-Step Deductive Reasoning in a Text-Based Game Environment

Abstract (English): Deducing whodunit proves challenging for LLM agents. In this paper, we implement a text-based multi-agent version of the classic board game Clue as a rule-based testbed for evaluating multi-step deductive reasoning, with six agents drawn from GPT-4o-mini and Gemini-2.5-Flash. We further investigate whether fine-tuning on structured logic puzzles transfers to improved in-game reasoning and gameplay. Across 18 simulated games, agents achieve only four correct wins, indicating difficulty in maintaining consistent deductive reasoning over the course of a full game. Additionally, we find that fine-tuning does not reliably improve performance and, in some cases, appears to increase reasoning volume without improving reasoning precision.

摘要（中文）: 在谁是凶手的游戏中进行推断对于大语言模型智能体而言充满挑战。本文实现了一个基于文本的多智能体版本的经典桌游“妙探寻凶”，作为评估多步演绎推理的基于规则的测试平台，其中六个智能体来自 GPT-4o-mini 和 Gemini-2.5-Flash。我们进一步研究了在结构化逻辑谜题上进行微调是否能转化为游戏中推理和游戏表现的提升。在18个模拟游戏中，智能体仅实现了四次正确的胜利，表明在完整的游戏过程中保持一致的演绎推理存在困难。此外，我们发现微调并不能可靠地提高性能，在某些情况下，似乎增加了推理量，但没有提高推理精度。

TLDR: This paper evaluates the multi-step deductive reasoning capabilities of LLMs (GPT-4o-mini and Gemini-2.5-Flash) in a text-based Clue game environment, finding limited success and no reliable improvement from fine-tuning.

Authors: Rebecca Ansell, Autumn Toney-Wails

SegFly: A 2D-3D-2D Paradigm for Aerial RGB-Thermal Semantic Segmentation at Scale

Abstract (English): Semantic segmentation for uncrewed aerial vehicles (UAVs) is fundamental for aerial scene understanding, yet existing RGB and RGB-T datasets remain limited in scale, diversity, and annotation efficiency due to the high cost of manual labeling and the difficulties of accurate RGB-T alignment on off-the-shelf UAVs. To address these challenges, we propose a scalable geometry-driven 2D-3D-2D paradigm that leverages multi-view redundancy in high-overlap aerial imagery to automatically propagate labels from a small subset of manually annotated RGB images to both RGB and thermal modalities within a unified framework. By lifting less than 3% of RGB images into a semantic 3D point cloud and reprojecting it into all views, our approach enables dense pseudo ground-truth generation across large image collections, automatically producing 97% of RGB labels and 100% of thermal labels while achieving 91% and 88% annotation accuracy without any 2D manual refinement. We further extend this 2D-3D-2D paradigm to cross-modal image registration, using 3D geometry as an intermediate alignment space to obtain fully automatic, strong pixel-level RGB-T alignment with 87% registration accuracy and no hardware-level synchronization. Applying our framework to existing geo-referenced aerial imagery, we construct SegFly, a large-scale benchmark with over 20,000 high-resolution RGB images and more than 15,000 geometrically aligned RGB-T pairs spanning diverse urban, industrial, and rural environments across multiple altitudes and seasons. On SegFly, we establish the Firefly baseline for RGB and thermal semantic segmentation and show that both conventional architectures and vision foundation models benefit substantially from SegFly supervision, highlighting the potential of geometry-driven 2D-3D-2D pipelines for scalable multi-modal scene understanding. Data and Code available at https://github.com/markus-42/SegFly.

摘要（中文）: 无人机（UAV）语义分割是空中场景理解的基础，但现有的RGB和RGB-T数据集在规模、多样性和标注效率方面仍然有限，这是由于人工标注的高成本以及现成无人机上精确RGB-T对齐的困难所致。为了应对这些挑战，我们提出了一种可扩展的几何驱动2D-3D-2D范式，该范式利用高重叠度航空影像中的多视点冗余，将少量手动标注的RGB图像中的标签自动传播到统一框架中的RGB和热红外模态。通过将不到3%的RGB图像提升到语义3D点云，然后将其重新投影到所有视角中，我们的方法可以实现大规模图像集上密集的伪真值生成，自动生成97%的RGB标签和100%的热红外标签，同时在没有任何2D手动优化的情况下实现91%和88%的标注精度。我们进一步将这种2D-3D-2D范式扩展到跨模态图像配准，使用3D几何作为中间对齐空间，获得完全自动的、强大的像素级RGB-T对齐，具有87%的配准精度且无需硬件级同步。通过将我们的框架应用于现有的地理参考航空影像，我们构建了SegFly，这是一个大规模基准测试集，包含超过20,000张高分辨率RGB图像和超过15,000对几何对齐的RGB-T图像对，涵盖了不同高度和季节的各种城市、工业和乡村环境。在SegFly上，我们建立了用于RGB和热红外语义分割的Firefly基线，并表明传统架构和视觉基础模型都受益于SegFly的监督，突出了几何驱动2D-3D-2D流水线在可扩展多模态场景理解方面的潜力。数据和代码可在https://github.com/markus-42/SegFly获取。

TLDR: The paper introduces SegFly, a large-scale RGB-Thermal semantic segmentation dataset for UAV imagery generated using a novel 2D-3D-2D label propagation technique, addressing limitations in existing datasets regarding scale, diversity, and annotation efficiency.

Authors: Markus Gross, Sai Bharadhwaj Matha, Rui Song, Viswanathan Muthuveerappan, Conrad Christoph, Julius Huber, Daniel Cremers

UniSem: Generalizable Semantic 3D Reconstruction from Sparse Unposed Images

Abstract (English): Semantic-aware 3D reconstruction from sparse, unposed images remains challenging for feed-forward 3D Gaussian Splatting (3DGS). Existing methods often predict an over-complete set of Gaussian primitives under sparse-view supervision, leading to unstable geometry and inferior depth quality. Meanwhile, they rely solely on 2D segmenter features for semantic lifting, which provides weak 3D-level and limited generalizable supervision, resulting in incomplete 3D semantics in novel scenes. To address these issues, we propose UniSem, a unified framework that jointly improves depth accuracy and semantic generalization via two key components. First, Error-aware Gaussian Dropout (EGD) performs error-guided capacity control by suppressing redundancy-prone Gaussians using rendering error cues, producing meaningful, geometrically stable Gaussian representations for improved depth estimation. Second, we introduce a Mix-training Curriculum (MTC) that progressively blends 2D segmenter-lifted semantics with the model's own emergent 3D semantic priors, implemented with object-level prototype alignment to enhance semantic coherence and completeness. Extensive experiments on ScanNet and Replica show that UniSem achieves superior performance in depth prediction and open-vocabulary 3D segmentation across varying numbers of input views. Notably, with 16-view inputs, UniSem reduces depth Rel by 15.2% and improves open-vocabulary segmentation mAcc by 3.7% over strong baselines.

摘要（中文）: 从稀疏、无姿态图像中进行语义感知的3D重建对于前馈3D高斯溅射（3DGS）仍然具有挑战性。现有方法通常在稀疏视图监督下预测一个过度完备的高斯基元集合，导致不稳定的几何形状和较差的深度质量。同时，它们仅依赖于2D分割器特征进行语义提升，这提供了较弱的3D级别和有限的泛化监督，导致新场景中不完整的3D语义。为了解决这些问题，我们提出了UniSem，一个统一框架，通过两个关键组件联合提高深度精度和语义泛化能力。首先，误差感知高斯Dropout（EGD）通过使用渲染误差线索抑制易于冗余的高斯，执行误差引导的容量控制，从而产生有意义、几何稳定的高斯表示，以实现改进的深度估计。其次，我们引入混合训练课程（MTC），该课程逐步将2D分割器提升的语义与模型自身出现的3D语义先验混合，通过对象级别原型对齐来增强语义一致性和完整性。在ScanNet和Replica上的大量实验表明，UniSem在不同数量的输入视图下，在深度预测和开放词汇3D分割方面均取得了优异的性能。值得注意的是，在16视图输入下，UniSem的深度Rel降低了15.2%，开放词汇分割mAcc提高了3.7%，性能优于强大的基线方法。

TLDR: The paper introduces UniSem, a unified framework that improves depth accuracy and semantic generalization in 3D Gaussian Splatting from sparse, unposed images using error-aware Gaussian dropout and a mix-training curriculum with object-level prototype alignment.

简要说明: 该论文介绍了UniSem，一个统一的框架，它通过使用误差感知高斯Dropout和混合训练课程（带有对象级原型比对），提高了从稀疏、非姿态图像进行三维高斯溅射的深度精度和语义泛化能力。

Authors: Guibiao Liao, Qian Ren, Kaimin Liao, Hua Wang, Zhi Chen, Luchao Wang, Yaohua Tang

DarkDriving: A Real-World Day and Night Aligned Dataset for Autonomous Driving in the Dark Environment

Abstract (English): The low-light conditions are challenging to the vision-centric perception systems for autonomous driving in the dark environment. In this paper, we propose a new benchmark dataset (named DarkDriving) to investigate the low-light enhancement for autonomous driving. The existing real-world low-light enhancement benchmark datasets can be collected by controlling various exposures only in small-ranges and static scenes. The dark images of the current nighttime driving datasets do not have the precisely aligned daytime counterparts. The extreme difficulty to collect a real-world day and night aligned dataset in the dynamic driving scenes significantly limited the research in this area. With a proposed automatic day-night Trajectory Tracking based Pose Matching (TTPM) method in a large real-world closed driving test field (area: 69 acres), we collected the first real-world day and night aligned dataset for autonomous driving in the dark environment. The DarkDriving dataset has 9,538 day and night image pairs precisely aligned in location and spatial contents, whose alignment error is in just several centimeters. For each pair, we also manually label the object 2D bounding boxes. DarkDriving introduces four perception related tasks, including low-light enhancement, generalized low-light enhancement, and low-light enhancement for 2D detection and 3D detection of autonomous driving in the dark environment. The experimental results show that our DarkDriving dataset provides a comprehensive benchmark for evaluating low-light enhancement for autonomous driving and it can also be generalized to enhance dark images and promote detection in some other low-light driving environment, such as nuScenes.

摘要（中文）: 在黑暗环境中，低光照条件对以视觉为中心的自动驾驶感知系统提出了挑战。本文提出了一个新的基准数据集（命名为DarkDriving），旨在研究自动驾驶的低光照增强问题。现有的真实世界低光照增强基准数据集只能通过在小范围内和静态场景中控制各种曝光来收集。当前的夜间驾驶数据集中的黑暗图像没有精确对齐的白天对应图像。在动态驾驶场景中收集真实世界的白天和夜晚对齐数据集的极端困难，显著限制了该领域的研究。我们提出了一种基于轨迹跟踪的姿态匹配（TTPM）自动日夜对齐方法，在一个大型真实世界封闭驾驶测试场（面积：69英亩）中，收集了第一个在黑暗环境中用于自动驾驶的真实世界日夜对齐数据集。DarkDriving数据集具有9,538对在位置和空间内容上精确对齐的日夜图像对，其对齐误差仅为几厘米。对于每一对图像，我们还手动标注了物体的2D边界框。DarkDriving引入了四个与感知相关的任务，包括低光照增强、广义低光照增强，以及针对黑暗环境中自动驾驶的2D检测和3D检测的低光照增强。实验结果表明，我们的DarkDriving数据集为评估自动驾驶的低光照增强提供了一个全面的基准，并且它也可以推广到增强黑暗图像并促进在其他一些低光照驾驶环境中的检测，例如nuScenes。

TLDR: The paper introduces DarkDriving, a new real-world day and night aligned dataset for low-light autonomous driving research, addressing limitations of existing datasets with precise alignment and object annotations.

Authors: Wuqi Wang, Haochen Yang, Baolu Li, Jiaqi Sun, Xiangmo Zhao, Zhigang Xu, Qing Guo, Haigen Min, Tianyun Zhang, Hongkai Yu

Adaptive Anchor Policies for Efficient 4D Gaussian Streaming

Abstract (English): Dynamic scene reconstruction with Gaussian Splatting has enabled efficient streaming for real-time rendering and free-viewpoint video. However, most pipelines rely on fixed anchor selection such as Farthest Point Sampling (FPS), typically using 8,192 anchors regardless of scene complexity, which over-allocates computation under strict budgets. We propose Efficient Gaussian Streaming (EGS), a plug-in, budget-aware anchor sampler that replaces FPS with a reinforcement-learned policy while keeping the Gaussian streaming reconstruction backbone unchanged. The policy jointly selects an anchor budget and a subset of informative anchors under discrete constraints, balancing reconstruction quality and runtime using spatial features of the Gaussian representation. We evaluate EGS in two settings: fast rendering, which prioritizes runtime efficiency, and high-quality refinement, which enables additional optimization. Experiments on dynamic multi-view datasets show consistent improvements in the quality--efficiency trade-off over FPS sampling. On unseen data, in fast rendering at 256 anchors ($32\times$ fewer than 8,192), EGS improves PSNR by $+0.52$--$0.61$\,dB while running $1.29$--$1.35\times$ faster than IGS@8192 (N3DV and MeetingRoom). In high-quality refinement, EGS remains competitive with the full-anchor baseline at substantially lower anchor budgets. \emph{Code and pretrained checkpoints will be released upon acceptance.} \keywords{4D Gaussian Splatting \and 4D Gaussian Streaming \and Reinforcement Learning}

摘要（中文）: 使用高斯溅射的动态场景重建实现了高效的实时渲染和自由视点视频流。然而，大多数流程依赖于固定的锚点选择方法，如最远点采样（FPS），通常无论场景复杂度如何都使用8,192个锚点，这会在严格的预算下过度分配计算资源。我们提出了一种高效高斯流（EGS），这是一种即插即用的、具有预算意识的锚点采样器，用强化学习策略取代FPS，同时保持高斯流重建的主干不变。该策略在离散约束下联合选择锚点预算和信息量丰富的锚点子集，利用高斯表示的空间特征来平衡重建质量和运行时间。我们在两种设置下评估EGS：快速渲染（优先考虑运行时效率）和高质量细化（允许额外的优化）。在动态多视角数据集上的实验表明，与FPS采样相比，EGS在质量-效率权衡方面始终表现出改进。在未见过的数据上，在快速渲染模式下，使用256个锚点（比8,192个锚点少$32\times$），EGS在PSNR上提高了$+0.52$–$0.61$\,dB，同时比IGS@8192（N3DV和MeetingRoom）运行速度快$1.29$–$1.35\times$。在高质量细化中，EGS在显著降低锚点预算的情况下，仍具有与全锚点基线相当的竞争力。\emph{代码和预训练检查点将在接收后发布。} 关键词{4D高斯溅射 \and 4D高斯流 \and 强化学习}

TLDR: This paper introduces Efficient Gaussian Streaming (EGS), a reinforcement learning-based anchor sampler for 4D Gaussian Splatting that adaptively selects anchor budgets, improving quality-efficiency trade-offs compared to fixed sampling methods like Farthest Point Sampling (FPS). EGS demonstrates performance gains in both fast rendering and high-quality refinement settings.

Authors: Ashim Dahal, Rabab Abdelfattah, Nick Rahimi

Final Report for the Workshop on Robotics & AI in Medicine

Abstract (English): The CARE Workshop on Robotics and AI in Medicine, held on December 1, 2025 in Indianapolis, convened leading researchers, clinicians, industry innovators, and federal stakeholders to shape a national vision for advancing robotics and artificial intelligence in healthcare. The event highlighted the accelerating need for coordinated research efforts that bridge engineering innovation with real clinical priorities, emphasizing safety, reliability, and translational readiness with an emphasis on the use of robotics and AI to achieve this readiness goal. Across keynotes, panels, and breakout sessions, participants underscored critical gaps in data availability, standardized evaluation methods, regulatory pathways, and workforce training that hinder the deployment of intelligent robotic systems in surgical, diagnostic, rehabilitative, and assistive contexts. Discussions emphasized the transformative potential of AI enabled robotics to improve precision, reduce provider burden, expand access to specialized care, and enhance patient outcomes particularly in undeserved regions and high risk procedural domains. Special attention was given to austere settings, disaster and relief and military settings. The workshop demonstrated broad consensus on the urgency of establishing a national Center for AI and Robotic Excellence in medicine (CARE). Stakeholders identified priority research thrusts including human robot collaboration, trustworthy autonomy, simulation and digital twins, multi modal sensing, and ethical integration of generative AI into clinical workflows. Participants also articulated the need for high quality datasets, shared test beds, autonomous surgical systems, clinically grounded benchmarks, and sustained interdisciplinary training mechanisms.

摘要（中文）: 于2025年12月1日在印第安纳波利斯举行的医疗机器人与人工智能CARE研讨会汇集了顶尖研究人员、临床医生、行业创新者和联邦利益相关者，旨在塑造一个推动医疗领域机器人和人工智能发展的国家愿景。本次活动突出了协调研究工作的迫切需求，将工程创新与实际临床优先事项联系起来，重点强调安全性、可靠性和转化准备度，并强调利用机器人和人工智能来实现这一准备度目标。 通过主题演讲、小组讨论和分组会议，与会者强调了数据可用性、标准化评估方法、监管途径和劳动力培训方面的关键差距，这些差距阻碍了智能机器人系统在外科、诊断、康复和辅助环境中的部署。讨论强调了人工智能赋能机器人技术在提高精确度、减轻医护人员负担、扩大专业护理的可及性以及改善患者疗效方面的变革潜力，尤其是在服务欠发达地区和高风险手术领域。研讨会特别关注了简朴环境、灾难救援和军事环境。 研讨会表明，在建立国家医疗人工智能与机器人卓越中心（CARE）的紧迫性方面达成了广泛共识。利益相关者确定了优先研究方向，包括人机协作、可信自主性、仿真和数字孪生、多模态传感以及生成式人工智能在临床工作流程中的伦理整合。与会者还阐明了对高质量数据集、共享试验平台、自主手术系统、基于临床的基准以及可持续的跨学科培训机制的需求。

TLDR: This report summarizes the CARE workshop on Robotics and AI in Medicine, highlighting the need for coordinated research efforts, addressing gaps in data and evaluation, and proposing a national Center for AI and Robotic Excellence in medicine (CARE).

Authors: Juan P Wachs

Huddle: Parallel Shape Assembly using Decentralized, Minimalistic Robots

Abstract (English): We propose a novel algorithm for forming arbitrarily shaped assemblies using decentralized robots. By relying on local interactions, the algorithm ensures there are no unreachable states or gaps in the assembly, which are global properties. The in-assembly robots attract passing-by robots into expanding the assembly via a simple implementation of signaling and alignment. Our approach is minimalistic, requiring only communication between attached, immediate neighbors. It is motion-agnostic and requires no pose localization, enabling asynchronous and order-independent assembly. We prove the algorithm's correctness and demonstrate its effectiveness in forming a 107-robot assembly.

摘要（中文）: 我们提出了一种新颖的算法，用于使用去中心化机器人形成任意形状的组件。该算法通过依赖局部交互，确保组件中不存在不可达状态或间隙，这些都是全局属性。组件内的机器人通过简单的信令和对齐机制吸引路过的机器人来扩展组件。 我们的方法具有极简性，仅需相邻机器人之间进行通信。它与运动无关，并且无需位姿定位，从而支持异步和顺序无关的组件。我们证明了该算法的正确性，并通过组装一个包含 107 个机器人的组件来展示其有效性。

TLDR: This paper introduces a decentralized algorithm for robotic shape assembly using local interactions and minimal robot capabilities, demonstrating assembly of a 107-robot structure. It focuses on motion-agnostic, communication-based assembly.

简要说明: 本文提出了一种基于局部交互和极简机器人能力的去中心化机器人形状组装算法，并演示了由 107 个机器人组成的结构的组装。它专注于与运动无关的、基于通信的组装。

Authors: Khai Yi Chin, Tingwei Meng, Zhe Chen, Daniel Bassett, Yuri Ivanov

Multi-Source Human-in-the-Loop Digital Twin Testbed for Connected and Autonomous Vehicles in Mixed Traffic Flow

Abstract (English): In the emerging mixed traffic environments, Connected and Autonomous Vehicles (CAVs) have to interact with surrounding human-driven vehicles (HDVs). This paper introduces MSH-MCCT (Multi-Source Human-in-the-Loop Mixed Cloud Control Testbed), a novel CAV testbed that captures complex interactions between various CAVs and HDVs. Utilizing the Mixed Digital Twin concept, which combines Mixed Reality with Digital Twin, MSH-MCCT integrates physical, virtual, and mixed platforms, along with multi-source control inputs. Bridged by the mixed platform, MSH-MCCT allows human drivers and CAV algorithms to operate both physical and virtual vehicles within multiple fields of view. Particularly, this testbed facilitates the coexistence and real-time interaction of physical and virtual CAVs \& HDVs, significantly enhancing the experimental flexibility and scalability. Experiments on vehicle platooning in mixed traffic showcase the potential of MSH-MCCT to conduct CAV testing with multi-source real human drivers in the loop through driving simulators of diverse fidelity. The videos for the experiments are available at our project website: https://dongjh20.github.io/MSH-MCCT.

Authors: Jianghong Dong, Jiawei Wang, Chunying Yang, Mengchi Cai, Chaoyi Chen, Qing Xu, Jianqiang Wang, Keqiang Li

Consistency-Driven Dual LSTM Models for Kinematic Control of a Wearable Soft Robotic Arm

Abstract (English): In this paper, we introduce a consistency-driven dual LSTM framework for accurately learning both the forward and inverse kinematics of a pneumatically actuated soft robotic arm integrated into a wearable device. This approach effectively captures the nonlinear and hysteretic behaviors of soft pneumatic actuators while addressing the one-to-many mapping challenge between actuation inputs and end-effector positions. By incorporating a cycle consistency loss, we enhance physical realism and improve the stability of inverse predictions. Extensive experiments-including trajectory tracking, ablation studies, and wearable demonstrations-confirm the effectiveness of our method. Results indicate that the inclusion of the consistency loss significantly boosts prediction accuracy and promotes physical consistency over conventional approaches. Moreover, the wearable soft robotic arm demonstrates strong human-robot collaboration capabilities and adaptability in everyday tasks such as object handover, obstacle-aware pick-and-place, and drawer operation. This work underscores the promising potential of learning-based kinematic models for human-centric, wearable robotic systems.

摘要（中文）: 本文介绍了一种一致性驱动的双LSTM框架，用于精确学习集成到可穿戴设备中的气动软体机械臂的正向和逆向运动学。该方法有效地捕捉了软气动驱动器的非线性和滞后行为，同时解决了驱动输入与末端执行器位置之间的一对多映射挑战。通过引入循环一致性损失，我们增强了物理真实性并提高了逆预测的稳定性。大量的实验，包括轨迹跟踪、消融研究和可穿戴演示，证实了我们方法的有效性。结果表明，与传统方法相比，包含一致性损失能够显著提高预测精度并促进物理一致性。此外，可穿戴软体机械臂在诸如物体传递、避障式抓取和放置以及抽屉操作等日常任务中展示了强大的人机协作能力和适应性。这项工作强调了基于学习的运动学模型在以人为中心的可穿戴机器人系统中的巨大潜力。

TLDR: This paper presents a consistency-driven dual LSTM framework for learning the kinematics of a wearable soft robotic arm, demonstrating improved prediction accuracy and human-robot collaboration capabilities in everyday tasks.

Authors: Xingyu Chen, Yi Xiong, Li Wen

From Optimizable to Interactable: Mixed Digital Twin-Empowered Testing of Vehicle-Infrastructure Cooperation Systems

Abstract (English): Sufficient testing under corner cases is critical for the long-term operation of vehicle-infrastructure cooperation systems (VICS). However, existing corner-case generation methods are primarily AI-driven, and VICS testing under corner cases is typically limited to simulation. In this paper, we introduce an L5 ''Interactable'' level to the VICS digital twin (VICS-DT) taxonomy, extending beyond the conventional L4 ''Optimizable'' level. We further propose an L5-level VICS testing framework, IMPACT (Interactive Mixed-digital-twin Paradigm for Advanced Cooperative vehicle-infrastructure Testing). By enabling direct human interactions with VICS entities, IMPACT incorporates highly uncertain and unpredictable human behaviors into the testing loop, naturally generating high-quality corner cases that complement AI-based methods. Furthermore, the mixedDT-enabled ''Physical-Virtual Action Interaction'' facilitates safe VICS testing under corner cases, incorporating real-world environments and entities rather than purely in simulation. Finally, we implement IMPACT on the I-VIT (Interactive Vehicle-Infrastructure Testbed), and experiments demonstrate its effectiveness. The experimental videos are available at our project website: https://dongjh20.github.io/IMPACT.

摘要（中文）: 极端情况下的充分测试对于车路协同系统(VICS)的长期运行至关重要。然而，现有的极端情况生成方法主要以人工智能驱动，且车路协同系统在极端情况下的测试通常仅限于仿真。本文引入车路协同数字孪生（VICS-DT）分类法的L5“可交互”级别，超越了传统的L4“可优化”级别。我们进一步提出了一个L5级别的车路协同系统测试框架，即IMPACT（先进协同车辆基础设施测试的交互式混合数字孪生范式）。通过使人能够直接与车路协同系统实体进行交互，IMPACT将高度不确定和不可预测的人类行为纳入测试循环，自然地生成高质量的极端情况，从而补充基于人工智能的方法。此外，混合数字孪生支持的“物理-虚拟行为交互”促进了极端情况下安全的车路协同系统测试，将真实世界环境和实体纳入其中，而非纯粹的仿真。最后，我们在交互式车辆基础设施测试平台(I-VIT)上实现了IMPACT，实验证明了其有效性。实验视频可在我们的项目网站找到：https://dongjh20.github.io/IMPACT。

Authors: Jianghong Dong, Chunying Yang, Mengchi Cai, Chaoyi Chen, Qing Xu, Jianqiang Wang, Keqiang Li

Influence of Gripper Design on Human Demonstration Quality for Robot Learning

Abstract (English): Opening sterile medical packaging is routine for healthcare workers but remains challenging for robots. Learning from demonstration enables robots to acquire manipulation skills directly from humans, and handheld gripper tools such as the Universal Manipulation Interface (UMI) offer a pathway for efficient data collection. However, the effectiveness of these tools depends heavily on their usability. We evaluated UMI in demonstrating a bandage opening task, a common manipulation task in hospital settings, by testing three conditions: distributed load grippers, concentrated load grippers, and bare hands. Eight participants performed timed trials, with task performance assessed by success rate, completion time, and damage, alongside perceived workload using the NASA-TLX questionnaire. Concentrated load grippers improved performance relative to distributed load grippers but remained substantially slower and less effective than hands. These results underscore the importance of ergonomic and mechanical refinements in handheld grippers to reduce user burden and improve demonstration quality, especially for applications in healthcare robotics.

摘要（中文）: 打开无菌医疗包装对于医护人员来说是常规操作，但对于机器人来说仍然具有挑战性。模仿学习使机器人能够直接从人类那里获得操作技能，而通用操作界面（UMI）等手持式夹持工具提供了一种高效数据采集的途径。然而，这些工具的有效性很大程度上取决于其可用性。我们评估了UMI在演示绷带打开任务中的表现，这是一个医院环境中常见的操作任务，通过测试三种条件：分散载荷夹持器、集中载荷夹持器和徒手。八名参与者进行了计时试验，任务性能通过成功率、完成时间和损伤进行评估，同时使用美国宇航局任务负荷量表 （NASA-TLX）评估感知工作负荷。相对于分散载荷夹持器，集中载荷夹持器提高了性能，但仍然明显慢于徒手且效果较差。这些结果强调了手持式夹持器在人机工程学和机械改进方面的重要性，以减轻用户负担并提高演示质量，尤其是在医疗保健机器人应用中。

TLDR: This paper investigates the impact of gripper design on the quality of human demonstrations for robot learning, finding that concentrated load grippers improve performance compared to distributed load grippers but are still inferior to bare hands, highlighting the need for ergonomic improvements in handheld grippers.

简要说明: 本文研究了夹爪设计对机器人学习中人类演示质量的影响，发现集中载荷夹爪比分布式载荷夹爪的性能有所提高，但仍然不如徒手操作，强调了手持夹爪在人体工程学方面需要改进。

Authors: Gina L. Georgadarellis, Natalija Beslic, Seonhun Lee, Frank C. Sup, Meghan E. Huber

Asymmetric Nash Seeking via Best Response Maps: Global Linear Convergence and Robustness to Inexact Reaction Models

Abstract (English): Nash equilibria provide a principled framework for modeling interactions in multi-agent decision-making and control. However, many equilibrium-seeking methods implicitly assume that each agent has access to the other agents' objectives and constraints, an assumption that is often unrealistic in practice. This letter studies a class of asymmetric-information two-player constrained games with decoupled feasible sets, in which Player 1 knows its own objective and constraints while Player 2 is available only through a best-response map. For this class of games, we propose an asymmetric projected gradient descent-best response iteration that does not require full mutual knowledge of both players' optimization problems. Under suitable regularity conditions, we establish the existence and uniqueness of the Nash equilibrium and prove global linear convergence of the proposed iteration when the best-response map is exact. Recognizing that best-response maps are often learned or estimated, we further analyze the inexact case and show that, when the approximation error is uniformly bounded by $\varepsilon$, the iterates enter an explicit $O(\varepsilon)$ neighborhood of the true Nash equilibrium. Numerical results on a benchmark game corroborate the predicted convergence behavior and error scaling.

摘要（中文）: 纳什均衡为多智能体决策和控制中的交互建模提供了一个有原则的框架。然而，许多寻找均衡的方法隐式地假设每个智能体都可以访问其他智能体的目标和约束，这种假设在实践中往往是不现实的。本文研究了一类具有解耦可行集的不对称信息双人约束博弈，其中玩家1知道自己的目标和约束，而玩家2只能通过最佳响应映射获得。针对这类博弈，我们提出了一种非对称投影梯度下降-最佳响应迭代方法，该方法不需要双方玩家的优化问题的完整互知。在适当的正则性条件下，我们建立了纳什均衡的存在性和唯一性，并证明了当最佳响应映射是精确时，所提出的迭代具有全局线性收敛性。考虑到最佳响应映射通常是学习或估计得到的，我们进一步分析了非精确情况，并表明当近似误差被 $\varepsilon$ 一致有界时，迭代会进入真纳什均衡的一个显式的 $O(\varepsilon)$ 邻域。在一个基准博弈上的数值结果证实了预测的收敛行为和误差缩放。

TLDR: This paper proposes an asymmetric projected gradient descent-best response iteration for two-player constrained games with asymmetric information, proving linear convergence and robustness to inexact best-response models. It's relevant to multi-agent RL but not directly to my other interests.

简要说明: 本文提出了一种非对称投影梯度下降-最佳响应迭代算法，用于解决具有非对称信息的双人约束博弈问题，证明了该算法的线性收敛性和对不精确最佳响应模型的鲁棒性。该研究与多智能体强化学习相关，但与我的其他研究兴趣方向关联不大。

Authors: Mahdis Rabbani, Navid Mojahed, Shima Nazari

Governed Memory: A Production Architecture for Multi-Agent Workflows

Abstract (English): Enterprise AI deploys dozens of autonomous agent nodes across workflows, each acting on the same entities with no shared memory and no common governance. We identify five structural challenges arising from this memory governance gap: memory silos across agent workflows; governance fragmentation across teams and tools; unstructured memories unusable by downstream systems; redundant context delivery in autonomous multi-step executions; and silent quality degradation without feedback loops. We present Governed Memory, a shared memory and governance layer addressing this gap through four mechanisms: a dual memory model combining open-set atomic facts with schema-enforced typed properties; tiered governance routing with progressive context delivery; reflection-bounded retrieval with entity-scoped isolation; and a closed-loop schema lifecycle with AI-assisted authoring and automated per-property refinement. We validate each mechanism through controlled experiments (N=250, five content types): 99.6% fact recall with complementary dual-modality coverage; 92% governance routing precision; 50% token reduction from progressive delivery; zero cross-entity leakage across 500 adversarial queries; 100% adversarial governance compliance; and output quality saturation at approximately seven governed memories per entity. On the LoCoMo benchmark, the architecture achieves 74.8% overall accuracy, confirming that governance and schema enforcement impose no retrieval quality penalty. The system is in production at Personize.ai.

摘要（中文）: 企业人工智能在工作流程中部署数十个自主代理节点，每个节点在没有共享内存和共同治理的情况下对同一实体执行操作。我们发现了由此内存治理差距产生的五个结构性挑战：跨代理工作流程的内存孤岛；跨团队和工具的治理碎片化；下游系统无法使用的非结构化记忆；自主多步骤执行中冗余的上下文传递；以及没有反馈循环的静默质量下降。我们提出受治理的内存，一个通过四种机制解决此差距的共享内存和治理层：结合开放集原子事实与模式强制类型属性的双重内存模型；具有渐进式上下文传递的分层治理路由；具有实体范围隔离的反射限制检索；以及具有AI辅助创作和自动逐属性细化的闭环模式生命周期。我们通过受控实验（N=250，五种内容类型）验证了每种机制：99.6%的事实召回率，具有互补的双模态覆盖；92%的治理路由精度；来自渐进式传递的50%的token减少；500个对抗性查询中零跨实体泄漏；100%的对抗性治理合规性；以及每个实体约七个受治理内存时的输出质量饱和。在LoCoMo基准测试上，该架构实现了74.8%的总体准确率，证实了治理和模式强制没有带来检索质量的损失。该系统已在Personize.ai投入生产。

TLDR: The paper introduces Governed Memory, a shared memory and governance architecture for multi-agent workflows, addressing memory silos and governance fragmentation by providing structured memories and progressive context delivery, validated through experiments and a benchmark.

简要说明: 该论文介绍了Governed Memory，一种用于多智能体工作流的共享记忆和治理架构，通过提供结构化记忆和渐进式上下文传递，解决了记忆孤岛和治理碎片化的问题，并通过实验和基准测试进行了验证。

Authors: Hamed Taheri

ShuttleEnv: An Interactive Data-Driven RL Environment for Badminton Strategy Modeling

Abstract (English): We present ShuttleEnv, an interactive and data-driven simulation environment for badminton, designed to support reinforcement learning and strategic behavior analysis in fast-paced adversarial sports. The environment is grounded in elite-player match data and employs explicit probabilistic models to simulate rally-level dynamics, enabling realistic and interpretable agent-opponent interactions without relying on physics-based simulation. In this demonstration, we showcase multiple trained agents within ShuttleEnv and provide live, step-by-step visualization of badminton rallies, allowing attendees to explore different play styles, observe emergent strategies, and interactively analyze decision-making behaviors. ShuttleEnv serves as a reusable platform for research, visualization, and demonstration of intelligent agents in sports AI. Our ShuttleEnv demo video URL: https://drive.google.com/file/d/1hTR4P16U27H2O0-w316bR73pxE2ucczX/view

摘要（中文）: 我们提出ShuttleEnv，一个交互式和数据驱动的羽毛球模拟环境，旨在支持强化学习和快节奏对抗性运动中的战略行为分析。该环境基于精英球员比赛数据，并采用显式的概率模型来模拟回合级动态，从而实现逼真且可解释的Agent-对手互动，而无需依赖基于物理的模拟。在此演示中，我们将展示ShuttleEnv中的多个训练好的Agent，并提供羽毛球回合的实时、逐步可视化，使与会者能够探索不同的比赛风格，观察涌现的策略，并以交互方式分析决策行为。ShuttleEnv是一个可重用的平台，用于体育人工智能中智能Agent的研究、可视化和演示。我们的ShuttleEnv演示视频URL：https://drive.google.com/file/d/1hTR4P16U27H2O0-w316bR73pxE2ucczX/view

Authors: Ang Li, Xinyang Gong, Bozhou Chen, Yunlong Lu, Jiaming Ji, Yongyi Wang, Yaodong Yang, Wenxin Li

AHOY! Animatable Humans under Occlusion from YouTube Videos with Gaussian Splatting and Video Diffusion Priors

Abstract (English): We present AHOY, a method for reconstructing complete, animatable 3D Gaussian avatars from in-the-wild monocular video despite heavy occlusion. Existing methods assume unoccluded input-a fully visible subject, often in a canonical pose-excluding the vast majority of real-world footage where people are routinely occluded by furniture, objects, or other people. Reconstructing from such footage poses fundamental challenges: large body regions may never be observed, and multi-view supervision per pose is unavailable. We address these challenges with four contributions: (i) a hallucination-as-supervision pipeline that uses identity-finetuned diffusion models to generate dense supervision for previously unobserved body regions; (ii) a two-stage canonical-to-pose-dependent architecture that bootstraps from sparse observations to full pose-dependent Gaussian maps; (iii) a map-pose/LBS-pose decoupling that absorbs multi-view inconsistencies from the generated data; (iv) a head/body split supervision strategy that preserves facial identity. We evaluate on YouTube videos and on multi-view capture data with significant occlusion and demonstrate state-of-the-art reconstruction quality. We also demonstrate that the resulting avatars are robust enough to be animated with novel poses and composited into 3DGS scenes captured using cell-phone video. Our project page is available at https://miraymen.github.io/ahoy/

摘要（中文）: 我们提出了AHOY，一种从野外单目视频中重建完整、可动画的3D高斯化身的方法，即使在严重遮挡的情况下也能实现。现有方法假定输入不受遮挡——主体完全可见，通常处于规范姿势——这排除了绝大多数真实世界素材，在这些素材中，人物经常被家具、物体或其他人遮挡。从此类素材中重建带来了根本性的挑战：大面积的身体区域可能永远无法被观察到，并且无法获得每个姿势的多视角监督。我们通过四项贡献来解决这些挑战：（i）一种幻觉即监督的流程，该流程使用身份微调的扩散模型来为先前未观察到的身体区域生成密集的监督信息；（ii）一种两阶段的规范到姿势相关的架构，该架构从稀疏的观测中启动到完整的姿势相关高斯图；（iii）一种地图姿势/LBS姿势解耦，用于吸收生成数据的多视角不一致性；（iv）一种头部/身体分离监督策略，用于保留面部身份。我们在YouTube视频和具有显著遮挡的多视角捕捉数据上进行了评估，并展示了最先进的重建质量。我们还证明了生成的化身足够鲁棒，可以用新的姿势进行动画处理，并合成到使用手机视频捕获的3DGS场景中。我们的项目页面位于 https://miraymen.github.io/ahoy/

TLDR: AHOY reconstructs animatable 3D human avatars from monocular YouTube videos with heavy occlusion by using diffusion models for hallucination and a novel two-stage architecture for handling sparse observations, enabling animation and compositing.

简要说明: AHOY通过使用扩散模型进行幻觉生成，并采用新颖的两阶段架构来处理稀疏观测，从单目YouTube视频中重建具有严重遮挡的可动画3D人体化身，从而实现动画和合成。

Authors: Aymen Mir, Riza Alp Guler, Xiangjun Tang, Peter Wonka, Gerard Pons-Moll

SpiderCam: Low-Power Snapshot Depth from Differential Defocus

Abstract (English): We introduce SpiderCam, an FPGA-based snapshot depth-from-defocus camera which produces 480x400 sparse depth maps in real-time at 32.5 FPS over a working range of 52 cm while consuming 624 mW of power in total. SpiderCam comprises a custom camera that simultaneously captures two differently focused images of the same scene, processed with a SystemVerilog implementation of depth from differential defocus (DfDD) on a low-power FPGA. To achieve state-of-the-art power consumption, we present algorithmic improvements to DfDD that overcome challenges caused by low-power sensors, and design a memory-local implementation for streaming depth computation on a device that is too small to store even a single image pair. We report the first sub-Watt total power measurement for passive FPGA-based 3D cameras in the literature.

摘要（中文）: 我们介绍了SpiderCam，这是一种基于FPGA的快照式散焦深度相机，它以32.5 FPS的实时速度生成480x400的稀疏深度图，有效工作范围为52厘米，总功耗仅为624 mW。SpiderCam包含一个定制相机，该相机同时捕获同一场景的两幅不同焦距的图像，并使用SystemVerilog实现差分散焦深度（DfDD）算法在低功耗FPGA上进行处理。为了实现最先进的功耗，我们针对DfDD提出了算法改进，以克服低功耗传感器带来的挑战，并设计了一种内存局部实现方案，以便在太小而无法存储甚至一对图像的设备上进行流式深度计算。我们报告了文献中第一个基于FPGA的无源3D相机低于1瓦的总功耗测量结果。

TLDR: SpiderCam introduces a low-power, FPGA-based depth camera using differential defocus, achieving real-time sparse depth maps with sub-Watt power consumption. It presents algorithmic improvements and a memory-local implementation for efficient depth computation.

简要说明: SpiderCam 提出了一种基于 FPGA 的低功耗深度相机，它使用差分散焦技术，以亚瓦级的功耗实现实时稀疏深度图。论文提出了算法改进和内存局部实现，以实现高效的深度计算。

Authors: Marcos A. Ferreira, Tianao Li, John Mamish, Josiah Hester, Yaman Sangar, Qi Guo, Emma Alexander

CrowdGaussian: Reconstructing High-Fidelity 3D Gaussians for Human Crowd from a Single Image

Abstract (English): Single-view 3D human reconstruction has garnered significant attention in recent years. Despite numerous advancements, prior research has concentrated on reconstructing 3D models from clear, close-up images of individual subjects, often yielding subpar results in the more prevalent multi-person scenarios. Reconstructing 3D human crowd models is a highly intricate task, laden with challenges such as: 1) extensive occlusions, 2) low clarity, and 3) numerous and various appearances. To address this task, we propose CrowdGaussian, a unified framework that directly reconstructs multi-person 3D Gaussian Splatting (3DGS) representations from single-image inputs. To handle occlusions, we devise a self-supervised adaptation pipeline that enables the pretrained large human model to reconstruct complete 3D humans with plausible geometry and appearance from heavily occluded inputs. Furthermore, we introduce Self-Calibrated Learning (SCL). This training strategy enables single-step diffusion models to adaptively refine coarse renderings to optimal quality by blending identity-preserving samples with clean/corrupted image pairs. The outputs can be distilled back to enhance the quality of multi-person 3DGS representations. Extensive experiments demonstrate that CrowdGaussian generates photorealistic, geometrically coherent reconstructions of multi-person scenes.

摘要（中文）: 单视角3D人体重建近年来备受关注。尽管取得了诸多进展，但以往的研究主要集中于从清晰、近距离的单人图像中重建3D模型，在更为普遍的多人场景中往往产生次优结果。重建3D人群模型是一项高度复杂的任务，面临诸多挑战，例如：1）广泛的遮挡，2）低清晰度，以及3）众多且各异的外观。为了解决这一任务，我们提出了CrowdGaussian，一个统一的框架，可以直接从单图像输入重建多人的3D高斯溅射(3DGS)表示。为了处理遮挡，我们设计了一种自监督适应管道，使得预训练的大型人体模型能够从严重遮挡的输入中重建具有合理几何形状和外观的完整3D人体。此外，我们引入了自校准学习（SCL）。这种训练策略使单步扩散模型能够通过将保持身份的样本与干净/损坏的图像对混合，自适应地将粗糙渲染优化到最佳质量。输出可以被提炼回来，以提高多人3DGS表示的质量。大量实验表明，CrowdGaussian可以生成逼真的、几何连贯的多人场景重建结果。

TLDR: The paper introduces CrowdGaussian, a novel framework that reconstructs high-fidelity 3D Gaussian Splatting representations of human crowds from single images, addressing challenges like occlusion and low clarity through self-supervised adaptation and self-calibrated learning.

简要说明: 该论文介绍了 CrowdGaussian，一种新颖的框架，可以从单张图像重建人体群体的逼真3D高斯溅射表示，通过自监督适应和自校准学习来解决遮挡和低清晰度等挑战。

Authors: Yizheng Song, Yiyu Zhuang, Qipeng Xu, Haixiang Wang, Jiahe Zhu, Jing Tian, Siyu Zhu, Hao Zhu

DancingBox: A Lightweight MoCap System for Character Animation from Physical Proxies

Abstract (English): Creating compelling 3D character animations typically requires either expert use of professional software or expensive motion capture systems operated by skilled actors. We present DancingBox, a lightweight, vision-based system that makes motion capture accessible to novices by reimagining the process as digital puppetry. Instead of tracking precise human motions, DancingBox captures the approximate movements of everyday objects manipulated by users with a single webcam. These coarse proxy motions are then refined into realistic character animations by conditioning a generative motion model on bounding-box representations, enriched with human motion priors learned from large-scale datasets. To overcome the lack of paired proxy-animation data, we synthesize training pairs by converting existing motion capture sequences into proxy representations. A user study demonstrates that DancingBox enables intuitive and creative character animation using diverse proxies, from plush toys to bananas, lowering the barrier to entry for novice animators.

摘要（中文）: 创建引人入胜的3D角色动画通常需要专业软件的专家级使用，或者由熟练演员操作的昂贵动作捕捉系统。我们提出了DancingBox，这是一个轻量级的、基于视觉的系统，它将动作捕捉重新构想为数字木偶，从而使新手也能轻松使用。DancingBox 不跟踪精确的人体运动，而是捕捉用户使用单个网络摄像头操纵的日常物品的近似运动。然后，通过将生成式运动模型建立在边界框表示之上并结合从大规模数据集中学习的人体运动先验知识，将这些粗略的代理运动细化为逼真的角色动画。为了克服缺乏配对的代理-动画数据的问题，我们通过将现有的动作捕捉序列转换为代理表示来合成训练对。用户研究表明，DancingBox 能够使用户通过多样的代理对象（从小毛绒玩具到香蕉）进行直观且富有创造性的角色动画制作，从而降低了新手动画师的入门门槛。

TLDR: DancingBox is a new vision-based motion capture system that uses everyday objects as proxies to generate realistic character animations, making motion capture more accessible to novice animators.

简要说明: DancingBox是一种新的基于视觉的动作捕捉系统，它使用日常物品作为代理来生成逼真的人物动画，使动作捕捉更容易被新手动画师使用。

Authors: Haocheng Yuan, Adrien Bousseau, Hao Pan, Lei Zhong, Changjian Li

UAV-CB: A Complex-Background RGB-T Dataset and Local Frequency Bridge Network for UAV Detection

Abstract (English): Detecting Unmanned Aerial Vehicles (UAVs) in low-altitude environments is essential for perception and defense systems but remains highly challenging due to complex backgrounds, camouflage, and multimodal interference. In real-world scenarios, UAVs are frequently visually blended with surrounding structures such as buildings, vegetation, and power lines, resulting in low contrast, weak boundaries, and strong confusion with cluttered background textures. Existing UAV detection datasets, though diverse, are not specifically designed to capture these camouflage and complex-background challenges, which limits progress toward robust real-world perception. To fill this gap, we construct UAV-CB, a new RGB-T UAV detection dataset deliberately curated to emphasize complex low-altitude backgrounds and camouflage characteristics. Furthermore, we propose the Local Frequency Bridge Network (LFBNet), which models features in localized frequency space to bridge both the frequency-spatial fusion gap and the cross-modality discrepancy gap in RGB-T fusion. Extensive experiments on UAV-CB and public benchmarks demonstrate that LFBNet achieves state-of-the-art detection performance and strong robustness under camouflaged and cluttered conditions, offering a frequency-aware perspective on multimodal UAV perception in real-world applications.

摘要（中文）: 在低空环境中检测无人机对于感知和防御系统至关重要，但由于复杂背景、伪装和多模态干扰，这项任务仍然极具挑战性。在实际场景中，无人机经常在视觉上与周围的建筑物、植被和电力线等结构融为一体，导致低对比度、弱边界以及与杂乱背景纹理的强烈混淆。现有的无人机检测数据集虽然多样，但并未专门设计用于捕捉这些伪装和复杂背景带来的挑战，这限制了在实现鲁棒的真实世界感知方面的进展。为了填补这一空白，我们构建了UAV-CB，这是一个新的RGB-T无人机检测数据集，专门设计用于强调复杂的低空背景和伪装特性。此外，我们提出了局部频率桥接网络（LFBNet），该网络在局部频率空间中建模特征，以桥接RGB-T融合中的频率-空间融合差距和跨模态差异差距。在UAV-CB和公共基准数据集上的大量实验表明，LFBNet实现了最先进的检测性能，并在伪装和杂乱条件下表现出强大的鲁棒性，为真实世界应用中的多模态无人机感知提供了一种频率感知的视角。

TLDR: The paper introduces a new RGB-T dataset (UAV-CB) focusing on UAV detection in complex backgrounds and a novel Local Frequency Bridge Network (LFBNet) for robust UAV detection via frequency-aware multimodal fusion.

简要说明: 该论文介绍了一个新的RGB-T数据集（UAV-CB），专注于复杂背景下的无人机检测，并提出了一个新的局部频率桥网络（LFBNet），通过频率感知的多模态融合实现鲁棒的无人机检测。

Authors: Shenghui Huang, Menghao Hu, Longkun Zou, Hongyu Chi, Zekai Li, Feng Gao, Fan Yang, Qingyao Wu, Ke Chen

EgoAdapt: Enhancing Robustness in Egocentric Interactive Speaker Detection Under Missing Modalities

Abstract (English): TTM (Talking to Me) task is a pivotal component in understanding human social interactions, aiming to determine who is engaged in conversation with the camera-wearer. Traditional models often face challenges in real-world scenarios due to missing visual data, neglecting the role of head orientation, and background noise. This study addresses these limitations by introducing EgoAdapt, an adaptive framework designed for robust egocentric "Talking to Me" speaker detection under missing modalities. Specifically, EgoAdapt incorporates three key modules: (1) a Visual Speaker Target Recognition (VSTR) module that captures head orientation as a non-verbal cue and lip movement as a verbal cue, allowing a comprehensive interpretation of both verbal and non-verbal signals to address TTM, setting it apart from tasks focused solely on detecting speaking status; (2) a Parallel Shared-weight Audio (PSA) encoder for enhanced audio feature extraction in noisy environments; and (3) a Visual Modality Missing Awareness (VMMA) module that estimates the presence or absence of each modality at each frame to adjust the system response dynamically.Comprehensive evaluations on the TTM benchmark of the Ego4D dataset demonstrate that EgoAdapt achieves a mean Average Precision (mAP) of 67.39% and an Accuracy (Acc) of 62.01%, significantly outperforming the state-of-the-art method by 4.96% in Accuracy and 1.56% in mAP.

摘要（中文）: TTM（对话者）任务是理解人类社交互动的一个关键组成部分，旨在确定谁正在与佩戴摄像机的人进行对话。由于视觉数据缺失、忽略头部朝向的作用以及背景噪声等问题，传统模型在现实场景中经常面临挑战。本研究通过引入EgoAdapt来解决这些局限性，EgoAdapt是一种自适应框架，专为在模态缺失情况下实现鲁棒的以自我为中心的“对话者”说话人检测而设计。具体来说，EgoAdapt包含三个关键模块：（1）视觉说话人目标识别（VSTR）模块，该模块捕捉头部朝向作为非语言线索，以及唇动作为语言线索，从而能够全面解释语言和非语言信号以解决TTM问题，使其区别于仅关注检测说话状态的任务；（2）用于增强噪声环境下音频特征提取的并行共享权重音频（PSA）编码器；以及（3）视觉模态缺失感知（VMMA）模块，该模块估计每帧中每种模态的存在与否，以动态调整系统响应。在Ego4D数据集的TTM基准上的全面评估表明，EgoAdapt实现了67.39%的平均精度均值（mAP）和62.01%的准确率（Acc），在准确率方面比最先进的方法高出4.96%，在mAP方面高出1.56%。

TLDR: The paper introduces EgoAdapt, a framework for robust egocentric interactive speaker detection under missing modalities, achieving state-of-the-art results on the Ego4D dataset by integrating head orientation, lip movement, audio processing, and modality missing awareness.

简要说明: 该论文介绍了EgoAdapt，一个在模态缺失情况下用于鲁棒自中心交互式说话人检测的框架。通过整合头部朝向、嘴唇运动、音频处理和模态缺失感知，在Ego4D数据集上取得了当前最优的结果。

Authors: Xinyuan Qian, Xinjia Zhu, Alessio Brutti, Dong Liang

ECHO: Towards Emotionally Appropriate and Contextually Aware Interactive Head Generation

Abstract (English): In natural face-to-face interaction, participants seamlessly alternate between speaking and listening, producing facial behaviors (FBs) that are finely informed by long-range context and naturally exhibit contextual appropriateness and emotional rationality. Interactive Head Generation (IHG) aims to synthesize lifelike avatar head video emulating such capabilities. Existing IHG methods typically condition on dual-track signals (i.e., human user's behaviors and pre-defined audio for avatar) within a short temporal window, jointly driving generation of avatar's audio-aligned lip articulation and non-verbal FBs. However, two main challenges persist in these methods: (i) the reliance on short-clip behavioral cues without long-range contextual modeling leads them to produce facial behaviors lacking contextual appropriateness; and (ii) the entangled, role-agnostic fusion of dual-track signals empirically introduces cross-signal interference, potentially compromising lip-region synchronization during speaking. To this end, we propose ECHO, a novel IHG framework comprising two key components: a Long-range Contextual Understanding (LCU) component that facilitates contextual understanding of both behavior-grounded dynamics and linguistic-driven affective semantics to promote contextual appropriateness and emotional rationality of synthesized avatar FBs; and a block-wise Spatial-aware Decoupled Cross-attention Modulation (SDCM) module, that preserves self-audio-driven lip articulation while adaptively integrating user contextual behavioral cues for non-lip facial regions, complemented by our designed two-stage training paradigm, to jointly enhance lip synchronization and visual fidelity. Extensive experiments demonstrate the effectiveness of proposed components and ECHO's superior IHG performance.

摘要（中文）: 在自然的面对面互动中，参与者无缝地交替进行说话和听取，产生由远距离上下文信息精细驱动的面部行为（FBs），并自然地表现出情境适当性和情感合理性。交互式头部生成（IHG）旨在合成逼真的头像头部视频，模拟此类能力。现有的IHG方法通常在较短的时间窗口内，以双轨信号（即，人类用户的行为和头像预定义的音频）为条件，共同驱动头像音频对齐唇部动作和非语言FBs的生成。然而，这些方法中仍然存在两个主要挑战：（i）依赖于缺乏远距离上下文建模的短片段行为线索，导致生成的面部行为缺乏情境适当性；以及（ii）双轨信号的纠缠的、角色无关的融合，在经验上引入了跨信号干扰，可能会损害说话期间唇部区域的同步。为此，我们提出ECHO，一种新颖的IHG框架，包含两个关键组成部分：一个远距离上下文理解（LCU）组件，有助于对行为驱动的动态和语言驱动的情感语义进行上下文理解，以促进合成头像FBs的情境适当性和情感合理性；以及一个分块的空间感知解耦互注意力调制（SDCM）模块，在自音频驱动唇部动作的同时，自适应地整合用户上下文行为线索用于非唇部面部区域，并辅以我们设计的两阶段训练范式，以共同增强唇部同步和视觉保真度。大量实验证明了所提出组件的有效性以及ECHO卓越的IHG性能。

TLDR: The paper introduces ECHO, a novel Interactive Head Generation framework that addresses the lack of long-range contextual awareness and cross-signal interference in existing methods, leading to more emotionally appropriate and contextually aware avatar facial behaviors.

简要说明: 该论文介绍了ECHO，一种新颖的交互式头部生成框架，旨在解决现有方法中缺乏长期上下文感知和跨信号干扰的问题，从而生成更具情感适应性和上下文感知的头像面部行为。

Authors: Xiangyu Kong, Xiaoyu Jin, Yihan Pan, Haoqin Sun, Hengde Zhu, Xiaoming Xu, Xiaoming Wei, Lu Liu, Siyang Song

Toward Phonology-Guided Sign Language Motion Generation: A Diffusion Baseline and Conditioning Analysis

Abstract (English): Generating natural, correct, and visually smooth 3D avatar sign language motion conditioned on the text inputs continues to be very challenging. In this work, we train a generative model of 3D body motion and explore the role of phonological attribute conditioning for sign language motion generation, using ASL-LEX 2.0 annotations such as hand shape, hand location and movement. We first establish a strong diffusion baseline using an Human Motion MDM-style diffusion model with SMPL-X representation, which outperforms SignAvatar, a state-of-the-art CVAE method, on gloss discriminability metrics. We then systematically study the role of text conditioning using different text encoders (CLIP vs. T5), conditioning modes (gloss-only vs. gloss+phonological attributes), and attribute notation format (symbolic vs. natural language). Our analysis reveals that translating symbolic ASL-LEX notations to natural language is a necessary condition for effective CLIP-based attribute conditioning, while T5 is largely unaffected by this translation. Furthermore, our best-performing variant (CLIP with mapped attributes) outperforms SignAvatar across all metrics. These findings highlight input representation as a critical factor for text-encoder-based attribute conditioning, and motivate structured conditioning approaches where gloss and phonological attributes are encoded through independent pathways.

摘要（中文）: 根据文本输入生成自然、正确且视觉流畅的3D头像手语动作依然极具挑战性。 在这项工作中，我们训练了一个3D身体动作的生成模型，并探讨了音位属性条件作用在手语动作生成中的作用，使用了诸如手形、手部位置和运动等ASL-LEX 2.0标注。 我们首先使用Human Motion MDM风格的扩散模型和SMPL-X表示建立了一个强大的扩散基线，在语料区分度指标上优于SignAvatar（一种先进的CVAE方法）。 然后，我们系统地研究了使用不同文本编码器（CLIP vs. T5）、条件作用模式（仅词汇标注 vs. 词汇标注+音位属性）和属性表示格式（符号式 vs. 自然语言）的文本条件作用的作用。 我们的分析表明，将符号式ASL-LEX标注转换为自然语言是基于CLIP的有效属性条件作用的必要条件，而T5基本上不受此转换的影响。 此外，我们表现最佳的变体（CLIP与映射属性）在所有指标上均优于SignAvatar。 这些发现突出了输入表示法是基于文本编码器的属性条件作用的关键因素，并激发了结构化的条件作用方法，在该方法中，词汇标注和音位属性通过独立的路径进行编码。

TLDR: This paper explores phonology-guided sign language generation using a diffusion model and analyzes different text conditioning strategies, finding that natural language translation of phonological attributes is crucial for CLIP-based models.

简要说明: 本文探索了语音学指导的手语生成，使用扩散模型并分析了不同的文本调节策略，发现将音系属性翻译成自然语言对于基于 CLIP 的模型至关重要。

Authors: Rui Hong, Jana Kosecka

A 3D Reconstruction Benchmark for Asset Inspection

Abstract (English): Asset management requires accurate 3D models to inform the maintenance, repair, and assessment of buildings, maritime vessels, and other key structures as they age. These downstream applications rely on high-fidelity models produced from aerial surveys in close proximity to the asset, enabling operators to locate and characterise deterioration or damage and plan repairs. Captured images typically have high overlap between adjacent camera poses, sufficient detail at millimetre scale, and challenging visual appearances such as reflections and transparency. However, existing 3D reconstruction datasets lack examples of these conditions, making it difficult to benchmark methods for this task. We present a new dataset with ground truth depth maps, camera poses, and mesh models of three synthetic scenes with simulated inspection trajectories and varying levels of surface condition on non-Lambertian scene content. We evaluate state-of-the-art reconstruction methods on this dataset. Our results demonstrate that current approaches struggle significantly with the dense capture trajectories and complex surface conditions inherent to this domain, exposing a critical scalability gap and pointing toward new research directions for deployable 3D reconstruction in asset inspection. Project page: https://roboticimaging.org/Projects/asset-inspection-dataset/

摘要（中文）: 资产管理需要精确的3D模型，以便为建筑物、海事船舶和其他关键结构的老化过程中的维护、修理和评估提供信息。这些下游应用依赖于从靠近资产的航空测量生成的高保真模型，使操作员能够定位和描述劣化或损坏，并规划维修。捕获的图像通常在相邻相机姿态之间具有高重叠度，具有毫米级的足够细节，以及具有挑战性的视觉外观，例如反射和透明度。然而，现有的3D重建数据集缺乏这些条件的示例，使得对该任务的方法进行基准测试变得困难。我们提出了一个新的数据集，其中包含地面实况深度图、相机姿态和三个合成场景的网格模型，这些场景具有模拟的检查轨迹以及非朗伯表面的不同表面条件。我们在此数据集上评估了最先进的重建方法。我们的结果表明，当前的方法在该领域固有的密集捕获轨迹和复杂表面条件下表现不佳，暴露出一个关键的可扩展性差距，并指向资产检查中可部署的3D重建的新研究方向。项目页面：https://roboticimaging.org/Projects/asset-inspection-dataset/

TLDR: This paper introduces a new synthetic dataset for 3D reconstruction tailored to asset inspection, highlighting the limitations of current methods in handling the complex conditions of this domain. They provide ground truth depth maps, camera poses, and mesh models of synthetic scenes.

Authors: James L. Gray, Nikolai Goncharov, Alexandre Cardaillac, Ryan Griffiths, Jack Naylor, Donald G. Dansereau

Patient4D: Temporally Consistent Patient Body Mesh Recovery from Monocular Operating Room Video

Abstract (English): Recovering a dense 3D body mesh from monocular video remains challenging under occlusion from draping and continuously moving camera viewpoints. This configuration arises in surgical augmented reality (AR), where an anesthetized patient lies under surgical draping while a surgeon's head-mounted camera continuously changes viewpoint. Existing human mesh recovery (HMR) methods are typically trained on upright, moving subjects captured from relatively stable cameras, leading to performance degradation under such conditions. To address this, we present Patient4D, a stationarity-constrained reconstruction pipeline that explicitly exploits the stationarity prior. The pipeline combines image-level foundation models for perception with lightweight geometric mechanisms that enforce temporal consistency across frames. Two key components enable robust reconstruction: Pose Locking, which anchors pose parameters using stable keyframes, and Rigid Fallback, which recovers meshes under severe occlusion through silhouette-guided rigid alignment. Together, these mechanisms stabilize predictions while remaining compatible with off-the-shelf HMR models. We evaluate Patient4D on 4,680 synthetic surgical sequences and three public HMR video benchmarks. Under surgical drape occlusion, Patient4D achieves a 0.75 mean IoU, reducing failure frames from 30.5% to 1.3% compared to the best baseline. Our findings demonstrate that exploiting stationarity priors can substantially improve monocular reconstruction in clinical AR scenarios.

摘要（中文）: 从单目视频中恢复稠密的3D人体网格在遮挡、垂坠以及持续移动的相机视角下仍然面临挑战。这种配置常见于外科增强现实(AR)中，麻醉的病人躺在手术铺巾下，而外科医生的头戴式相机持续改变视角。 现有的人体网格恢复(HMR)方法通常在站立、运动的主体上进行训练，这些主体是从相对稳定的相机捕获的，导致在这种条件下性能下降。 为了解决这个问题，我们提出了Patient4D，一种显式利用静止性先验的、具有静止性约束的重建管线。该管线结合了用于感知的图像级基础模型和轻量级的几何机制，以强制执行跨帧的时间一致性。两个关键组件实现了鲁棒的重建：姿势锁定，利用稳定的关键帧来锚定姿势参数；刚性回退，通过轮廓引导的刚性对齐来恢复严重遮挡下的网格。 这些机制共同稳定了预测，同时保持与现成HMR模型的兼容性。 我们在4680个合成手术序列和三个公开的HMR视频基准上评估了Patient4D。 在手术铺巾遮挡下，Patient4D实现了0.75的平均IoU，与最佳基线相比，故障帧从30.5%降低到1.3%。 我们的研究结果表明，在临床AR场景中，利用静止性先验可以显著改善单目重建。

TLDR: Patient4D is a novel method for recovering temporally consistent 3D body meshes from monocular operating room videos, addressing challenges posed by surgical draping and camera movement through stationarity priors and lightweight geometric mechanisms.

简要说明: Patient4D 是一种新颖的方法，用于从单目手术室视频中恢复时间上一致的3D人体网格。它通过利用静止先验和轻量级几何机制来解决手术覆盖和相机运动带来的挑战。

Authors: Mingxiao Tu, Hoijoon Jung, Alireza Moghadam, Andre Kyme, Jinman Kim

GazeOnce360: Fisheye-Based 360° Multi-Person Gaze Estimation with Global-Local Feature Fusion

Abstract (English): We present GazeOnce360, a novel end-to-end model for multi-person gaze estimation from a single tabletop-mounted upward-facing fisheye camera. Unlike conventional approaches that rely on forward-facing cameras in constrained viewpoints, we address the underexplored setting of estimating the 3D gaze direction of multiple people distributed across a 360° scene from an upward fisheye perspective. To support research in this setting, we introduce MPSGaze360, a large-scale synthetic dataset rendered using Unreal Engine, featuring diverse multi-person configurations with accurate 3D gaze and eye landmark annotations. Our model tackles the severe distortion and perspective variation inherent in fisheye imagery by incorporating rotational convolutions and eye landmark supervision. To better capture fine-grained eye features crucial for gaze estimation, we propose a dual-resolution architecture that fuses global low-resolution context with high-resolution local eye regions. Experimental results demonstrate the effectiveness of each component in our model. This work highlights the feasibility and potential of fisheye-based 360° gaze estimation in practical multi-person scenarios. Project page: https://caizhuojiang.github.io/GazeOnce360/.

摘要（中文）: 我们提出了GazeOnce360，一种新颖的端到端模型，用于从单个安装在桌面上的向上鱼眼相机进行多人注视估计。与依赖于受限视点的前置相机的传统方法不同，我们解决了在向上鱼眼视角下，估计分布在360°场景中的多个人的3D注视方向这一尚未充分探索的设置。为了支持该设置下的研究，我们引入了MPSGaze360，一个大规模合成数据集，使用Unreal Engine渲染，具有各种多人配置以及精确的3D注视和眼睛地标标注。我们的模型通过结合旋转卷积和眼睛地标监督来解决鱼眼图像中固有的严重失真和透视变化问题。为了更好地捕捉对注视估计至关重要的细粒度眼睛特征，我们提出了一种双分辨率架构，将全局低分辨率上下文与高分辨率局部眼睛区域融合。实验结果表明了我们模型中每个组件的有效性。这项工作突出了基于鱼眼的360°注视估计在实际多人场景中的可行性和潜力。项目主页：https://caizhuojiang.github.io/GazeOnce360/。

TLDR: The paper introduces GazeOnce360, a novel end-to-end model for multi-person 3D gaze estimation using a single fisheye camera, along with a large-scale synthetic dataset. The model tackles fisheye distortion and utilizes global-local feature fusion for accurate gaze prediction.

Authors: Zhuojiang Cai, Zhenghui Sun, Feng Lu

SMAL-pets: SMAL Based Avatars of Pets from Single Image

Abstract (English): Creating high-fidelity, animatable 3D dog avatars remains a formidable challenge in computer vision. Unlike human digital doubles, animal reconstruction faces a critical shortage of large-scale, annotated datasets for specialized applications. Furthermore, the immense morphological diversity across species, breeds, and crosses, which varies significantly in size, proportions, and features, complicates the generalization of existing models. Current reconstruction methods often struggle to capture realistic fur textures. Additionally, ensuring these avatars are fully editable and capable of performing complex, naturalistic movements typically necessitates labor-intensive manual mesh manipulation and expert rigging. This paper introduces SMAL-pets, a comprehensive framework that generates high-quality, editable animal avatars from a single input image. Our approach bridges the gap between reconstruction and generative modeling by leveraging a hybrid architecture. Our method integrates 3D Gaussian Splatting with the SMAL parametric model to provide a representation that is both visually high-fidelity and anatomically grounded. We introduce a multimodal editing suite that enables users to refine the avatar's appearance and execute complex animations through direct textual prompts. By allowing users to control both the aesthetic and behavioral aspects of the model via natural language, SMAL-pets provides a flexible, robust tool for animation and virtual reality.

摘要（中文）: 创建高保真、可动画的3D犬类化身在计算机视觉领域仍然是一个巨大的挑战。与人类数字替身不同，动物重建面临着针对特定应用的大规模、带标注数据集的严重短缺。此外，物种、品种和杂交之间的巨大形态差异，在大小、比例和特征方面差异显著，使得现有模型的泛化变得复杂。目前的重建方法通常难以捕捉逼真的毛发纹理。此外，确保这些化身完全可编辑并能够执行复杂的、自然的运动，通常需要耗费大量人力的手动网格操作和专业绑定。本文介绍了一种名为SMAL-pets的综合框架，可以从单张输入图像生成高质量、可编辑的动物化身。我们的方法通过利用混合架构弥合了重建和生成建模之间的差距。我们的方法将3D高斯溅射与SMAL参数化模型相结合，提供了一种在视觉上高度保真且在解剖学上具有基础的表示。我们引入了一个多模态编辑套件，使用户能够通过直接的文本提示来细化化身的外观并执行复杂的动画。通过允许用户通过自然语言控制模型的审美和行为方面，SMAL-pets为动画和虚拟现实提供了一种灵活、强大的工具。

Authors: Piotr Borycki, Joanna Waczyńska, Yizhe Zhu, Yongqiang Gao, Przemysław Spurek

RHYME-XT: A Neural Operator for Spatiotemporal Control Systems

Abstract (English): We propose RHYME-XT, an operator-learning framework for surrogate modeling of spatiotemporal control systems governed by input-affine nonlinear partial integro-differential equations (PIDEs) with localized rhythmic behavior. RHYME-XT uses a Galerkin projection to approximate the infinite-dimensional PIDE on a learned finite-dimensional subspace with spatial basis functions parameterized by a neural network. This yields a projected system of ODEs driven by projected inputs. Instead of integrating this non-autonomous system, we directly learn its flow map using an architecture for learning flow functions, avoiding costly computations while obtaining a continuous-time and discretization-invariant representation. Experiments on a neural field PIDE show that RHYME-XT outperforms a state-of-the-art neural operator and is able to transfer knowledge effectively across models trained on different datasets, through a fine-tuning process.

摘要（中文）: 我们提出 RHYME-XT，一个算子学习框架，用于对受局部节律行为的输入仿射非线性偏积分微分方程 (PIDE) 控制的时空系统进行代理建模。RHYME-XT 使用 Galerkin 投影在一个学习到的有限维子空间上近似无限维 PIDE，其中的空间基函数由神经网络参数化。这产生了一个由投影输入驱动的常微分方程 (ODE) 投影系统。我们没有对这个非自治系统进行积分，而是直接使用一种用于学习流函数的架构学习它的流映射，从而避免了昂贵的计算，同时获得了连续时间和离散化不变的表示。在神经场 PIDE 上的实验表明，RHYME-XT 优于最先进的神经算子，并且能够通过微调过程，在不同数据集上训练的模型之间有效地传递知识。

TLDR: RHYME-XT is a neural operator framework for learning surrogate models of spatiotemporal control systems governed by complex PIDEs, outperforming existing methods and demonstrating transfer learning capabilities via fine-tuning.

简要说明: RHYME-XT 是一种神经算子框架，用于学习由复杂偏积分微分方程控制的时空控制系统的代理模型，其性能优于现有方法，并通过微调展示了迁移学习能力。

Authors: Marijn Ruiter, Miguel Aguiar, Jake Rap, Karl H. Johansson, Amritam Das

Symmetry-Reduced Physics-Informed Learning of Tensegrity Dynamics

Abstract (English): Tensegrity structures possess intrinsic geometric symmetries that govern their dynamic behavior. However, most existing physics-informed neural network (PINN) approaches for tensegrity dynamics do not explicitly exploit these symmetries, leading to high computational complexity and unstable optimization. In this work, we propose a symmetry-reduced physics-informed neural network (SymPINN) framework that embeds group-theory-based symmetry directly into both the solution expression and the neural network architecture to predict tensegrity dynamics. By decomposing nodes into symmetry orbits and representing free nodal coordinates using a symmetry basis, the proposed method constructs a reduced coordinate representation that preserves geometric symmetry of the structure. The full coordinates are then recovered via symmetry transformations of the reduced solution learned by the network, ensuring that the predicted configurations automatically satisfy the symmetry constraints. In this framework, equivariance is enforced through orbit-based coordinate generation, symmetry-consistent message passing, and physics residual constraints. In addition, SymPINN improves training effectiveness by encoding initial conditions as hard constraints, incorporating Fourier feature encoding to enhance the representation of dynamic motions, and employing a two-stage optimization strategy. Extensive numerical experiments on symmetric T-bars and lander structures demonstrate significantly improved prediction accuracy and computational efficiency compared to standard physics-informed models, indicating the great potential of symmetry-aware learning for structure-preserving modeling of tensegrity dynamics.

摘要（中文）: 张拉整体结构具有内在的几何对称性，这支配着它们的动力学行为。然而，现有的大多数基于物理信息神经网络（PINN）的张拉整体动力学方法并没有明确地利用这些对称性，导致计算复杂度高和优化不稳定。在这项工作中，我们提出了一种对称性简化的物理信息神经网络（SymPINN）框架，该框架直接将基于群论的对称性嵌入到解的表达和神经网络架构中，以预测张拉整体动力学。通过将节点分解为对称轨道，并使用对称基来表示自由节点坐标，所提出的方法构建了一个简化的坐标表示，从而保留了结构的几何对称性。然后，通过网络学习的简化解的对称变换来恢复完整的坐标，确保预测的配置自动满足对称约束。在该框架中，等变性通过基于轨道的坐标生成、对称一致的消息传递和物理残差约束来强制执行。此外，SymPINN通过将初始条件编码为硬约束，结合傅里叶特征编码来增强动态运动的表示，并采用两阶段优化策略，从而提高了训练效率。在对称T型杆和着陆器结构上的大量数值实验表明，与标准的物理信息模型相比，预测精度和计算效率都得到了显著提高，表明了对称性感知学习在张拉整体动力学结构保持建模方面的巨大潜力。

TLDR: The paper introduces a symmetry-reduced physics-informed neural network (SymPINN) for predicting tensegrity dynamics, improving accuracy and efficiency by incorporating structural symmetry constraints. It shows great potential for structure-preserving modeling.

Authors: Jing Qin, Muhao Chen

Personalized Fall Detection by Balancing Data with Selective Feedback Using Contrastive Learning

Abstract (English): Personalized fall detection models can significantly improve accuracy by adapting to individual motion patterns, yet their effectiveness is often limited by the scarcity of real-world fall data and the dominance of non-fall feedback samples. This imbalance biases the model toward routine activities and weakens its sensitivity to true fall events. To address this challenge, we propose a personalization framework that combines semi-supervised clustering with contrastive learning to identify and balance the most informative user feedback samples. The framework is evaluated under three retraining strategies, including Training from Scratch (TFS), Transfer Learning (TL), and Few-Shot Learning (FSL), to assess adaptability across learning paradigms. Real-time experiments with ten participants show that the TFS approach achieves the highest performance, with up to a 25% improvement over the baseline, while FSL achieves the second-highest performance with a 7% improvement, demonstrating the effectiveness of selective personalization for real-world deployment.

摘要（中文）: 个性化跌倒检测模型可以通过适应个体运动模式显著提高准确性，但其有效性通常受到真实跌倒数据稀缺以及非跌倒反馈样本占主导地位的限制。这种不平衡使模型偏向常规活动，并削弱其对真实跌倒事件的敏感性。为了应对这一挑战，我们提出了一种个性化框架，该框架结合了半监督聚类和对比学习，以识别和平衡信息量最大的用户反馈样本。该框架在三种重训练策略下进行评估，包括从头开始训练（TFS）、迁移学习（TL）和少样本学习（FSL），以评估其在不同学习范式中的适应性。对十名参与者进行的实时实验表明，TFS方法取得了最高的性能，比基线提高了高达25%，而FSL取得了第二高的性能，提高了7%，证明了选择性个性化在实际部署中的有效性。

TLDR: This paper presents a personalized fall detection framework using semi-supervised clustering and contrastive learning to address data imbalance issues, showing significant performance improvements in real-time experiments, especially with Training From Scratch and Few-Shot Learning strategies.

Authors: Awatif Yasmin, Tarek Mahmud, Sana Alamgeer, Anne H. H. Ngu

Contextual Preference Distribution Learning

Abstract (English): Decision-making problems often feature uncertainty stemming from heterogeneous and context-dependent human preferences. To address this, we propose a sequential learning-and-optimization pipeline to learn preference distributions and leverage them to solve downstream problems, for example risk-averse formulations. We focus on human choice settings that can be formulated as (integer) linear programs. In such settings, existing inverse optimization and choice modelling methods infer preferences from observed choices but typically produce point estimates or fail to capture contextual shifts, making them unsuitable for risk-averse decision-making. Using a bounded-variance score function gradient estimator, we train a predictive model mapping contextual features to a rich class of parameterizable distributions. This approach yields a maximum likelihood estimate. The model generates scenarios for unseen contexts in the subsequent optimization phase. In a synthetic ridesharing environment, our approach reduces average post-decision surprise by up to 114$\times$ compared to a risk-neutral approach with perfect predictions and up to 25$\times$ compared to leading risk-averse baselines.

摘要（中文）: 决策问题通常具有源于异构和上下文相关的人类偏好的不确定性。为了解决这个问题，我们提出了一种序贯学习与优化流程，以学习偏好分布并利用它们来解决下游问题，例如风险规避公式。我们专注于可以被公式化为（整数）线性规划的人类选择场景。在这种场景下，现有的逆优化和选择建模方法会从观察到的选择中推断偏好，但通常产生点估计或者无法捕捉上下文变化，因此不适用于风险规避决策。我们使用有界方差的分数函数梯度估计器，训练一个预测模型，将上下文特征映射到一类丰富的参数化分布。这种方法可以得到最大似然估计。该模型在后续优化阶段为未知的上下文生成情景。在一个合成的网约车环境中，与具有完美预测的风险中性方法相比，我们的方法将平均决策后意外度降低了高达114倍，与领先的风险规避基线方法相比，降低了高达25倍。

TLDR: This paper proposes a method for learning contextual preference distributions in decision-making problems, especially those involving human choices modeled as (integer) linear programs, and demonstrates its effectiveness in a ridesharing environment by reducing post-decision surprise.

简要说明: 本文提出了一种在决策问题中学习上下文偏好分布的方法，尤其是在涉及建模为（整数）线性规划的人类选择的问题中，并通过减少决策后的意外性，证明了其在拼车环境中的有效性。

Authors: Benjamin Hudson, Laurent Charlin, Emma Frejinger

Physics-informed Deep Mixture-of-Koopmans Vehicle Dynamics Model with Dual-branch Encoder for Distributed Electric-drive Trucks

Abstract (English): Advanced autonomous driving systems require accurate vehicle dynamics modeling. However, identifying a precise dynamics model remains challenging due to strong nonlinearities and the coupled longitudinal and lateral dynamic characteristics. Previous research has employed physics-based analytical models or neural networks to construct vehicle dynamics representations. Nevertheless, these approaches often struggle to simultaneously achieve satisfactory performance in terms of system identification efficiency, modeling accuracy, and compatibility with linear control strategies. In this paper, we propose a fully data-driven dynamics modeling method tailored for complex distributed electric-drive trucks (DETs), leveraging Koopman operator theory to represent highly nonlinear dynamics in a lifted linear embedding space. To achieve high-precision modeling, we first propose a novel dual-branch encoder which encodes dynamic states and provides a powerful basis for the proposed Koopman-based methods entitled KODE. A physics-informed supervision mechanism, grounded in the geometric consistency of temporal vehicle motion, is incorporated into the training process to facilitate effective learning of both the encoder and the Koopman operator. Furthermore, to accommodate the diverse driving patterns of DETs, we extend the vanilla Koopman operator to a mixture-of-Koopman operator framework, enhancing modeling capability. Simulations conducted in a high-fidelity TruckSim environment and real-world experiments demonstrate that the proposed approach achieves state-of-the-art performance in long-term dynamics state estimation.

摘要（中文）: 高级自动驾驶系统需要精确的车辆动力学建模。然而，由于强非线性和纵向与横向动力学特征的耦合，识别精确的动力学模型仍然具有挑战性。先前的研究已采用基于物理的解析模型或神经网络来构建车辆动力学表示。然而，这些方法通常难以在系统辨识效率、建模精度以及与线性控制策略的兼容性方面同时取得令人满意的性能。本文提出了一种完全数据驱动的动力学建模方法，专门为复杂的分布式电驱动卡车（DETs）定制，利用Koopman算子理论在高维的线性嵌入空间中表示高度非线性的动力学。为了实现高精度建模，我们首先提出一种新颖的双分支编码器，其编码动态状态，并为提出的基于Koopman算子的方法（名为KODE）提供强大的基础。一种基于时间车辆运动几何一致性的、基于物理信息的监督机制被纳入训练过程，以促进编码器和Koopman算子的有效学习。此外，为了适应DETs的多样化驾驶模式，我们将原始Koopman算子扩展到混合Koopman算子框架，从而增强建模能力。在高保真TruckSim环境中的仿真和真实世界的实验表明，所提出的方法在长期动力学状态估计方面取得了最先进的性能。

TLDR: This paper introduces a physics-informed deep mixture-of-Koopmans model for vehicle dynamics modeling in distributed electric-drive trucks, aiming for improved accuracy and compatibility with linear control. They use a dual-branch encoder and physics-informed supervision.

简要说明: 本文提出了一种基于物理信息的 Koopman 混合模型，用于分布式电驱动卡车的车辆动力学建模，旨在提高精度并与线性控制兼容。他们使用了双分支编码器和基于物理信息的监督。

Authors: Jinyu Miao, Pu Zhang, Rujun Yan, Yifei He, Bowei Zhang, Zheng Fu, Ke Wang, Qi Song, Kun Jiang, Mengmeng Yang, Diange Yang

FastLoop: Parallel Loop Closing with GPU-Acceleration in Visual SLAM

Abstract (English): Visual SLAM systems combine visual tracking with global loop closure to maintain a consistent map and accurate localization. Loop closure is a computationally expensive process as we need to search across the whole map for matches. This paper presents FastLoop, a GPU-accelerated loop closing module to alleviate this computational complexity. We identify key performance bottlenecks in the loop closing pipeline of visual SLAM and address them through parallel optimizations on the GPU. Specifically, we use task-level and data-level parallelism and integrate a GPU-accelerated pose graph optimization. Our implementation is built on top of ORB-SLAM3 and leverages CUDA for GPU programming. Experimental results show that FastLoop achieves an average speedup of 1.4x and 1.3x on the EuRoC dataset and 3.0x and 2.4x on the TUM-VI dataset for the loop closing module on desktop and embedded platforms, respectively, while maintaining the accuracy of the original system.

摘要（中文）: 视觉SLAM系统结合了视觉跟踪与全局回环检测，以维持一致的地图和精确的定位。回环检测是一个计算密集型的过程，因为我们需要在整个地图中搜索匹配项。本文提出了一种GPU加速的回环闭合模块FastLoop，以减轻这种计算复杂度。我们识别了视觉SLAM回环闭合流程中的关键性能瓶颈，并通过GPU上的并行优化来解决这些问题。具体而言，我们使用任务级和数据级并行性，并集成了一个GPU加速的姿态图优化。我们的实现基于ORB-SLAM3之上，并利用CUDA进行GPU编程。实验结果表明，在桌面和嵌入式平台上，FastLoop分别在EuRoC数据集上实现了1.4倍和1.3倍的平均加速，在TUM-VI数据集上实现了3.0倍和2.4倍的平均加速，同时保持了原始系统的精度。

TLDR: The paper presents FastLoop, a GPU-accelerated loop closing module for visual SLAM that improves computational efficiency by 1.3-3.0x on EuRoC and TUM-VI datasets while maintaining accuracy.

简要说明: 该论文提出了FastLoop，一个用于视觉SLAM的GPU加速的回环闭合模块，在EuRoC和TUM-VI数据集上，在保持精度的同时，计算效率提高了1.3-3.0倍。

Authors: Soudabeh Mohammadhashemi, Shishir Gopinath, Kimia Khabiri, Parsa Hosseininejad, Karthik Dantu, Steven Y. Ko

ReLMXEL: Adaptive RL-Based Memory Controller with Explainable Energy and Latency Optimization

Abstract (English): Reducing latency and energy consumption is critical to improving the efficiency of memory systems in modern computing. This work introduces ReLMXEL (Reinforcement Learning for Memory Controller with Explainable Energy and Latency Optimization), a explainable multi-agent online reinforcement learning framework that dynamically optimizes memory controller parameters using reward decomposition. ReLMXEL operates within the memory controller, leveraging detailed memory behavior metrics to guide decision-making. Experimental evaluations across diverse workloads demonstrate consistent performance gains over baseline configurations, with refinements driven by workload-specific memory access behaviour. By incorporating explainability into the learning process, ReLMXEL not only enhances performance but also increases the transparency of control decisions, paving the way for more accountable and adaptive memory system designs.

摘要（中文）: 降低延迟和功耗对于提高现代计算中存储器系统的效率至关重要。本文介绍了一种可解释的多智能体在线强化学习框架ReLMXEL（基于强化学习的可解释能耗与延迟优化存储器控制器），该框架利用奖励分解动态地优化存储器控制器参数。ReLMXEL在存储器控制器内部运行，利用详细的存储器行为指标来指导决策。针对不同工作负载的实验评估表明，与基线配置相比，ReLMXEL实现了持续的性能提升，并且改进是由工作负载特定的存储器访问行为驱动的。通过将可解释性融入学习过程，ReLMXEL不仅提高了性能，还提高了控制决策的透明度，为更负责任和自适应的存储器系统设计铺平了道路。

TLDR: ReLMXEL is a multi-agent reinforcement learning framework that dynamically optimizes memory controller parameters for energy and latency reduction, with explainability incorporated to increase transparency.

Authors: Panuganti Chirag Sai, Gandholi Sarat, R. Raghunatha Sarma, Venkata Kalyan Tavva, Naveen M

AdaRadar: Rate Adaptive Spectral Compression for Radar-based Perception

Abstract (English): Radar is a critical perception modality in autonomous driving systems due to its all-weather characteristics and ability to measure range and Doppler velocity. However, the sheer volume of high-dimensional raw radar data saturates the communication link to the computing engine (e.g., an NPU), which is often a low-bandwidth interface with data rate provisioned only for a few low-resolution range-Doppler frames. A generalized codec for utilizing high-dimensional radar data is notably absent, while existing image-domain approaches are unsuitable, as they typically operate at fixed compression ratios and fail to adapt to varying or adversarial conditions. In light of this, we propose radar data compression with adaptive feedback. It dynamically adjusts the compression ratio by performing gradient descent from the proxy gradient of detection confidence with respect to the compression rate. We employ a zeroth-order gradient approximation as it enables gradient computation even with non-differentiable core operations--pruning and quantization. This also avoids transmitting the gradient tensors over the band-limited link, which, if estimated, would be as large as the original radar data. In addition, we have found that radar feature maps are heavily concentrated on a few frequency components. Thus, we apply the discrete cosine transform to the radar data cubes and selectively prune out the coefficients effectively. We preserve the dynamic range of each radar patch through scaled quantization. Combining those techniques, our proposed online adaptive compression scheme achieves over 100x feature size reduction at minimal performance drop (~1%p). We validate our results on the RADIal, CARRADA, and Radatron datasets.

摘要（中文）: 雷达是自动驾驶系统中至关重要的传感模态，这归功于其全天候特性以及测量距离和多普勒速度的能力。然而，大量高维原始雷达数据会使通往计算引擎（例如NPU）的通信链路饱和，而该链路通常是低带宽接口，其数据速率仅为几个低分辨率距离-多普勒帧提供。目前普遍缺乏用于利用高维雷达数据的通用编解码器，而现有的图像域方法并不适用，因为它们通常以固定的压缩比率运行，并且无法适应变化或对抗性条件。鉴于此，我们提出了一种具有自适应反馈的雷达数据压缩方法。它通过执行检测置信度代理梯度相对于压缩率的梯度下降来动态调整压缩比。我们采用零阶梯度近似，因为它即使在存在不可微的核心操作（剪枝和量化）的情况下也能进行梯度计算。这也避免了通过带宽受限链路传输梯度张量，因为如果估计它们，它们将与原始雷达数据一样大。此外，我们发现雷达特征图集中在少数几个频率分量上。因此，我们将离散余弦变换应用于雷达数据立方体，并有选择地有效地剪除系数。我们通过缩放量化来保留每个雷达补丁的动态范围。结合这些技术，我们提出的在线自适应压缩方案实现了超过100倍的特征尺寸缩减，同时性能损失极小（约1%p）。我们在RADIal、CARRADA和Radatron数据集上验证了我们的结果。

TLDR: The paper introduces AdaRadar, an adaptive radar data compression scheme that uses a proxy gradient descent approach to dynamically adjust the compression ratio, achieving significant data reduction with minimal performance loss. It improves over existing methods by adapting to varying conditions and is validated on multiple radar datasets.

简要说明: 该论文提出了一种名为AdaRadar的自适应雷达数据压缩方案，该方案使用代理梯度下降方法动态调整压缩率，以最小的性能损失实现显著的数据缩减。它通过适应不同的条件改进了现有方法，并在多个雷达数据集上进行了验证。
