Authors: Jinho Park, Se Young Chun, Mingoo Seok

Edge-Efficient Two-Stream Multimodal Architecture for Non-Intrusive Bathroom Fall Detection

Abstract (English): Falls in wet bathroom environments are a major safety risk for seniors living alone. Recent work has shown that mmWave-only, vibration-only, and existing multimodal schemes, such as vibration-triggered radar activation, early feature concatenation, and decision-level score fusion, can support privacy-preserving, non-intrusive fall detection. However, these designs still treat motion and impact as loosely coupled streams, depending on coarse temporal alignment and amplitude thresholds, and do not explicitly encode the causal link between radar-observed collapse and floor impact or address timing drift, object drop confounders, and latency and energy constraints on low-power edge devices. To this end, we propose a two-stream architecture that encodes radar signals with a Motion--Mamba branch for long-range motion patterns and processes floor vibration with an Impact--Griffin branch that emphasizes impact transients and cross-axis coupling. Cross-conditioned fusion uses low-rank bilinear interaction and a Switch--MoE head to align motion and impact tokens and suppress object-drop confounders. The model keeps inference cost suitable for real-time execution on a Raspberry Pi 4B gateway. We construct a bathroom fall detection benchmark dataset with frame-level annotations, comprising more than 3~h of synchronized mmWave radar and triaxial vibration recordings across eight scenarios under running water, together with subject-independent training, validation, and test splits. On the test split, our model attains 96.1% accuracy, 94.8% precision, 88.0% recall, a 91.1% macro F1 score, and an AUC of 0.968. Compared with the strongest baseline, it improves accuracy by 2.0 percentage points and fall recall by 1.3 percentage points, while reducing latency from 35.9 ms to 15.8 ms and lowering energy per 2.56 s window from 14200 mJ to 10750 mJ on the Raspberry Pi 4B gateway.

摘要（中文）: 独自居住的老年人在潮湿浴室环境中跌倒是一个重要的安全风险。最近的研究表明，仅使用毫米波、仅使用振动以及现有的多模态方案，如振动触发的雷达激活、早期特征拼接和决策层分数融合，可以支持保护隐私、非侵入式的跌倒检测。然而，这些设计仍然将运动和冲击视为松散耦合的流，依赖于粗略的时间对齐和幅度阈值，并且没有明确地编码雷达观察到的倒地和地板冲击之间的因果关系，也没有解决时间漂移、物体掉落混淆因素以及低功耗边缘设备的延迟和能量约束。为此，我们提出了一种双流架构，该架构使用Motion-Mamba分支编码雷达信号以捕获长程运动模式，并使用Impact-Griffin分支处理地板振动，该分支强调冲击瞬态和跨轴耦合。交叉条件融合使用低秩双线性交互和一个Switch-MoE头来对齐运动和冲击令牌，并抑制物体掉落混淆因素。该模型保持了适用于在Raspberry Pi 4B网关上实时执行的推理成本。我们构建了一个带有帧级别注释的浴室跌倒检测基准数据集，其中包含在自来水下八种场景下的超过3小时的同步毫米波雷达和三轴振动记录，以及主题独立的训练、验证和测试分割。在测试分割上，我们的模型达到了96.1%的准确率、94.8%的精确率、88.0%的召回率、91.1%的宏F1分数和0.968的AUC。与最强的基线相比，它将准确率提高了2.0个百分点，跌倒召回率提高了1.3个百分点，同时将Raspberry Pi 4B网关上的延迟从35.9毫秒降低到15.8毫秒，并将每2.56秒窗口的能量从14200 mJ降低到10750 mJ。

TLDR: This paper presents a two-stream multimodal architecture leveraging mmWave radar and triaxial vibration for non-intrusive bathroom fall detection, achieving improved accuracy, reduced latency, and lower energy consumption on a Raspberry Pi 4B compared to existing methods.

简要说明: 本文提出了一种双流多模态架构，利用毫米波雷达和三轴振动进行非侵入式浴室跌倒检测。与现有方法相比，该架构在 Raspberry Pi 4B 上实现了更高的准确率、更低的延迟和更低的能耗。

Authors: Haitian Wang, Yiren Wang, Xinyu Wang, Sheldon Fung, Atif Mansoor

A Single-Fiber Optical Frequency Domain Reflectometry (OFDR)-Based Shape Sensing of Concentric Tube Steerable Drilling Robots

Abstract (English): This paper introduces a novel shape-sensing approach for Concentric Tube Steerable Drilling Robots (CT-SDRs) based on Optical Frequency Domain Reflectometry (OFDR). Unlike traditional FBG-based methods, OFDR enables continuous strain measurement along the entire fiber length with enhanced spatial resolution. In the proposed method, a Shape Sensing Assembly (SSA) is first fabricated by integrating a single OFDR fiber with a flat NiTi wire. The calibrated SSA is then routed through and housed within the internal channel of a flexible drilling instrument, which is guided by the pre-shaped NiTi tube of the CT-SDR. In this configuration, the drilling instrument serves as a protective sheath for the SSA during drilling, eliminating the need for integration or adhesion to the instrument surface that is typical of conventional optical sensor approaches. The performance of the proposed SSA, integrated within the cannulated CT-SDR, was thoroughly evaluated under free-bending conditions and during drilling along multiple J-shaped trajectories in synthetic Sawbones phantoms. Results demonstrate accurate and reliable shape-sensing capability, confirming the feasibility and robustness of this integration strategy.

摘要（中文）: 本文介绍了一种基于光频域反射技术(OFDR)的新型同心管可导向钻孔机器人(CT-SDRs)的形状感知方法。与传统的基于光纤布拉格光栅(FBG)的方法不同，OFDR能够以更高的空间分辨率沿整个光纤长度进行连续应变测量。 在所提出的方法中，首先通过将单根OFDR光纤与扁平的NiTi线集成来制造形状感知组件(SSA)。然后，将校准后的SSA穿过并安置在柔性钻孔仪器的内部通道中，该仪器由CT-SDR的预成型NiTi管引导。在这种配置中，钻孔仪器充当钻孔过程中SSA的保护套，无需像传统光学传感器方法那样集成或粘附到仪器表面。对集成在带内腔的CT-SDR内的所提出的SSA的性能，在自由弯曲条件下以及在合成Sawbones模型中沿多个J形轨迹钻孔期间进行了全面评估。结果表明，其具有准确且可靠的形状感知能力，证实了这种集成策略的可行性和鲁棒性。

TLDR: This paper presents a shape-sensing method for Concentric Tube Steerable Drilling Robots (CT-SDRs) using Optical Frequency Domain Reflectometry (OFDR), achieving continuous strain measurement and accurate shape reconstruction during drilling.

简要说明: 本文提出了一种基于光频域反射 (OFDR) 的同心管可操纵钻孔机器人 (CT-SDR) 的形状感知方法，可在钻孔过程中实现连续应变测量和精确的形状重构。
